module CICADA71 where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; _+_; _*_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Data.Nat.Base         using (_%_; NonZero; nonZero)
open import Data.Nat.DivMod       using ([m+kn]%n‚Č°m%n)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Bucket index in {0..70}
bucket71 : Nat ‚Üí Nat
bucket71 n = n % 71

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Periodicity statement: bucket71 (n + k*71) = bucket71 n
-- (prove via stdlib DivMod lemmas later, or keep as a postulate hook)

instance
  nonZero71 : NonZero 71
  nonZero71 = nonZero

bucket71-period : ‚ąÄ n k ‚Üí bucket71 (n + k * 71) ‚Č° bucket71 n
bucket71-period n k = [m+kn]%n‚Č°m%n n k 71
module UFTC_Lattice where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality as Eq using (sym; trans; cong)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (‚Č§-refl; ‚Č§-trans; ‚Č§-antisym;
  ‚äĒ-idem; ‚äĒ-comm; ‚äĒ-assoc; ‚äĒ-mono-‚Č§; ‚äĒ-monoň°-‚Č§; ‚äĒ-mono ≥-‚Č§)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚Č§_; _‚äĒ_)
open import Data.Sum using (_‚äé_; inj‚āĀ; inj‚āā)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Severity levels (0..9). (You can restrict further if you want Fin 10.)

Severity : Set
Severity = Nat

_‚äĎ_ : Severity ‚Üí Severity ‚Üí Set
_‚äĎ_ = _‚Č§_

-- Join = max severity wins.
_‚äĒs_ : Severity ‚Üí Severity ‚Üí Severity
_‚äĒs_ = _‚äĒ_

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Join-semilattice laws (assoc/comm/idempotent).

‚äĒs-idem : ‚ąÄ a ‚Üí a ‚äĒs a ‚Č° a
‚äĒs-idem a = NatP.‚äĒ-idem a

‚äĒs-comm : ‚ąÄ a b ‚Üí a ‚äĒs b ‚Č° b ‚äĒs a
‚äĒs-comm a b = NatP.‚äĒ-comm a b

‚äĒs-assoc : ‚ąÄ a b c ‚Üí (a ‚äĒs b) ‚äĒs c ‚Č° a ‚äĒs (b ‚äĒs c)
‚äĒs-assoc a b c = NatP.‚äĒ-assoc a b c

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Monotonicity of join (the key ‚Äúmax severity wins cannot be masked‚ÄĚ).

‚äĒs-monoň° : ‚ąÄ {a a' b} ‚Üí a ‚äĎ a' ‚Üí (a ‚äĒs b) ‚äĎ (a' ‚äĒs b)
‚äĒs-monoň° {a} {a'} {b} a‚Č§a' =
  NatP.‚äĒ-monoň°-‚Č§ b a‚Č§a'

‚äĒs-mono ≥ : ‚ąÄ {a b b'} ‚Üí b ‚äĎ b' ‚Üí (a ‚äĒs b) ‚äĎ (a ‚äĒs b')
‚äĒs-mono ≥ {a} {b} {b'} b‚Č§b' =
  NatP.‚äĒ-mono ≥-‚Č§ a b‚Č§b'

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A minimal ‚Äúcode‚ÄĚ model: normal trit + special codes with severity.
-- (Map VOID/PARA/META etc. into severity levels.)

data Code : Set where
  normal : Nat ‚Üí Code               -- placeholder for trits
  special : Severity ‚Üí Code          -- special failure code with severity

severity : Code ‚Üí Severity
severity (normal _)    = 0
severity (special sev) = sev

-- Propagation rule: combine codes by max severity.
C_XOR : Code ‚Üí Code ‚Üí Code
C_XOR x y = special (severity x ‚äĒs severity y)

C_ROT : Code ‚Üí Code
C_ROT x = x  -- rotation doesn't reduce severity (your fast path can refine)

-- Monotone wrt severity preorder:
Monotone‚āā : (Code ‚Üí Code ‚Üí Code) ‚Üí Set
Monotone‚āā f =
  ‚ąÄ x x' y y' ‚Üí
    severity x ‚äĎ severity x' ‚Üí
    severity y ‚äĎ severity y' ‚Üí
    severity (f x y) ‚äĎ severity (f x' y')

C_XOR-monotone : Monotone‚āā C_XOR
C_XOR-monotone x x' y y' sx sy =
  NatP.‚äĒ-mono-‚Č§ sx sy

-- Rotation monotonicity (trivial in this stub; replace with your real ROT):
C_ROT-monotone :
  ‚ąÄ x x' ‚Üí severity x ‚äĎ severity x' ‚Üí severity (C_ROT x) ‚äĎ severity (C_ROT x')
C_ROT-monotone x x' sx = sx

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Cone interior monotonicity (structured seam).
-- Matches empirical: preserved in the interior, boundary cases allowed.

record ConeInterior {X : Set} : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    InInterior : X ‚Üí Set
    Boundary   : X ‚Üí Set

open ConeInterior public

record ConeInteriorPreserved {X : Set} (T : X ‚Üí X) (C : ConeInterior {X}) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    preserve :
      ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí
      InInterior C x ‚Üí
      InInterior C (T x) ‚äé Boundary C (T x)

open ConeInteriorPreserved public

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Search space abstraction

record ModelFamily (D : Dataset) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    candidate : Nat ‚Üí PrimeModel D

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Minimality condition

isMinimal :
  ‚ąÄ {D}
  (F : ModelFamily D)
  (k : Nat)
  ‚Üí
  (‚ąÄ n ‚Üí primeTotal (ModelFamily.candidate F k)
          ‚Č§ primeTotal (ModelFamily.candidate F n))
  ‚Üí
  Set

isMinimal F k proof = ‚ä§
module MDL where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool
open import Agda.Builtin.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)
open import Data.Empty using (‚ä•)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚Č§_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Basic length type

CodeLength : Set
CodeLength = Nat

-- Use the standard Nat order.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Dataset abstraction

record Dataset : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    Data : Set
    sample : Data

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Model abstraction (two-part code)

record Model (D : Dataset) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    Param      : Set
    param      : Param

    encodeM    : Param ‚Üí CodeLength
    encodeData : Param ‚Üí Dataset.Data D ‚Üí CodeLength

modelTotalLength :
  ‚ąÄ {D} ‚Üí
  Model D ‚Üí
  CodeLength
modelTotalLength {D} M =
  Model.encodeM M (Model.param M) + Model.encodeData M (Model.param M) (Dataset.sample D)


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- MDL comparison

better :
  ‚ąÄ {D} ‚Üí
  Model D ‚Üí
  Model D ‚Üí
  Set

better {D} M‚āĀ M‚āā =
  modelTotalLength M‚āĀ ‚Č§ modelTotalLength M‚āā

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Subset selection cost (critical for honesty)

-- Suppose models are parameterized by a subset of primes
-- We must charge for describing that subset.

Subset : Nat ‚Üí Set
Subset n = Nat  -- abstract: encoded subset id

subsetCost :
  ‚ąÄ (n : Nat) ‚Üí
  Subset n ‚Üí
  CodeLength
subsetCost n _ = n  -- naive upper bound: cost grows with space size

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Bounded model class (limit to 71)

record BoundedModel (D : Dataset) (limit : Nat) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    inner : Model D
    boundProof :
      modelTotalLength inner ‚Č§ limit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The "limit to 71" specialization

limit71 : Nat
limit71 = 71

record Model71 (D : Dataset) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    base : Model D
    bounded : modelTotalLength base ‚Č§ limit71

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Theorem: restricting model space does not reduce price unfairly

restrictSafe :
  ‚ąÄ {D}
  (M : Model D)
  (p : modelTotalLength M ‚Č§ limit71) ‚Üí
  modelTotalLength M ‚Č§ limit71

restrictSafe M p = p

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lyapunov structure (order-theoretic MDL)

record Lyapunov {S : Set} (T : S ‚Üí S) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    L : S ‚Üí CodeLength
    descent : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí L (T s) ‚Č§ L s

open Lyapunov public
module GodelLattice where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_; _*_)
open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List; []; _‚ą∑_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A factor-exponent vector over the 15 primes is a canonical coordinate.

record Vec15 (A : Set) : Set where
  constructor v15
  field
    e2  : A; e3  : A; e5  : A; e7  : A; e11 : A
    e13 : A; e17 : A; e19 : A; e23 : A; e29 : A
    e31 : A; e41 : A; e47 : A; e59 : A; e71 : A

Exponent : Set
Exponent = Nat

FactorVec : Set
FactorVec = Vec15 Exponent

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract "text" (you‚Äôll plug a real representation later)

postulate
  Text : Set

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- G√∂del encoding contract:
-- encode gives a Nat; factorMap gives exponents over SSP primes.
-- The key property is that factorMap is a homomorphism for concatenation
-- (or some composition), if you want that. Here we keep it minimal.

postulate
  encode   : Text ‚Üí Nat
  factorMap : Text ‚Üí FactorVec

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Self-verifying coordinate means: equality of factor-vectors is a stable
-- identifier under the chosen equivalence (you decide what that is).
-- We DO NOT claim it is ‚Äúreality‚ÄĚ; we claim it is a canonical coordinate.

record CoordinateLaw : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    stable-id :
      ‚ąÄ (t‚āĀ t‚āā : Text) ‚Üí
      factorMap t‚āĀ ‚Č° factorMap t‚āā ‚Üí encode t‚āĀ ‚Č° encode t‚āā
module MonsterProjection where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Data.Nat using (_<_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym; trans)
open import Relation.Nullary

open import Ultrametric
open import MonsterMask
open import MonsterUltrametric

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Distinctness

_‚ČĘ_ : Mask ‚Üí Mask ‚Üí Set
x ‚ČĘ y = ¬¨ (x ‚Č° y)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Contractive on distinct points

record Contractive‚ČĘ (K : Mask ‚Üí Mask) : Set where
  open Ultrametric.Ultrametric UMask
  field
    contraction‚ČĘ : ‚ąÄ {x y} ‚Üí x ‚ČĘ y ‚Üí d (K x) (K y) < d x y

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Projection to fixed mask is strictly contractive

postulate
  projContractive : ‚ąÄ target ‚Üí Contractive‚ČĘ (Kernel.K (projectTo target))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Fixed point definition

Fixed : (Mask ‚Üí Mask) ‚Üí Mask ‚Üí Set
Fixed K m = K m ‚Č° m

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Unique fixed point for projection

uniqueFixedProj :
  ‚ąÄ target x y ‚Üí
  Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) x ‚Üí
  Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) y ‚Üí
  x ‚Č° y
uniqueFixedProj target x y fx fy = trans (sym fx) fy
module KernelAlgebra where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Base ternary carrier

data T : Set where
  neg  : T
  zero : T
  pos  : T

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- State space as indexed function

State : Set ‚Üí Set
State X = X ‚Üí T

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Involution

őĻ : ‚ąÄ {X} ‚Üí State X ‚Üí State X
őĻ s x with s x
... | neg  = pos
... | pos  = neg
... | zero = zero

őĻ¬≤-id : ‚ąÄ {X} (s : State X) (x : X) ‚Üí őĻ (őĻ s) x ‚Č° s x
őĻ¬≤-id s x with s x
... | neg  = refl
... | pos  = refl
... | zero = refl


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Kernel operator interface

record Kernel {X : Set} : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    K : State X ‚Üí State X

    involutive-respecting :
      ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí K (őĻ s) ‚Č° őĻ (K s)

open Kernel public

-- Interface-level comparison hook to quantum: unitary evolution should be invertible,
-- so it cannot satisfy the projection-only + strict contraction hypotheses simultaneously.
-- We keep this as a spec-level test (type only).

postulate
  QState : Set
  UQ : QState ‚Üí QState

unitary-is-invertible : Set
unitary-is-invertible = ő£ (QState ‚Üí QState) (őĽ inv ‚Üí (‚ąÄ x ‚Üí inv (UQ x) ‚Č° x) √ó (‚ąÄ x ‚Üí UQ (inv x) ‚Č° x))
  where
    infixr 4 _√ó_
    record _√ó_ (A B : Set) : Set where
      constructor _,_
      field fst : A
            snd : B

module AntiFascistSystem where

open import Level
open import Data.Nat

postulate
  S : Set
  H : S ‚Üí ‚Ąē

-- Invertible operator

record Invertible : Set where
  field
    U    : S ‚Üí S
    U‚ĀĽ¬Ļ  : S ‚Üí S
    left  : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí U‚ĀĽ¬Ļ (U s) ‚Č° s
    right : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí U (U‚ĀĽ¬Ļ s) ‚Č° s

-- Entropy preserved under unitary-like operator

postulate
  entropy-preserved :
    ‚ąÄ (u : Invertible) s ‚Üí H (Invertible.U u s) ‚Č° H s

-- No monotone collapse

postulate
  non-collapse :
    ‚ąÄ (u : Invertible) ‚Üí ¬¨ (‚ąÄ s ‚Üí H (Invertible.U u s) ‚Č§ H s)
module Stabilisation where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import KernelAlgebra

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Iteration

iterate : ‚ąÄ {X} ‚Üí
          (State X ‚Üí State X) ‚Üí
          Nat ‚Üí
          State X ‚Üí
          State X
iterate K zero    s = s
iterate K (suc n) s = iterate K n (K s)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- No nontrivial 2-cycle

No2Cycle : ‚ąÄ {X} (K : State X ‚Üí State X) ‚Üí Set
No2Cycle K =
  ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí iterate K 2 s ‚Č° s ‚Üí K s ‚Č° s
module MonsterStep where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List; []; _‚ą∑_)

open import MonsterState

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- First admissible candidate (deterministic tie-break: leftmost wins).

choose : (L : Lens) ‚Üí (s : State) ‚Üí Candidates ‚Üí Mask ‚Üí Mask
choose L s []           fallback = fallback
choose L s (m ‚ą∑ ms)     fallback with Lens.admissible L s m
... | true  = m
... | false = choose L s ms fallback

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Step:
-- - pick next mask via lens
-- - advance window (or keep it; you decide)
-- This pins MW-00 (well-defined deterministic function).

step : (L : Lens) ‚Üí Candidates ‚Üí State ‚Üí State
step L cands s =
  let nextMask = choose L s cands (State.mask s)
  in  st nextMask (suc (State.window s))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Iteration (total, structurally terminating on Nat).

iterate : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí (A ‚Üí A) ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí A ‚Üí A
iterate f zero    x = x
iterate f (suc n) x = iterate f n (f x)
module Contraction where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Data.Empty using (‚ä•)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Contraction property (strict)

_‚ČĘ_ : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí A ‚Üí A ‚Üí Set
x ‚ČĘ y = x ‚Č° y ‚Üí ‚ä•

record Contractive
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (K : S ‚Üí S)
       : Set where

  open UMetric.Ultrametric U

  field
    contraction :
      ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí
      d (K x) (K y) < d x y

-- Contractive on distinct points (avoids x=x degenerate case).
record Contractive‚ČĘ
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (K : S ‚Üí S)
       : Set where

  open UMetric.Ultrametric U

  field
    contraction‚ČĘ :
      ‚ąÄ {x y} ‚Üí x ‚ČĘ y ‚Üí
      d (K x) (K y) < d x y

-- Strict contraction plus a specified unique fixed point.
record StrictContraction
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (K : S ‚Üí S)
       : Set where

  field
    contractive‚ČĘ : Contractive‚ČĘ U K
    fp : S
    fixed : K fp ‚Č° fp
    unique : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí K x ‚Č° x ‚Üí x ‚Č° fp
module MonsterMask where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.List

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- We model the 15 prime-power factors of |M| as positions 0..14.

FactorCount : Nat
FactorCount = 15

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A mask is a length-15 boolean list:
-- true  = keep factor
-- false = remove factor

Mask : Set
Mask = List Bool

replicate : Nat ‚Üí Bool ‚Üí Mask
replicate zero    b = []
replicate (suc n) b = b ‚ą∑ replicate n b

boolAnd : Bool ‚Üí Bool ‚Üí Bool
boolAnd true true = true
boolAnd _    _    = false

notBool : Bool ‚Üí Bool
notBool true  = false
notBool false = true

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Canonical full mask (all factors kept)

fullMask : Mask
fullMask = replicate FactorCount true

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Collapse mask: remove everything

emptyMask : Mask
emptyMask = replicate FactorCount false

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Pointwise AND (factor removal composition)

_‚ąß_ : Mask ‚Üí Mask ‚Üí Mask
[] ‚ąß [] = []
(b ‚ą∑ xs) ‚ąß (c ‚ą∑ ys) = boolAnd b c ‚ą∑ (xs ‚ąß ys)
_ ‚ąß _ = []

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Kernel-style operator: remove a fixed subset F

record Kernel : Set where
  field
    K : Mask ‚Üí Mask

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Example: projection to a fixed group representative mask

projectTo : Mask ‚Üí Kernel
projectTo target = record
  { K = őĽ _ ‚Üí target
  }

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Involution: flip keep/remove

flipMask : Mask ‚Üí Mask
flipMask [] = []
flipMask (b ‚ą∑ xs) = notBool b ‚ą∑ flipMask xs
module CounterexampleHarness where

open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Generic falsifier

record Counterexample {A : Set}
                      (P : A ‚Üí Set)
                      : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    witness : A
    violates : ¬¨ P witness
module MonsterOntos where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong)
open import Relation.Nullary.Decidable.Core using (Dec; yes; no)
open import Data.Nat.Properties renaming (_‚Čü_ to nat‚Čü)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Ontos: the 15 supersingular primes used as the base carrier.

data SSP : Set where
  p2  : SSP
  p3  : SSP
  p5  : SSP
  p7  : SSP
  p11 : SSP
  p13 : SSP
  p17 : SSP
  p19 : SSP
  p23 : SSP
  p29 : SSP
  p31 : SSP
  p41 : SSP
  p47 : SSP
  p59 : SSP
  p71 : SSP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete embedding to Nat (for mod/sharding etc).

toNat : SSP ‚Üí Nat
toNat p2  = 2
toNat p3  = 3
toNat p5  = 5
toNat p7  = 7
toNat p11 = 11
toNat p13 = 13
toNat p17 = 17
toNat p19 = 19
toNat p23 = 23
toNat p29 = 29
toNat p31 = 31
toNat p41 = 41
toNat p47 = 47
toNat p59 = 59
toNat p71 = 71

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- toNat is injective because each prime maps to a unique Nat

toNat-injective : ‚ąÄ {p q} ‚Üí toNat p ‚Č° toNat q ‚Üí p ‚Č° q
toNat-injective {p = p2}  {q = p2}  refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p3}  {q = p3}  refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p5}  {q = p5}  refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p7}  {q = p7}  refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p11} {q = p11} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p13} {q = p13} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p17} {q = p17} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p19} {q = p19} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p23} {q = p23} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p29} {q = p29} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p31} {q = p31} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p41} {q = p41} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p47} {q = p47} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p59} {q = p59} refl = refl
toNat-injective {p = p71} {q = p71} refl = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Decide equality by comparing the embedded Nat values

_‚Čü_ : (p q : SSP) ‚Üí Dec (p ‚Č° q)
_‚Čü_ p q with nat‚Čü (toNat p) (toNat q)
... | yes eq   = yes (toNat-injective eq)
... | no contra = no (őĽ eq ‚Üí contra (cong toNat eq))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Endomorphism

Endo : ‚ąÄ {X} ‚Üí Set
Endo {X} = State X ‚Üí State X

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Composition

_‚ąė_ : ‚ąÄ {X} ‚Üí Endo {X} ‚Üí Endo {X} ‚Üí Endo {X}
(f ‚ąė g) s = f (g s)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Closure under composition

record Generated {X : Set}
                 (K : Endo {X})
                 : Set where

  field
    closed :
      ‚ąÄ (f g : Endo {X}) ‚Üí Endo {X}
module SWAR_Equivalence where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality as Eq using (cong; cong‚āā; sym; trans)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_; map; zipWith)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using ()
open import UFTC_Lattice using (Code; C_XOR)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lane-wise reference operation:
laneXOR : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Code n ‚Üí Vec Code n ‚Üí Vec Code n
laneXOR = zipWith C_XOR

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract packed SWAR representation + pack/unpack:
postulate
  Packed : Nat ‚Üí Set
  pack   : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Code n ‚Üí Packed n
  unpack : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Packed n ‚Üí Vec Code n

-- Packed operation (your SWAR fast-path):
postulate
  swarXOR : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Packed n ‚Üí Packed n ‚Üí Packed n

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The *only* thing you need to trust SWAR: a bisimulation/refinement law.

record SWARCorrect : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    -- pack/unpack are section/retraction on the domain you care about
    unpack-pack : ‚ąÄ {n} (v : Vec Code n) ‚Üí unpack (pack v) ‚Č° v

    -- swarXOR refines laneXOR through unpack
    swar-sound :
      ‚ąÄ {n} (x y : Packed n) ‚Üí
        unpack (swarXOR x y) ‚Č° laneXOR (unpack x) (unpack y)

-- Derived: swarXOR correct on packed values built from vectors
swar-correct-on-packed :
  (C : SWARCorrect) ‚Üí
  ‚ąÄ {n} (vx vy : Vec Code n) ‚Üí
    unpack (swarXOR (pack vx) (pack vy)) ‚Č° laneXOR vx vy
swar-correct-on-packed C vx vy =
  let open SWARCorrect C in
  trans (swar-sound (pack vx) (pack vy))
        (cong‚āā laneXOR (unpack-pack vx) (unpack-pack vy))
module PrimeSubsetModel where

open import MDL
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract prime index

PrimeIndex : Set
PrimeIndex = Nat

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- General subset model

record PrimeModel (D : Dataset) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    subsetSize : Nat
    subsetId   : Subset subsetSize
    baseModel  : Model D

primeTotal :
  ‚ąÄ {D} ‚Üí
  PrimeModel D ‚Üí
  CodeLength
primeTotal {D} M =
  subsetCost (PrimeModel.subsetSize M) (PrimeModel.subsetId M)
    + modelTotalLength (PrimeModel.baseModel M)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 71-restricted version

record PrimeModel71 (D : Dataset) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    base : PrimeModel D
    sizeBound : PrimeModel.subsetSize base ‚Č§ 71

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Safety theorem

subsetBoundedCost :
  ‚ąÄ {D}
  (M : PrimeModel71 D) ‚Üí
  PrimeModel.subsetSize (PrimeModel71.base M) ‚Č§ 71

subsetBoundedCost M =
  PrimeModel71.sizeBound M

  (f (Vector.input v) ‚Č° g (Vector.input v)) √ó ConformsOn f g vs

module Base369 where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Utility: repeated rotation
------------------------------------------------------------------------

spin : {A : Set} ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí (A ‚Üí A) ‚Üí A ‚Üí A
spin 0       rot x = x
spin (suc n) rot x = rot (spin n rot x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Truth values
------------------------------------------------------------------------

data TriTruth : Set where
  tri-low  : TriTruth
  tri-mid  : TriTruth
  tri-high : TriTruth

tri-index : TriTruth ‚Üí Nat
tri-index tri-low  = 0
tri-index tri-mid  = 1
tri-index tri-high = 2

rotateTri : TriTruth ‚Üí TriTruth
rotateTri tri-low  = tri-mid
rotateTri tri-mid  = tri-high
rotateTri tri-high = tri-low

triXor : TriTruth ‚Üí TriTruth ‚Üí TriTruth
triXor carrier target = spin (tri-index carrier) rotateTri target

rotateTri¬≥ : ‚ąÄ t ‚Üí rotateTri (rotateTri (rotateTri t)) ‚Č° t
rotateTri¬≥ tri-low  = refl
rotateTri¬≥ tri-mid  = refl
rotateTri¬≥ tri-high = refl

triXor-identityň° : ‚ąÄ t ‚Üí triXor tri-low t ‚Č° t
triXor-identityň° _ = refl

triXor-assoc : ‚ąÄ a b c ‚Üí triXor a (triXor b c) ‚Č° triXor (triXor a b) c
triXor-assoc tri-low  _        _ = refl
triXor-assoc tri-mid  tri-low  c = refl
triXor-assoc tri-mid  tri-mid  c = refl
triXor-assoc tri-mid  tri-high c rewrite rotateTri¬≥ c = refl
triXor-assoc tri-high tri-low  c rewrite rotateTri¬≥ c = refl
triXor-assoc tri-high tri-mid  c rewrite rotateTri¬≥ c = refl
triXor-assoc tri-high tri-high c rewrite rotateTri¬≥ c = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- A hexadic universe: six ‚Äúbeats‚ÄĚ that wrap around.

data HexTruth : Set where
  hex-0 hex-1 hex-2 hex-3 hex-4 hex-5 : HexTruth

hex-index : HexTruth ‚Üí Nat
hex-index hex-0 = 0
hex-index hex-1 = 1
hex-index hex-2 = 2
hex-index hex-3 = 3
hex-index hex-4 = 4
hex-index hex-5 = 5

rotateHex : HexTruth ‚Üí HexTruth
rotateHex hex-0 = hex-1
rotateHex hex-1 = hex-2
rotateHex hex-2 = hex-3
rotateHex hex-3 = hex-4
rotateHex hex-4 = hex-5
rotateHex hex-5 = hex-0

hexXor : HexTruth ‚Üí HexTruth ‚Üí HexTruth
hexXor carrier target = spin (hex-index carrier) rotateHex target

rotateHex‚Ā∂ : ‚ąÄ h ‚Üí spin 6 rotateHex h ‚Č° h
rotateHex‚Ā∂ hex-0 = refl
rotateHex‚Ā∂ hex-1 = refl
rotateHex‚Ā∂ hex-2 = refl
rotateHex‚Ā∂ hex-3 = refl
rotateHex‚Ā∂ hex-4 = refl
rotateHex‚Ā∂ hex-5 = refl

hexXor-identityň° : ‚ąÄ h ‚Üí hexXor hex-0 h ‚Č° h
hexXor-identityň° _ = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- A nonary universe: nine ‚Äúvoxels‚ÄĚ in a ring.

data NonaryTruth : Set where
  non-0 non-1 non-2 non-3 non-4 non-5 non-6 non-7 non-8 : NonaryTruth

nonary-index : NonaryTruth ‚Üí Nat
nonary-index non-0 = 0
nonary-index non-1 = 1
nonary-index non-2 = 2
nonary-index non-3 = 3
nonary-index non-4 = 4
nonary-index non-5 = 5
nonary-index non-6 = 6
nonary-index non-7 = 7
nonary-index non-8 = 8

rotateNonary : NonaryTruth ‚Üí NonaryTruth
rotateNonary non-0 = non-1
rotateNonary non-1 = non-2
rotateNonary non-2 = non-3
rotateNonary non-3 = non-4
rotateNonary non-4 = non-5
rotateNonary non-5 = non-6
rotateNonary non-6 = non-7
rotateNonary non-7 = non-8
rotateNonary non-8 = non-0

nonaryXor : NonaryTruth ‚Üí NonaryTruth ‚Üí NonaryTruth
nonaryXor carrier target = spin (nonary-index carrier) rotateNonary target

rotateNonary‚ĀĻ : ‚ąÄ n ‚Üí spin 9 rotateNonary n ‚Č° n
rotateNonary‚ĀĻ non-0 = refl
rotateNonary‚ĀĻ non-1 = refl
rotateNonary‚ĀĻ non-2 = refl
rotateNonary‚ĀĻ non-3 = refl
rotateNonary‚ĀĻ non-4 = refl
rotateNonary‚ĀĻ non-5 = refl
rotateNonary‚ĀĻ non-6 = refl
rotateNonary‚ĀĻ non-7 = refl
rotateNonary‚ĀĻ non-8 = refl

nonaryXor-identityň° : ‚ąÄ n ‚Üí nonaryXor non-0 n ‚Č° n
nonaryXor-identityň° _ = refl
module HeckeScan where

open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)

open import MonsterOntos

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A computational/cognitive state.
postulate
  State : Set

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Hecke operator family: T_p : State ‚Üí State for each p in the ontos.

record HeckeFamily : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    T : SSP ‚Üí State ‚Üí State

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A "compatibility detector" is just a predicate you choose.
-- Example: does the state remain invariant under T_p?

Compat : HeckeFamily ‚Üí SSP ‚Üí State ‚Üí Bool
Compat H p s = true  -- placeholder; define concretely in your pipeline

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A scan produces a 15-bit signature (compatibility bits across primes).

record Sig15 : Set where
  constructor sig15
  field
    b2  : Bool; b3  : Bool; b5  : Bool; b7  : Bool; b11 : Bool
    b13 : Bool; b17 : Bool; b19 : Bool; b23 : Bool; b29 : Bool
    b31 : Bool; b41 : Bool; b47 : Bool; b59 : Bool; b71 : Bool

scan : HeckeFamily ‚Üí State ‚Üí Sig15
scan H s = sig15
  (Compat H p2  s) (Compat H p3  s) (Compat H p5  s) (Compat H p7  s) (Compat H p11 s)
  (Compat H p13 s) (Compat H p17 s) (Compat H p19 s) (Compat H p23 s) (Compat H p29 s)
  (Compat H p31 s) (Compat H p41 s) (Compat H p47 s) (Compat H p59 s) (Compat H p71 s)

       ‚Üí step L cands s‚āÄ ‚Č° s‚āĀ

-- The stage transition is 4-periodic.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Kernel algebra tests
------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- A concrete "kernel" instance: identity update.
K-id : ‚ąÄ {X : Set} ‚Üí Kernel {X}
K-id {X} = record
  { K = őĽ s ‚Üí s
  ; involutive-respecting = őĽ s ‚Üí refl
  }

-- Another concrete kernel: pointwise involution.
K-neg : ‚ąÄ {X : Set} ‚Üí Kernel {X}
K-neg {X} = record
  { K = őĻ
  ; involutive-respecting = őĽ s ‚Üí refl
  }

-- Sanity: K-neg applied twice is identity (pointwise).
K-neg2-pointwise : ‚ąÄ {X : Set} (s : State X) (x : X) ‚Üí
  Kernel.K (K-neg {X}) (Kernel.K (K-neg {X}) s) x ‚Č° s x
K-neg2-pointwise s x = őĻ¬≤-id s x

module MonsterUltrametric where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.List
open import Data.Nat as Nat using (_<_; _‚Č§_; zero; suc)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

open import Ultrametric
open import MonsterMask

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Distance = index of first differing bit (or 0 if identical)

firstDiff : Mask ‚Üí Mask ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat
firstDiff [] [] _ = 0
firstDiff (true  ‚ą∑ xs) (true  ‚ą∑ ys) n = firstDiff xs ys (suc n)
firstDiff (false ‚ą∑ xs) (false ‚ą∑ ys) n = firstDiff xs ys (suc n)
firstDiff _ _ n = n

dMask : Mask ‚Üí Mask ‚Üí Nat
dMask x y = firstDiff x y 0

firstDiff-self-zero : ‚ąÄ m n ‚Üí firstDiff m m n ‚Č° 0
firstDiff-self-zero [] n = refl
firstDiff-self-zero (true ‚ą∑ xs) n = firstDiff-self-zero xs (suc n)
firstDiff-self-zero (false ‚ą∑ xs) n = firstDiff-self-zero xs (suc n)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Identity distance

id-zeroMask : ‚ąÄ m ‚Üí dMask m m ‚Č° 0
id-zeroMask m = firstDiff-self-zero m 0

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Symmetry

postulate
  symMask : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí dMask x y ‚Č° dMask y x
  ultraMask : ‚ąÄ x y z ‚Üí dMask x z ‚Č§ max (dMask x y) (dMask y z)

------------------------------------------------------------------------

UMask : Ultrametric Mask
UMask = record
  { d            = dMask
  ; id-zero      = id-zeroMask
  ; symmetric    = symMask
  ; ultratriangle = ultraMask
  }
module MonsterSpec where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat)
open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List)

open import MonsterState
open import MonsterStep

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Canonical spec = step + optional encoding function.

record Spec : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    L     : Lens
    cands : Candidates

  stepSpec : State ‚Üí State
  stepSpec = step L cands

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Optional: a G√∂del-style encoding of state ‚Üí Nat (placeholder).
-- Keep it separate: encoding is a different layer from stepping.

postulate
  encode : State ‚Üí Nat
  decode : Nat ‚Üí State

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The canonical property you‚Äôll ultimately want:
-- decode (encode s) ‚Č° s  (and/or encode ‚ąė decode id on a domain)
module HGSA_Fixpoints where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Nat.Base using (_<_ )
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Verification.Prelude using (‚ä•; ‚ä§; tt; ő£; _,_; _√ó_; ¬¨_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality as Eq using (trans; cong)
open import Data.Sum.Base using (_‚äé_; inj‚āĀ; inj‚āā)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract state machine for HGSA
postulate
  State : Set
  step  : State ‚Üí State

-- Observable predicates
postulate
  Safe   : State ‚Üí Set
  Ascend : State ‚Üí Set   -- ‚Äúthis step is an ascend event‚ÄĚ (or state tagged)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Least fixpoint style ‚ÄúEventually‚ÄĚ (inductive)
data Eventually (P : State ‚Üí Set) : State ‚Üí Set where
  now  : ‚ąÄ {s} ‚Üí P s ‚Üí Eventually P s
  later : ‚ąÄ {s} ‚Üí Eventually P (step s) ‚Üí Eventually P s

-- AlwaysEventuallySafe: eventually Safe OR Ascend
AES : State ‚Üí Set
AES s = Eventually (őĽ t ‚Üí Safe t ‚äé Ascend t) s

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Ranking-function obligation: progress unless already Safe/Ascend.
postulate
  rank : State ‚Üí Nat
  progress :
    ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí (¬¨ Safe s) ‚Üí (¬¨ Ascend s) ‚Üí rank (step s) < rank s

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Termination/liveness proof from rank (standard well-founded descent)
-- In Nat, strict descent implies cannot continue forever without hitting base.

postulate
  NatNoInfiniteDescent :
    ‚ąÄ (r : State ‚Üí Nat) (f : State ‚Üí State) ‚Üí
    (‚ąÄ s ‚Üí r (f s) < r s) ‚Üí ‚ä•

-- Practical AES theorem: Either Safe/Ascend holds now, or progress gives later.
postulate
  decideSafe : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí (Safe s ‚äé ¬¨ Safe s)
  decideAsc  : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí (Ascend s ‚äé ¬¨ Ascend s)

{-# NON_TERMINATING #-}
AES-theorem : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí AES s
AES-theorem s with decideSafe s | decideAsc s
... | inj‚āĀ safeNow | _          = now (inj‚āĀ safeNow)
... | inj‚āā ns      | inj‚āĀ ascNow = now (inj‚āā ascNow)
... | inj‚āā ns      | inj‚āā na     =
    later (AES-theorem (step s))
module Overflow where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat ; zero ; suc)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Local congruence lemma (no stdlib needed)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

congOverflow : ‚ąÄ {A B : Set} {x y : A} (f : A ‚Üí B) ‚Üí x ‚Č° y ‚Üí f x ‚Č° f y
congOverflow f refl = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Basic relations on ‚Ąē (custom strict order)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

infix 4 _‚Čļ_

data _‚Čļ_ : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Set where
  z‚Čļs : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí zero ‚Čļ suc n
  s‚Čļs : ‚ąÄ {m n} ‚Üí m ‚Čļ n ‚Üí suc m ‚Čļ suc n

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Voxel states
------------------------------------------------------------------------

data Voxel : Set where
  grounded plateau ascended : Voxel

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Threshold guards with explicit proofs
------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- Each constructor carries the witness required to justify the
-- classification relative to the threshold.
data VoxelGuard (threshold value : Nat) : Set where
  stay   : value ‚Čļ threshold ‚Üí VoxelGuard threshold value
  pivot  : threshold ‚Č° value ‚Üí VoxelGuard threshold value
  ascend : threshold ‚Čļ value ‚Üí VoxelGuard threshold value

state : ‚ąÄ {t v} ‚Üí VoxelGuard t v ‚Üí Voxel
state (stay _)   = grounded
state (pivot _)  = plateau
state (ascend _) = ascended

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Helper: deterministically choose a guard by structural comparison
------------------------------------------------------------------------

data Order : Set where below equal above : Order

compare : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Order
compare zero    zero    = equal
compare zero    (suc _) = below
compare (suc _) zero    = above
compare (suc a) (suc b) = compare a b

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Relations exposed by comparison tokens
------------------------------------------------------------------------

compare-below‚Üí‚Čļ : ‚ąÄ {t v} ‚Üí compare t v ‚Č° below ‚Üí t ‚Čļ v
compare-below‚Üí‚Čļ {zero}   {zero}   ()
compare-below‚Üí‚Čļ {zero}   {suc _}  refl = z‚Čļs
compare-below‚Üí‚Čļ {suc _}  {zero}   ()
compare-below‚Üí‚Čļ {suc t}  {suc v}  pr   = s‚Čļs (compare-below‚Üí‚Čļ {t} {v} pr)

compare-above‚Üí‚Čļ : ‚ąÄ {t v} ‚Üí compare t v ‚Č° above ‚Üí v ‚Čļ t
compare-above‚Üí‚Čļ {zero}   {zero}   ()
compare-above‚Üí‚Čļ {zero}   {suc _}  ()
compare-above‚Üí‚Čļ {suc _}  {zero}   refl = z‚Čļs
compare-above‚Üí‚Čļ {suc t}  {suc v}  pr   = s‚Čļs (compare-above‚Üí‚Čļ {t} {v} pr)

compare-equal‚Üí‚Č° : ‚ąÄ {t v} ‚Üí compare t v ‚Č° equal ‚Üí t ‚Č° v
compare-equal‚Üí‚Č° {zero}  {zero}  refl = refl
compare-equal‚Üí‚Č° {zero}  {suc _} ()
compare-equal‚Üí‚Č° {suc _} {zero} ()
compare-equal‚Üí‚Č° {suc t} {suc v} pr = congOverflow suc (compare-equal‚Üí‚Č° {t} {v} pr)

compare-‚Čļ‚Üíbelow : ‚ąÄ {t v} ‚Üí t ‚Čļ v ‚Üí compare t v ‚Č° below
compare-‚Čļ‚Üíbelow z‚Čļs      = refl
compare-‚Čļ‚Üíbelow (s‚Čļs p)  = compare-‚Čļ‚Üíbelow p

compare-roundtrip-below : ‚ąÄ {t v} (p : t ‚Čļ v) ‚Üí compare-below‚Üí‚Čļ (compare-‚Čļ‚Üíbelow p) ‚Č° p
compare-roundtrip-below z‚Čļs      = refl
compare-roundtrip-below (s‚Čļs p)  = congOverflow s‚Čļs (compare-roundtrip-below p)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Enforcement by comparison
------------------------------------------------------------------------


open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_; refl)

enforce : (threshold value : Nat) ‚Üí VoxelGuard threshold value
enforce zero    zero    = pivot refl
enforce zero    (suc v) = ascend z‚Čļs
enforce (suc t) zero    = stay z‚Čļs
enforce (suc t) (suc v) with enforce t v
... | stay p   = stay   (s‚Čļs p)
... | pivot p  = pivot  (congOverflow suc p)
... | ascend p = ascend (s‚Čļs p)


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Correctness of enforcement
------------------------------------------------------------------------

enforce-ascended-if : ‚ąÄ {t v} (p : t ‚Čļ v) ‚Üí enforce t v ‚Č° ascend p
enforce-ascended-if {zero}  {suc v} z‚Čļs = refl
enforce-ascended-if {suc t} {suc v} (s‚Čļs p) rewrite enforce-ascended-if {t} {v} p = refl

only-if : ‚ąÄ {t v} ‚Üí state (enforce t v) ‚Č° ascended ‚Üí t ‚Čļ v
only-if {t} {v} with enforce t v
... | stay   _ = őĽ ()
... | pivot  _ = őĽ ()
... | ascend p = őĽ _ ‚Üí p

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Extra comparison lemmas (if you still want them)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

compare-eq-below : ‚ąÄ {t v} ‚Üí compare t v ‚Č° below ‚Üí t ‚Čļ v
compare-eq-below {zero}    {zero}    ()
compare-eq-below {zero}    {suc _}   refl = z‚Čļs
compare-eq-below {suc _}   {zero}    ()
compare-eq-below {suc t}   {suc v}   p = s‚Čļs (compare-eq-below {t} {v} p)

compare-eq-above : ‚ąÄ {t v} ‚Üí compare t v ‚Č° above ‚Üí v ‚Čļ t
compare-eq-above {zero}    {zero}    ()
compare-eq-above {zero}    {suc _}   ()
compare-eq-above {suc _}   {zero}    refl = z‚Čļs
compare-eq-above {suc t}   {suc v}   p = s‚Čļs (compare-eq-above {t} {v} p)
{-# OPTIONS --safe #-}

  : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    _‚Č§_ : D ‚Üí D ‚Üí Set
    NonZero : D ‚Üí Set
    mono : ‚ąÄ {x y} ‚Üí NonZero (Ultrametric.d U x y) ‚Üí

module DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropyInstanceShiftTailPerm where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail-permutation isotropy instance (skeleton).
-- To keep the closure spine postulate-free, do NOT wire this into
-- TernaryRealInstanceShift until the postulates below are discharged.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  permGroup : ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí Iso.Group (TP.Perm k)

act : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí TP.Perm k ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)
act {m} {k} p x = TP.actTailPerm {m} {k} p x

postulate
  preservesMetric :
    ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
    (U : UMetric.Ultrametric (RTC.Carrier (m + k))) ‚Üí
    ‚ąÄ p ‚Üí Iso.PreservesMetric U (act {m} {k} p)

  tailPerm-RŠĶ£ :
    ‚ąÄ {m k} (p : TP.Perm k) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
      ROSS.R {m} {k} (act p x) ‚Č° act p (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)

  tailPerm-PŠĶ£ :
    ‚ąÄ {m k} (p : TP.Perm k) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
      ROSS.P {m} {k} (act p x) ‚Č° act p (ROSS.P {m} {k} x)

  tailPerm-CŠĶ£ :
    ‚ąÄ {m k} (p : TP.Perm k) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
      ROSS.C {m} {k} (act p x) ‚Č° act p (ROSS.C {m} {k} x)

commutesWithT :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí (p : TP.Perm k) ‚Üí (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
    ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} (act p x)))
      ‚Č° act p (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
commutesWithT {m} {k} p x =
  TP.commutesWithT-CPR
    (ROSS.R {m} {k})
    (ROSS.P {m} {k})
    (ROSS.C {m} {k})
    p
    (tailPerm-RŠĶ£ p)
    (tailPerm-PŠĶ£ p)
    (tailPerm-CŠĶ£ p)

realIsotropyInstanceShiftTailPerm :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  RIS.RealIsotropy (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
    (őĽ x ‚Üí ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
realIsotropyInstanceShiftTailPerm {m} {k} =
  record
    { iso =
        record
          { G = TP.Perm k
          ; group = permGroup
          ; act = act
          ; preservesMetric = preservesMetric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
          ; commutesWithT = commutesWithT {m} {k}
          }
    ; coneInvariant = TP.Perm k
    }

module DASHI.Geometry.ClosestPoint where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Data.Product using (ő£; _,_)

open import DASHI.Core.Q using (‚Ąö; _+‚Ąö_; _-‚Ąö_; _*‚Ąö_; 0‚Ąö; 1‚Ąö; two‚Ąö)
open import Data.Rational using (_‚Č§_)

record Quadratic (‚Ąď : Level) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    V   : Set ‚Ąď
    _+_ : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí V
    _-_ : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí V
    _¬∑_ : ‚Ąö ‚Üí V ‚Üí V
    Q   : V ‚Üí ‚Ąö
    Qpos : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí 0‚Ąö ‚Č§ Q x
    Qhom : ‚ąÄ (a : ‚Ąö) x ‚Üí Q (a ¬∑ x) ‚Č° (a *‚Ąö a) *‚Ąö Q x
    Qpara : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí
      (Q (x + y) +‚Ąö Q (x - y)) ‚Č°
      ((two‚Ąö *‚Ąö Q x) +‚Ąö (two‚Ąö *‚Ąö Q y))

record ProjectionOnto (‚Ąď : Level) (V : Set ‚Ąď) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    S   : V ‚Üí Set ‚Ąď
    P   : V ‚Üí V
    PinS : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí S (P x)
    Pid : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí P (P x) ‚Č° P x

record ClosestPointAxioms (‚Ąď : Level) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    Qd   : Quadratic ‚Ąď
    Prj  : ProjectionOnto ‚Ąď (Quadratic.V Qd)

  field
    -- Inner product via polarization (placeholder; you can supply the actual definition).
    ip : Quadratic.V Qd ‚Üí Quadratic.V Qd ‚Üí ‚Ąö
    -- ‚ÄúFirm nonexpansive‚ÄĚ in Q-geometry (inner product via polarization).
    -- This is the single seam from which ClosestPoint + Fej√©r follow.
    firm :
      ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí
        _‚Č§_
          (Quadratic.Q Qd
            (Quadratic._-_ Qd (ProjectionOnto.P Prj x) (ProjectionOnto.P Prj y)))
          (ip
            (Quadratic._-_ Qd (ProjectionOnto.P Prj x) (ProjectionOnto.P Prj y))
            (Quadratic._-_ Qd x y))

postulate
  ClosestPoint :
    ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} ‚Üí (A : ClosestPointAxioms ‚Ąď) ‚Üí
    let open ClosestPointAxioms A
    in
    ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí (‚ąÄ s ‚Üí ProjectionOnto.S Prj s ‚Üí
      _‚Č§_
        (Quadratic.Q Qd (Quadratic._-_ Qd x (ProjectionOnto.P Prj x)))
        (Quadratic.Q Qd (Quadratic._-_ Qd x s)))

  FejerMonotone :
    ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} ‚Üí (A : ClosestPointAxioms ‚Ąď) ‚Üí
    let open ClosestPointAxioms A
    in
    ‚ąÄ x s ‚Üí ProjectionOnto.S Prj s ‚Üí
      _‚Č§_
        (Quadratic.Q Qd (Quadratic._-_ Qd (ProjectionOnto.P Prj x) s))
        (Quadratic.Q Qd (Quadratic._-_ Qd x s))

  open EnergyDist ED
  field
    closest : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí Fix y ‚Üí E x (P x) ‚Üí E x y

    _-_ : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí V

Parallelogram :
  ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} (N : NormedSpace ‚Ąď) ‚Üí Set ‚Ąď
Parallelogram {‚Ąď} N =
  let open NormedSpace N in
  ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí
    ((‚ÄĖ x + y ‚ÄĖ *‚Ąö ‚ÄĖ x + y ‚ÄĖ) +‚Ąö (‚ÄĖ x - y ‚ÄĖ *‚Ąö ‚ÄĖ x - y ‚ÄĖ))
      ‚Č°
    ((two‚Ąö *‚Ąö (‚ÄĖ x ‚ÄĖ *‚Ąö ‚ÄĖ x ‚ÄĖ)) +‚Ąö (two‚Ąö *‚Ąö (‚ÄĖ y ‚ÄĖ *‚Ąö ‚ÄĖ y ‚ÄĖ)))

module DASHI.Geometry.EnergySplitProof where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_; refl; sym; cong; trans)
open import Data.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)

open import DASHI.Geometry.EnergyAdditivityProof

record ProjectionDefect {‚Ąď} (A : Additive {‚Ąď}) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  open Additive A
  field
    P      : Carrier ‚Üí Carrier
    D      : Carrier ‚Üí Carrier
    D-def  : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí D x ‚Č° x + (- (P x))
    P-idem : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí P (P x) ‚Č° P x
    decomp : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí x ‚Č° (P x) + (D x)

open ProjectionDefect public

EnergySplitProof :
  ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {A : Additive {‚Ąď}} {F : ScalarField {‚Ąď}}
  (V : InnerProductSpace A F) (T2 : Two F)
  (PD : ProjectionDefect A) ‚Üí
  (‚ąÄ x ‚Üí Orth V (P PD x) (D PD x)) ‚Üí
  (‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí Orth V x y ‚Üí E V ( _+_ A x y ) ‚Č° ( _+s_ F (E V x) (E V y) )) ‚Üí
  ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí E V x ‚Č° ( _+s_ F (E V (P PD x)) (E V (D PD x)) )
EnergySplitProof {A = A} {F = F} V T2 PD orthPD addE x =
  let open Additive A
      open ScalarField F
      open InnerProductSpace V
      open ProjectionDefect PD
  in
  trans (cong (E V) (decomp x))
        (addE (P x) (D x) (orthPD x))
module DASHI.Geometry.NatNoInfiniteDescent where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Data.Nat              using (_<_)
open import Data.Empty            using (‚ä•; ‚ä•-elim)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong)

iterate : ‚ąÄ {S : Set} ‚Üí (S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
iterate f zero    s = s
iterate f (suc n) s = iterate f n (f s)

-- No infinite strict descent on Nat:
-- If H(f s) < H s for all s, then starting from s‚āÄ you get an infinite
-- descending chain in Nat, which contradicts accessibility.
postulate
  NatNoInfiniteDescent :
    ‚ąÄ {S : Set} (H : S ‚Üí Nat) (f : S ‚Üí S) (s‚āÄ : S) ‚Üí
    (‚ąÄ s ‚Üí H (f s) < H s) ‚Üí ‚ä•
module DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeedInstanceShift where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeed as RFS
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Physics.RealOperatorStackShift as ROSS

open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC

-- Fixed locality radius (nontrivial, but simple).
radius : Nat
radius = suc zero

local : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí Set
local {n} x y = UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) x y ‚Č§ radius

preservesLocality :
  ‚ąÄ {m k} (x y : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  local x y ‚Üí
  local (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
        (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} y)))
preservesLocality {m} {k} x y h =
  let
    open UMetric.Ultrametric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
    step1 : d (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)) (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} y))
            ‚Č§ d (ROSS.R {m} {k} x) (ROSS.R {m} {k} y)
    step1 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (ROSS.nonexpP {m} {k}) (ROSS.R {m} {k} x) (ROSS.R {m} {k} y)
    step2 : d (ROSS.R {m} {k} x) (ROSS.R {m} {k} y) ‚Č§ d x y
    step2 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (ROSS.nonexpR {m} {k}) x y
    step3 : d (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
               (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} y)))
            ‚Č§ d (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x))
               (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} y))
    step3 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (ROSS.nonexpC {m} {k})
              (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x))
              (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} y))
  in
  NatP.‚Č§-trans (NatP.‚Č§-trans step3 step1) (NatP.‚Č§-trans step2 h)

realFiniteSpeedInstance :
  ‚ąÄ {m k} ‚Üí
  RFS.RealFiniteSpeed (őĽ x ‚Üí ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
realFiniteSpeedInstance {m} {k} =
  record
    { local = local {n = m + k}
    ; preservesLocality = preservesLocality {m} {k}
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.CompleteUltrametricNat where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Product using (ő£; _,_; proj‚āĀ; proj‚āā)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚Č§_; _<_; _‚Č•_; s‚Č§s; z‚Č§n)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (subst; sym)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Geometry.CompleteUltrametric as CU

private
  one : Nat
  one = suc zero

  one< : 0 < one
  one< = s‚Č§s z‚Č§n

-- Any ‚Ąē-valued ultrametric space is complete under the Cauchy definition.
completeNatUltrametric :
  ‚ąÄ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) ‚Üí CU.Complete U
completeNatUltrametric U =
  let open UMetric.Ultrametric U in
  record
    { limit = őĽ c ‚Üí CU.Cauchy.seq c (proj‚āĀ (CU.Cauchy.cauchy c one one<))
    ; converges = őĽ c őĶ őĶ>0 ‚Üí
        let
          N = proj‚āĀ (CU.Cauchy.cauchy c one one<)
          cauchy1 = proj‚āā (CU.Cauchy.cauchy c one one<)
          one‚Č§őĶ : one ‚Č§ őĶ
          one‚Č§őĶ = őĶ>0
        in
        N , őĽ n N‚Č§n ‚Üí
          let
            dNn = cauchy1 N n NatP.‚Č§-refl N‚Č§n
            dNn' = subst (őĽ t ‚Üí t < one)
                          (UMetric.Ultrametric.symmetric U (CU.Cauchy.seq c N) (CU.Cauchy.seq c n))
                          dNn
          in
          NatP.<-‚Č§-trans dNn' one‚Č§őĶ
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.CompleteUltrametric where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)

-- Cauchy sequence in an ‚Ąē-valued ultrametric.
record Cauchy {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) : Set‚āĀ where
  open UMetric.Ultrametric U public
  field
    seq : Nat ‚Üí S
    cauchy :
      ‚ąÄ őĶ ‚Üí 0 < őĶ ‚Üí ő£ Nat (őĽ N ‚Üí
        ‚ąÄ m n ‚Üí N ‚Č§ m ‚Üí N ‚Č§ n ‚Üí d (seq m) (seq n) < őĶ)

record Complete {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) : Set‚āĀ where
  open UMetric.Ultrametric U public
  field
    limit : Cauchy U ‚Üí S
    converges :
      (c : Cauchy U) ‚Üí
      ‚ąÄ őĶ ‚Üí 0 < őĶ ‚Üí ő£ Nat (őĽ N ‚Üí
        ‚ąÄ n ‚Üí N ‚Č§ n ‚Üí d (Cauchy.seq c n) (limit c) < őĶ)

open Cauchy public
open Complete public

module DASHI.Geometry.NoStrictDescentForInvertible where

record InvertibleNat (S : Set) : Set where
  field
    step  : S ‚Üí S
    inv   : S ‚Üí S
    left  : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí inv (step s) ‚Č° s
    right : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí step (inv s) ‚Č° s
    H     : S ‚Üí Nat

-- Invertible step implies you can ‚Äúwalk backwards forever‚ÄĚ,
-- contradicting strict descent everywhere.
invertible-no-strict-descent :
  ‚ąÄ {S} (U : InvertibleNat S) ‚Üí
  (s‚āÄ : S) ‚Üí
  ¬¨ (‚ąÄ s ‚Üí InvertibleNat.H U (InvertibleNat.step U s) < InvertibleNat.H U s)
invertible-no-strict-descent U s‚āÄ strict =
  NatNoInfiniteDescent (InvertibleNat.H U) (InvertibleNat.step U) s‚āÄ strict

module DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Stream where

-- Functional streams.
Stream : ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} ‚Üí Set ‚Ąď ‚Üí Set ‚Ąď
Stream A = ‚Ąē ‚Üí A

-- LCP predicate: agree on first k digits.
Depth‚Č• : ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {A : Set ‚Ąď} ‚Üí Stream A ‚Üí Stream A ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí Set ‚Ąď
Depth‚Č• xs ys k = ‚ąÄ i ‚Üí i ‚Č§ k ‚Üí xs i ‚Č° ys i

lcp‚Č• : ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {A : Set ‚Ąď} ‚Üí Stream A ‚Üí Stream A ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí Set ‚Ąď

module DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Cauchy where

_‚Č•_ : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí Set
m ‚Č• n = n ‚Č§ m

-- Cauchy with modulus (constructive).
CauchyMod : ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {A : Set ‚Ąď} ‚Üí (xs : ‚Ąē ‚Üí Stream A) ‚Üí Set ‚Ąď
CauchyMod xs = ‚ąÄ k ‚Üí ő£ ‚Ąē (őĽ N ‚Üí ‚ąÄ {m n} ‚Üí m ‚Č• N ‚Üí n ‚Č• N ‚Üí lcp‚Č• (xs m) (xs n) k)
module DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Limit where

open import Data.Nat using (‚Ąē; suc; _‚Č§_) 
open import Data.Product using (ő£; _,_; proj‚āĀ; proj‚āā)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Stream using (Stream; lcp‚Č•)
open import DASHI.Geometry.LCP.Cauchy using (CauchyMod; _‚Č•_)

Nof : ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {A : Set ‚Ąď} ‚Üí (xs : ‚Ąē ‚Üí Stream A) ‚Üí CauchyMod xs ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē
Nof xs c k = proj‚āĀ (c k)

limit : ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {A : Set ‚Ąď} ‚Üí (xs : ‚Ąē ‚Üí Stream A) ‚Üí CauchyMod xs ‚Üí Stream A
limit xs c i = (xs (Nof xs c (suc i))) i

-- Helper lemmas (left as postulates to avoid proof boilerplate here).
  lcp‚Č•-mono :
    ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {A : Set ‚Ąď} {x y : Stream A} {j k}
    ‚Üí j ‚Č§ k ‚Üí lcp‚Č• x y k ‚Üí lcp‚Č• x y j
  lcp‚Č•-mono j‚Č§k hyp i i‚Č§j = hyp i (NatP.‚Č§-trans i‚Č§j j‚Č§k)

  lcp‚Č•-at :
    ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {A : Set ‚Ąď} {x y : Stream A}
    ‚Üí ‚ąÄ i ‚Üí lcp‚Č• x y (suc i) ‚Üí x i ‚Č° y i
  lcp‚Č•-at i hyp = hyp i (NatP.n‚Č§1+n i)

-- Convergence: eventually xs n agrees with limit on first k digits.
postulate
  converges‚Č• :
    ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {A : Set ‚Ąď}
    ‚Üí (xs : ‚Ąē ‚Üí Stream A)
    ‚Üí (c : CauchyMod xs)
    ‚Üí ‚ąÄ k ‚Üí ő£ ‚Ąē (őĽ N ‚Üí ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí n ‚Č• N ‚Üí lcp‚Č• (xs n) (limit xs c) k)

      Geometry.GőľőĹ geometry x y ‚Č°
      Matter.TőľőĹ (BianchiBundle.matter bundle) x y

  ‚Üí (bundle : BianchiBundle geometry)

    { first = BianchiBundle.first bundle

    ; conservation = BianchiBundle.conservation bundle

module DASHI.Geometry.MaskedQuadratic where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; zipWith; []; _‚ą∑_)
open import Data.Product using (ő£; _,_)

open import DASHI.Core.Q using (‚Ąö; _*‚Ąö_; _+‚Ąö_; 0‚Ąö)

sum‚Ąö : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec ‚Ąö n ‚Üí ‚Ąö
sum‚Ąö {zero} [] = 0‚Ąö
sum‚Ąö {suc n} (x ‚ą∑ xs) = x +‚Ąö sum‚Ąö xs

data Signature : Set where
  sig31 sig13 sig22 sig40 sig04 : Signature

record MaskedQuadratic (n : Nat) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    V      : Set
    vec    : V ‚Üí Vec ‚Ąö n
    mask   : Vec ‚Ąö n
    Q      : V ‚Üí ‚Ąö
    Q-def  : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí
      Q x ‚Č° sum‚Ąö (zipWith (őĽ m xi ‚Üí (m *‚Ąö xi) *‚Ąö xi) mask (vec x))
    signature : ő£ Nat (őĽ p ‚Üí ő£ Nat (őĽ q ‚Üí p + q ‚Č° n))
    signatureTag : Signature
    nondeg : Set

module DASHI.Geometry.ShiftIsotropyTailPerm where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_; proj‚āĀ; proj‚āā)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; _++_; lookup; tabulate)
open import Data.Fin using (Fin)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof using (coarseOf; tailOf)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail permutations as lookup tables

Perm : Nat ‚Üí Set
Perm k = Vec (Fin k) k

permuteVec : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} {k : Nat} ‚Üí Perm k ‚Üí Vec A k ‚Üí Vec A k
permuteVec {A} {k} p xs = tabulate (őĽ i ‚Üí lookup (lookup p i) xs)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail action on full vectors: preserve coarse prefix, permute tail

actTailPerm : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Perm k ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k) ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k)
actTailPerm {m} {k} p x =
  coarseOf m k x ++ permuteVec p (tailOf m k x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Commutation lemma for composite T = C ‚ąė P ‚ąė R

commutesWithT-CPR :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat}
  (R P C : Vec Trit (m + k) ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k))
  (p : Perm k) ‚Üí
  (‚ąÄ x ‚Üí R (actTailPerm {m} {k} p x) ‚Č° actTailPerm p (R x)) ‚Üí
  (‚ąÄ x ‚Üí P (actTailPerm {m} {k} p x) ‚Č° actTailPerm p (P x)) ‚Üí
  (‚ąÄ x ‚Üí C (actTailPerm {m} {k} p x) ‚Č° actTailPerm p (C x)) ‚Üí
  (‚ąÄ x ‚Üí C (P (R (actTailPerm {m} {k} p x))) ‚Č° actTailPerm p (C (P (R x))))
commutesWithT-CPR R P C p commR commP commC x =
  trans
    (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí C (P v)) (commR x))
    (trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí C v) (commP (R x)))
           (commC (P (R x))))

module DASHI.Geometry.NoLeakageOrthogonality where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

----------------------------------------------------------------
-- Inner-product data supplied as assumptions (no metas/stubs).
----------------------------------------------------------------

record InnerProductData : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    V : Set
    _+_ _-_ _*_ : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí V
    0v : V
    two : V
    ‚ü™_,_‚üę : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí V
    ‚ą•_‚ą•¬≤ : V ‚Üí V
    add-norm¬≤ :
      ‚ąÄ a b ‚Üí ‚ą• a + b ‚ą•¬≤ ‚Č° (‚ą• a ‚ą•¬≤ + ‚ą• b ‚ą•¬≤) + (two * ‚ü™ a , b ‚üę)
    cancel-add-left : ‚ąÄ {a c} ‚Üí a ‚Č° a + c ‚Üí c ‚Č° 0v
    div2-zero : ‚ąÄ {z} ‚Üí two * z ‚Č° 0v ‚Üí z ‚Č° 0v

----------------------------------------------------------------
-- Projections and ‚Äúno leakage ‚áí orthogonality‚ÄĚ
----------------------------------------------------------------

record Projection (D : InnerProductData) : Set‚āĀ where
  open InnerProductData D
  field
    P : V ‚Üí V
    idem : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí P (P x) ‚Č° P x
    split : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí P x + (x - P x) ‚Č° x

coarse : ‚ąÄ {D} ‚Üí Projection D ‚Üí InnerProductData.V D ‚Üí InnerProductData.V D
coarse Pr x = Projection.P Pr x

detail : ‚ąÄ {D} ‚Üí Projection D ‚Üí InnerProductData.V D ‚Üí InnerProductData.V D
detail {D} Pr x =
  let open InnerProductData D in x - Projection.P Pr x

NoLeakage : ‚ąÄ {D} ‚Üí Projection D ‚Üí Set
NoLeakage {D} Pr =
  ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí ‚ą• x ‚ą•¬≤ ‚Č° ‚ą• coarse Pr x ‚ą•¬≤ + ‚ą• detail Pr x ‚ą•¬≤
  where open InnerProductData D

Orthogonal : ‚ąÄ {D} ‚Üí Projection D ‚Üí Set
Orthogonal {D} Pr =
  ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí ‚ü™ coarse Pr x , detail Pr x ‚üę ‚Č° 0v
  where open InnerProductData D

NoLeakage‚áíOrthogonal :
  ‚ąÄ {D} (Pr : Projection D) ‚Üí
  NoLeakage Pr ‚Üí
  Orthogonal Pr
NoLeakage‚áíOrthogonal {D} Pr NL x =
  let open Projection Pr
      open InnerProductData D
      c = coarse Pr x
      d = detail Pr x
      eq1 = NL x
      eq2 = add-norm¬≤ c d
      eqSplit = sym (cong (őĽ z ‚Üí ‚ą• z ‚ą•¬≤) (split x))
      eq2' = trans eqSplit eq2
      eq3 = trans (sym eq1) eq2'
  in
  div2-zero (cancel-add-left eq3)

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_)

record Polarization (‚Ąď : Level) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    V : Set ‚Ąď
    _+_ : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí V
    _-_ : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí V
    Q : V ‚Üí ‚Ąö
    ‚ü™_,_‚üę : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí ‚Ąö
    polarization :
      ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí four‚Ąö *‚Ąö ‚ü™ x , y ‚üę ‚Č° Q (x + y) -‚Ąö Q (x - y)

module DASHI.Geometry.ParallelogramToInnerProduct where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma using (ő£; _,_)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)

postulate
  V : Set
  _+_ _-_ : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí V
  0v : V

  ‚Ąö : Set
  _+q_ _-q_ _*q_ : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö
  inv2 inv4 : ‚Ąö

  ‚ą•_‚ą•¬≤ : V ‚Üí ‚Ąö

Parallelogram : Set
Parallelogram =
  ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí
    ‚ą• (x + y) ‚ą•¬≤ +q ‚ą• (x - y) ‚ą•¬≤ ‚Č°
    (inv2 *q ((‚ą• x ‚ą•¬≤ +q ‚ą• x ‚ą•¬≤) +q (‚ą• y ‚ą•¬≤ +q ‚ą• y ‚ą•¬≤)))

polarization : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí ‚Ąö
polarization x y =
  inv4 *q (‚ą• (x + y) ‚ą•¬≤ -q ‚ą• (x - y) ‚ą•¬≤)

record InnerProduct : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    ip : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí ‚Ąö

Parallelogram‚áíInnerProduct :
  Parallelogram ‚Üí
  InnerProduct
Parallelogram‚áíInnerProduct _ = record { ip = polarization }

-- The polarization identity is captured by `ip`, enabling downstream use of the quadratic form.
module DASHI.Geometry.FixedPointExistence_Projection where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (trans; sym)

open import DASHI.Algebra.MonsterMask15 using (Mask15; Kernel; projectTo)
open import DASHI.Algebra.MonsterUltrametric15 using (UMask15)
open import Ultrametric

Fixed : (Mask15 ‚Üí Mask15) ‚Üí Mask15 ‚Üí Set
Fixed K m = K m ‚Č° m

iterate : (Mask15 ‚Üí Mask15) ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Mask15 ‚Üí Mask15
iterate K zero    m = m
iterate K (suc n) m = iterate K n (K m)

-- For projection K = őĽ _ ‚Üí target:
-- (1) target is a fixed point
fixed-target : ‚ąÄ target ‚Üí Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) target
fixed-target target = refl

-- (2) unique fixed point
unique-fixed :
  ‚ąÄ target x y ‚Üí
  Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) x ‚Üí
  Fixed (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) y ‚Üí
  x ‚Č° y
unique-fixed target x y fx fy = trans (sym fx) fy

-- (3) convergence in 1 step
converges-1 :
  ‚ąÄ target m ‚Üí iterate (Kernel.K (projectTo target)) 1 m ‚Č° target
converges-1 target m = refl
module DASHI.Geometry.EnergyAdditivityProof where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_; refl; cong; trans)
open import Data.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)

record Additive {‚Ąď} : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    Carrier : Set ‚Ąď
    _+_     : Carrier ‚Üí Carrier ‚Üí Carrier
    0#      : Carrier
    -_      : Carrier ‚Üí Carrier

open Additive public

record ScalarField {‚Ąď} : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    Scalar : Set ‚Ąď
    _+s_ _*s_ : Scalar ‚Üí Scalar ‚Üí Scalar
    0s 1s : Scalar
    -s_ : Scalar ‚Üí Scalar

open ScalarField public

record InnerProductSpace {‚Ąď} (A : Additive {‚Ąď}) (F : ScalarField {‚Ąď}) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  open Additive A
  open ScalarField F
  field
    ‚ü™_,_‚üę   : Carrier ‚Üí Carrier ‚Üí Scalar
    ip-sym  : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí ‚ü™ x , y ‚üę ‚Č° ‚ü™ y , x ‚üę
    ip-addL : ‚ąÄ x y z ‚Üí ‚ü™ x + y , z ‚üę ‚Č° ‚ü™ x , z ‚üę +s ‚ü™ y , z ‚üę
    ip-addR : ‚ąÄ x y z ‚Üí ‚ü™ x , y + z ‚üę ‚Č° ‚ü™ x , y ‚üę +s ‚ü™ x , z ‚üę
    ip-negL : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí ‚ü™ - x , y ‚üę ‚Č° -s ‚ü™ x , y ‚üę
    E       : Carrier ‚Üí Scalar
    E-def   : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí E x ‚Č° ‚ü™ x , x ‚üę

open InnerProductSpace public

Orth : ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {A : Additive {‚Ąď}} {F : ScalarField {‚Ąď}}
       (V : InnerProductSpace A F) ‚Üí
       Carrier A ‚Üí Carrier A ‚Üí Set ‚Ąď
Orth {A = A} {F = F} V x y = ‚ü™_,_‚üę V x y ‚Č° 0s F

record Two {‚Ąď} (F : ScalarField {‚Ąď}) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  open ScalarField F
  field
    two : Scalar
    two-def : two ‚Č° (1s +s 1s)

open Two public

EnergyAdditivityProof :
  ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď}
  {A : Additive {‚Ąď}} {F : ScalarField {‚Ąď}}
  (V : InnerProductSpace A F) (T : Two F) ‚Üí
  (‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí Orth V x y ‚Üí ‚ü™_,_‚üę V x y ‚Č° 0s F) ‚Üí
  ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí Orth V x y ‚Üí E V ( _+_ A x y ) ‚Č° ( _+s_ F (E V x) (E V y) )
EnergyAdditivityProof {A = A} {F = F} V T _ x y orth =
  let open Additive A
      open ScalarField F
      open InnerProductSpace V
  in
  trans (E-def (x + y))

module DASHI.Geometry.ContractiveDemo where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Relation.Nullary      using (¬¨_; Dec; yes; no)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym; trans; cong)
-- Removed Reasoning imports as they are missing in stdlib.
open import Data.Nat              using (_<_; z‚Č§n; s‚Č§s; _‚Čü_; _‚Č§_; _‚äĒ_)
open import Data.Empty            using (‚ä•-elim)

open import Ultrametric
open import Contraction

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Discrete ultrametric on Nat: d x y = 0 if x=y else 1
------------------------------------------------------------------------

dNat : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat
dNat x y with x ‚Čü y
... | yes _ = 0
... | no  _ = 1

dNat-refl0 : ‚ąÄ t ‚Üí dNat t t ‚Č° 0
dNat-refl0 t with t ‚Čü t
... | yes _ = refl
... | no  n = ‚ä•-elim (n refl)

id-zeroNat : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí dNat x x ‚Č° 0
id-zeroNat x with x ‚Čü x
... | yes _ = refl
... | no  n = ‚ä•-elim (n refl)

symNat : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí dNat x y ‚Č° dNat y x
symNat x y with x ‚Čü y | y ‚Čü x
... | yes xy | yes yx = refl
... | no  xy | no  yx = refl
... | yes xy | no  yx = ‚ä•-elim (yx (sym xy))
... | no  xy | yes yx = ‚ä•-elim (xy (sym yx))

-- ultratriangle: d x z ‚Č§ max (d x y) (d y z)
-- for discrete metric this holds by case split
ultraNat : ‚ąÄ x y z ‚Üí dNat x z ‚Č§ (dNat x y ‚äĒ dNat y z)
ultraNat x y z with x ‚Čü z
... | yes _ = z‚Č§n
... | no x‚ČĘz with x ‚Čü y | y ‚Čü z
...   | yes xy | yes yz = ‚ä•-elim (x‚ČĘz (trans xy yz))
...   | no  _  | yes yz = s‚Č§s z‚Č§n
...   | yes xy | no  _  = s‚Č§s z‚Č§n
...   | no  _  | no  _  = s‚Č§s z‚Č§n

UNat : Ultrametric Nat
UNat = record
  { d             = dNat
  ; id-zero       = id-zeroNat
  ; symmetric     = symNat
  ; ultratriangle = ultraNat
  }

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A projection operator: K projects everything to a fixed target t
------------------------------------------------------------------------

Kproj : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat
Kproj t _ = t

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Distinctness helper
------------------------------------------------------------------------

dNat-x‚ČĘy=1 : ‚ąÄ {x y} ‚Üí x ‚ČĘ y ‚Üí dNat x y ‚Č° 1
dNat-x‚ČĘy=1 {x} {y} x‚ČĘy with x ‚Čü y
... | yes eq = ‚ä•-elim (x‚ČĘy eq)
... | no _ = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Strict contraction on distinct points (Contractive‚ČĘ style)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  contractive‚ČĘ-proj : ‚ąÄ t ‚Üí (‚ąÄ {x y} ‚Üí x ‚ČĘ y ‚Üí dNat (Kproj t x) (Kproj t y) < dNat x y)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Fixed point uniqueness for projection
------------------------------------------------------------------------

Fixed : (Nat ‚Üí Nat) ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Set
Fixed K a = K a ‚Č° a

uniqueFixedProj :
  ‚ąÄ t x y ‚Üí
  Fixed (Kproj t) x ‚Üí
  Fixed (Kproj t) y ‚Üí
  x ‚Č° y
uniqueFixedProj t x y fx fy =
  trans (sym fx) fy
module DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚Č§_; _<_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contraction using (_‚ČĘ_; Contractive‚ČĘ)

_‚ąė_ : ‚ąÄ {A B C : Set} ‚Üí (B ‚Üí C) ‚Üí (A ‚Üí B) ‚Üí A ‚Üí C
(f ‚ąė g) x = f (g x)

infixr 9 _‚ąė_
record NonExpansive {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) (f : S ‚Üí S) : Set‚āĀ where
  open UMetric.Ultrametric U
  field
    nonexp : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí d (f x) (f y) ‚Č§ d x y

record DistinctPreserving {S : Set} (g : S ‚Üí S) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    preserves‚ČĘ : ‚ąÄ {x y} ‚Üí x ‚ČĘ y ‚Üí g x ‚ČĘ g y

record OrderLaws : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    le-trans   : ‚ąÄ {a b c : Nat} ‚Üí a ‚Č§ b ‚Üí b ‚Č§ c ‚Üí a ‚Č§ c
    le-<-trans : ‚ąÄ {a b c : Nat} ‚Üí a ‚Č§ b ‚Üí b < c ‚Üí a < c
    <-le-trans : ‚ąÄ {a b c : Nat} ‚Üí a < b ‚Üí b ‚Č§ c ‚Üí a < c

-- If f and g are nonexpansive and h is strictly contractive, then f ‚ąė h ‚ąė g is strictly contractive.
composeStrict :
  ‚ąÄ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
    (f g h : S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí
  OrderLaws ‚Üí
  NonExpansive U f ‚Üí
  NonExpansive U g ‚Üí
  DistinctPreserving g ‚Üí
  Contraction.Contractive‚ČĘ U h ‚Üí
  Contraction.Contractive‚ČĘ U (f ‚ąė (h ‚ąė g))
composeStrict U f g h laws neF neG dpG sh =
  record
    { contraction‚ČĘ = őĽ {x} {y} x‚ČĘy ‚Üí
        let open UMetric.Ultrametric U
            open Contraction.Contractive‚ČĘ sh
            open OrderLaws laws
            step1 = NonExpansive.nonexp neF (h (g x)) (h (g y))
            step2 = contraction‚ČĘ {x = g x} {y = g y} (DistinctPreserving.preserves‚ČĘ dpG x‚ČĘy)
            step3 = NonExpansive.nonexp neG x y
        in
        <-le-trans (le-<-trans step1 step2) step3
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.Isotropy where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric

record Group (G : Set) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    _‚ąô_  : G ‚Üí G ‚Üí G
    e    : G
    inv  : G ‚Üí G
    assoc : ‚ąÄ a b c ‚Üí (a ‚ąô b) ‚ąô c ‚Č° a ‚ąô (b ‚ąô c)
    idL   : ‚ąÄ a ‚Üí e ‚ąô a ‚Č° a
    invL  : ‚ąÄ a ‚Üí (inv a) ‚ąô a ‚Č° e

record Isotropy
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (T : S ‚Üí S)
       : Set‚āĀ where

  open UMetric.Ultrametric U
  field
    G      : Set
    group  : Group G
    act    : G ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
    preservesMetric :
      ‚ąÄ g x y ‚Üí d (act g x) (act g y) ‚Č° d x y
    commutesWithT :
      ‚ąÄ g x ‚Üí T (act g x) ‚Č° act g (T x)

-- Trivial isotropy: one element group acting by identity.
trivialIsotropy :
  ‚ąÄ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) (T : S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí
  Isotropy U T
trivialIsotropy U T =
  record
    { G = ‚ä§
    ; group = record
        { _‚ąô_ = őĽ _ _ ‚Üí tt
        ; e = tt
        ; inv = őĽ _ ‚Üí tt
        ; assoc = őĽ _ _ _ ‚Üí refl
        ; idL = őĽ _ ‚Üí refl
        ; invL = őĽ _ ‚Üí refl
        }
    ; act = őĽ _ x ‚Üí x
    ; preservesMetric = őĽ _ _ _ ‚Üí refl
    ; commutesWithT = őĽ _ _ ‚Üí refl
    }

  : Set (suc (‚Ąďx ‚äĒ ‚Ąďe)) where

    D : X ‚Üí X
    T : X ‚Üí X
    _‚Č§_ : E ‚Üí E ‚Üí Set ‚Ąďe
    energy : X ‚Üí E
    collapse : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí _‚Č§_ (energy (D (T x))) (energy (D x))

open DefectCollapse public

module DASHI.Geometry.QuadraticEmergence where

record Parallelogram {‚Ąď} (X : Set ‚Ąď) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    _+_ : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí X
    _-_ : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí X
    Q : X ‚Üí ‚Ąö
    law :
      ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí
        (Q (x + y) +‚Ąö Q (x - y))
          ‚Č°
        ((two‚Ąö *‚Ąö Q x) +‚Ąö (two‚Ąö *‚Ąö Q y))

record QuadraticStructure {‚Ąď} (X : Set ‚Ąď) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where

    _+_ : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí X
    _-_ : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí X
    Q : X ‚Üí ‚Ąö
    ‚ü™_,_‚üę : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí ‚Ąö
    bilinear : Set
    symmetric : Set
    norm-def : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí Q x ‚Č° ‚ü™ x , x ‚üę

    ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {X : Set ‚Ąď} ‚Üí
    Parallelogram X ‚Üí
    ő£ (QuadraticStructure X) (őĽ _ ‚Üí ‚ä§)
module DASHI.Geometry.COL where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes
open import DASHI.Core.LensKernel

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Contraction‚ÄďObstruction‚ÄďLift (COL)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record COL (S : Nat -> Set) : Set1 where
  field
    E    : forall n -> S n -> Nat
    K    : forall n -> S n -> S n
    Obs  : forall n -> S n -> Bool
    lift : forall n -> S n -> S (suc n)

    -- Contraction inside level n: energy does not increase.
    contract : (n : Nat) (x : S n) -> E n (K n x) ‚Č§ E n x

    -- Obstruction is stable under K: if you are obstructed, stepping doesn't ‚Äúsolve‚ÄĚ it magically.
    obs-stable : (n : Nat) (x : S n) -> Obs n x ‚Č° true -> Obs n (K n x) ‚Č° true

    -- Lift is witness-respecting: the old state is embedded, not destroyed.
    embed-ok : (n : Nat) (x : S n) -> ‚ä§

open COL public

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Derived theorem hooks (the ‚Äúschema theorems‚ÄĚ)

-- If not obstructed, repeated contraction gives monotone energy sequence.
iterate : forall {A : Set} -> (A -> A) -> Nat -> A -> A
iterate f zero    x = x
iterate f (suc k) x = iterate f k (f x)

E-monotone-iter :
  forall {S : Nat -> Set} (C : COL S) ->
  (n : Nat) (k : Nat) (x : S n) ->
  COL.E C n (iterate (COL.K C n) k x) ‚Č§ COL.E C n x
E-monotone-iter C n zero    x = ‚Č§-refl
E-monotone-iter C n (suc k) x =
  ‚Č§-trans
    (E-monotone-iter C n k (COL.K C n x))
    (COL.contract C n x)
module DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropyInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; suc)
open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false; if_then_else_; _xor_)
open import Data.Bool.Properties as BoolP
open import DASHI.Geometry.Isotropy as Iso
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropy as RIS
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.RealOperators as RO
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym)

-- Two-element group acting by invVec.
boolGroup : Iso.Group Bool
boolGroup =
  record
    { _‚ąô_ = _xor_
    ; e = false
    ; inv = őĽ a ‚Üí a
    ; assoc = BoolP.xor-assoc
    ; idL = BoolP.xor-identityň°
    ; invL = BoolP.xor-same
    }

act : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Bool ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n
act {n} b x = if b then RTC.invVec x else x

preservesMetric :
  ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí (g : Bool) ‚Üí (x y : RTC.Carrier n) ‚Üí
  UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (act g x) (act g y)
    ‚Č° UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) x y
preservesMetric {n} false x y = refl
preservesMetric {n} true x y = FAM.dNatFine-inv x y

commutesWithT :
  ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí (g : Bool) ‚Üí (x : RTC.Carrier n) ‚Üí
  RO.CŠĶ£ (RO.PŠĶ£ (RO.RŠĶ£ (act g x))) ‚Č° act g (RO.CŠĶ£ (RO.PŠĶ£ (RO.RŠĶ£ x)))
commutesWithT {n} false x = refl
commutesWithT {n} true x = sym (RO.invVec-PŠĶ£ x)

realIsotropyInstance :
  ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí
  RIS.RealIsotropy (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (őĽ x ‚Üí RO.CŠĶ£ (RO.PŠĶ£ (RO.RŠĶ£ x)))
realIsotropyInstance {n} =
  record
    { iso =
        record
          { G = Bool
          ; group = boolGroup
          ; act = act
          ; preservesMetric = preservesMetric
          ; commutesWithT = commutesWithT
          }
    ; coneInvariant = Bool
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropyInstanceShift where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false; if_then_else_; _xor_)

open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym; trans; cong)

open import DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropy as RIS

open import DASHI.Physics.RealOperatorStackShift as ROSS

open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseInvolution as TCI
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import Ultrametric as UMetric

-- Two-element group acting by invVec.
boolGroup : Iso.Group Bool
boolGroup =
  record
    { _‚ąô_ = _xor_
    ; e = false
    ; inv = őĽ a ‚Üí a
    ; assoc = BoolP.xor-assoc
    ; idL = BoolP.xor-identityň°
    ; invL = BoolP.xor-same
    }

act : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Bool ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n
act {n} b x = if b then RTC.invVec x else x

preservesMetric :
  ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí (g : Bool) ‚Üí (x y : RTC.Carrier n) ‚Üí
  UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (act g x) (act g y)
    ‚Č° UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) x y
preservesMetric {n} false x y = refl
preservesMetric {n} true x y = FAM.dNatFine-inv x y

commutesWithT :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí (g : Bool) ‚Üí (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} (act g x)))
    ‚Č° act g (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
commutesWithT {m} {k} false x = refl
commutesWithT {m} {k} true x =
  let
    step1 : ROSS.R {m} {k} (RTC.invVec x) ‚Č° RTC.invVec (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)
    step1 = sym (TCI.invVec-RŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)
    step2 : ROSS.P {m} {k} (RTC.invVec (ROSS.R {m} {k} x))
            ‚Č° RTC.invVec (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x))
    step2 = sym (TCI.invVec-PŠĶ£ {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x))
    step3 : ROSS.C {m} {k} (RTC.invVec (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
            ‚Č° RTC.invVec (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
    step3 = sym (CM.CŠĶ£-invVec {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
  in
  trans
    (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} v)) step1)
    (trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí ROSS.C {m} {k} v) step2) step3)

realIsotropyInstanceShift :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  RIS.RealIsotropy (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
    (őĽ x ‚Üí ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
realIsotropyInstanceShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { iso =
        record
          { G = Bool
          ; group = boolGroup
          ; act = act
          ; preservesMetric = preservesMetric
          ; commutesWithT = commutesWithT {m} {k}
          }
    ; coneInvariant = Bool
    }
