module DASHI.Geometry.ProjectionContractionOrthogonalityTests where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma
open import Data.Product public using (_√ó_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Minimal algebra: additive group structure (abstract)
-- (You can replace these postulates with your concrete state carrier.)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  S   : Set
  _S+_ : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
  _S-_ : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
  0#  : S

infixl 6 _S+_ _S-_

postulate
  -- Group-ish laws you‚Äôll need for ‚Äúdetail = x - P x‚ÄĚ reasoning
  +-assoc : ‚ąÄ x y z ‚Üí (x S+ y) S+ z ‚Č° x S+ (y S+ z)
  +-id ≥   : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí x S+ 0# ‚Č° x
  +-idň°   : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí 0# S+ x ‚Č° x
  +-inv ≥  : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí x S- x ‚Č° 0#

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Metric / norm interface (keep abstract; later bind to your induced norm)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  dist : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set  -- you may replace with ‚ĄĚ or ‚Ąö; kept abstract here

-- A ‚Äúnorm‚ÄĚ is distance to 0. (You can swap this for your actual norm.)
postulate
  ‚ą•_‚ą• : S ‚Üí Set
  ‚ą•x‚ą•-def : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí ‚ą• x ‚ą• ‚Č° dist x 0#

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Recognisable lift decomposition (your ‚Äútelescoping identity‚ÄĚ)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record RecognisableLift (P : S ‚Üí S) : Set where
  field
    -- every x decomposes uniquely into coarse + detail:
    coarse   : S ‚Üí S
    detail   : S ‚Üí S
    split    : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí x ‚Č° coarse x S+ detail x

    -- recognisable uniqueness: if x = c+d = c'+d' with both c,c' fixed by P
    -- and both d,d' in the fiber kernel, then equal (abstracted)
    uniq :
      ‚ąÄ x c d c' d' ‚Üí
      x ‚Č° c S+ d ‚Üí
      x ‚Č° c' S+ d' ‚Üí
      P c ‚Č° c ‚Üí
      P c' ‚Č° c' ‚Üí
      P d ‚Č° 0# ‚Üí
      P d' ‚Č° 0# ‚Üí
      (c ‚Č° c') √ó (d ‚Č° d')

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Non-expansive idempotent projection axioms
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record NonExpansiveProjection (P : S ‚Üí S) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    idem  : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí P (P x) ‚Č° P x
    nonexp : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí dist (P x) (P y) ‚Č° dist x y
    -- (If you want ‚Č§ instead of ‚Č°, change dist codomain to ‚Ąö/‚ĄĚ and use ‚Č§.)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Orthogonality: ‚Äúno double counting‚ÄĚ in the induced quadratic energy
--
-- This is the *test* you want Agda to force:
--   from RecognisableLift + NonExpansiveProjection (+ stability axiom),
--   derive Pythagorean split for a quadratic norm and orthogonality.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record OrthogonalSplit (P : S ‚Üí S) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    ‚üā-pred : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set          -- ‚Äúorthogonal‚ÄĚ predicate (abstract)
    pythag :
      ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí
      let c = P x
          d = x S- P x
      in  ‚ą• x ‚ą• ‚Č° (‚ą• c ‚ą•) √ó (‚ą• d ‚ą•)   -- placeholder shape; replace with numeric identity
    orth :
      ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí
      let c = P x
          d = x S- P x
      in  ‚üā-pred c d

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The Master Theorem (as a test harness)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  -- Stability premise: the multiscale hierarchy must forbid leakage.
  -- You can replace this with your contractive fixed-point stability lemma.
  StabilityNoLeakage :
    (P : S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí Set

postulate
  MasterTheorem :
    (P : S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí
    RecognisableLift P ‚Üí
    NonExpansiveProjection P ‚Üí
    StabilityNoLeakage P ‚Üí
    OrthogonalSplit P

open import DASHI.Physics.CanonicalizationMinimal as CM
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseInvolution as TCI

open import Ultrametric as UMetric

cong‚āā' :
  ‚ąÄ {A B C : Set} {x‚āĀ x‚āā : A} {y‚āĀ y‚āā : B}
  (f : A ‚Üí B ‚Üí C) ‚Üí x‚āĀ ‚Č° x‚āā ‚Üí y‚āĀ ‚Č° y‚āā ‚Üí f x‚āĀ y‚āĀ ‚Č° f x‚āā y‚āā
cong‚āā' f refl refl = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Two-element group acting by tail inversion

boolGroup : Iso.Group Bool
boolGroup =
  record
    { _‚ąô_ = _xor_
    ; e = false
    ; inv = őĽ a ‚Üí a
    ; assoc = BoolP.xor-assoc
    ; idL = BoolP.xor-identityň°
    ; invL = BoolP.xor-same
    }

-- Apply invVec to tail only

tailInv : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)
tailInv {m} {k} x = TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ RTC.invVec (TCP.tailOf m k x)

tailInv-++ :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  tailInv {m} {k} (c ++ t) ‚Č° c ++ RTC.invVec t
tailInv-++ {m} {k} c t
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c t = refl

coarseOf-tailInv :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.coarseOf m k (tailInv {m} {k} x) ‚Č° TCP.coarseOf m k x
coarseOf-tailInv {m} {k} x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (RTC.invVec t)
  = refl

act : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Bool ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)
act {m} {k} b x = if b then tailInv {m} {k} x else x

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- tailInv is an involution

tailInv-invol : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí tailInv {m} {k} (tailInv {m} {k} x) ‚Č° x
tailInv-invol {m} {k} x =
  let
    c = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    t = TCP.tailOf m k x
    p : x ‚Č° c ++ t
    p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
  in
  trans
    (tailInv-++ c (RTC.invVec t))
    (trans
      (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí c ++ v) (RTC.invVec-invol t))
      (sym p))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Metric invariance for tailInv

preservesMetric :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí (g : Bool) ‚Üí (x y : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (act {m} {k} g x) (act {m} {k} g y)
    ‚Č° UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y
preservesMetric {m} {k} false x y = refl
preservesMetric {m} {k} true x y =
  let
    c  = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    t  = TCP.tailOf m k x
    c' = TCP.coarseOf m k y
    t' = TCP.tailOf m k y
    p : x ‚Č° c ++ t
    p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
    q : y ‚Č° c' ++ t'
    q = sym (TCP.merge-split m k y)
    le1 : FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t') ‚Č§ FAM.dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
    le1 = FAM.dNatFine-++-map‚Č§-tail c c' t t' inv
    le2 : FAM.dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t') ‚Č§ FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t')
    le2 =
      let
        le2' : FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec (RTC.invVec t))
                            (c' ++ RTC.invVec (RTC.invVec t'))
               ‚Č§ FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t')
        le2' = FAM.dNatFine-++-map‚Č§-tail c c' (RTC.invVec t) (RTC.invVec t') inv
        r1 : c ++ RTC.invVec (RTC.invVec t) ‚Č° c ++ t
        r1 = cong (őĽ v ‚Üí c ++ v) (RTC.invVec-invol t)
        r2 : c' ++ RTC.invVec (RTC.invVec t') ‚Č° c' ++ t'
        r2 = cong (őĽ v ‚Üí c' ++ v) (RTC.invVec-invol t')
      in
      NatP.‚Č§-trans
        (NatP.‚Č§-reflexive (sym (cong‚āā' FAM.dNatFine r1 r2)))
        le2'
    le1' : FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t') ‚Č§ FAM.dNatFine x y
    le1' = subst‚āā (őĽ a b ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t') ‚Č§ FAM.dNatFine a b)
                  (sym p) (sym q) le1
    le2' : FAM.dNatFine x y ‚Č§ FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t')
    le2' = subst‚āā (őĽ a b ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine a b ‚Č§ FAM.dNatFine (c ++ RTC.invVec t) (c' ++ RTC.invVec t'))
                  (sym p) (sym q) le2
  in
  NatP.‚Č§-antisym le1' le2'

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Commutation with the shift stack

commutesWithT :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí (g : Bool) ‚Üí (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} (act {m} {k} g x)))
    ‚Č° act {m} {k} g (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
commutesWithT {m} {k} false x = refl
commutesWithT {m} {k} true x =
  let
    c = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    t = TCP.tailOf m k x
    r : act {m} {k} true x ‚Č° c ++ RTC.invVec t
    r = refl
    stepR : TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} (c ++ RTC.invVec t) ‚Č° c ++ TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t)
    stepR = TCP.RŠĶ£-++ m k c (RTC.invVec t)
    stepP : TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} (c ++ TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t)) ‚Č° c ++ TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t))
    stepP = TCP.PŠĶ£-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t))
    stepRP : TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} (TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} (c ++ RTC.invVec t)) ‚Č° c ++ TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t))
    stepRP = trans (cong (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k}) stepR) stepP
    stepC : ROSS.C {m} {k} (c ++ TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t)))
            ‚Č° CM.canonVec c ++ TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t))
    stepC = CM.CŠĶ£-++ c (TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t)))
    t' = TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail t)
    p : x ‚Č° c ++ t
    p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
    stepT : ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)) ‚Č° CM.canonVec c ++ t'
    stepT =
      let
        r : TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} x ‚Č° c ++ TCP.shiftTail t
        r = trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.RŠĶ£-++ m k c t)
        pr : TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} (TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° c ++ TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail t)
        pr = trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} v) r) (TCP.PŠĶ£-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t))
      in
      trans
        (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí ROSS.C {m} {k} v) pr)
        (CM.CŠĶ£-++ c t')
    stepAct : act {m} {k} true (ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x))) ‚Č° CM.canonVec c ++ RTC.invVec t'
    stepAct =
      trans
        (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí tailInv {m} {k} v) stepT)
        (tailInv-++ (CM.canonVec c) t')
    stepInv : RTC.invVec (TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail t)) ‚Č° TCP.projTail (TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t))
    stepInv =
      trans
        (TCI.invVec-projTail (TCP.shiftTail t))
        (cong TCP.projTail (TCI.invVec-shiftTail t))
  in
  trans
    (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} v))) r)
    (trans
      (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí ROSS.C {m} {k} v) stepRP)
      (trans
        stepC
        (trans
          (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí CM.canonVec c ++ v) (sym stepInv))
          (sym stepAct))))

realIsotropyInstanceTailInv :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  RIS.RealIsotropy (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
    (őĽ x ‚Üí ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
realIsotropyInstanceTailInv {m} {k} =
  record
    { iso =
        record
          { G = Bool
          ; group = boolGroup
          ; act = act {m} {k}
          ; preservesMetric = preservesMetric {m} {k}
          ; commutesWithT = commutesWithT {m} {k}
          }
    ; coneInvariant = Bool
    }

module DASHI.Geometry.BanachFixedPointNat where

-- For ‚Ąē-valued ultrametrics, a StrictContraction already packages the fixed point.
banachFromStrict :
  ‚ąÄ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) (T : S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí
  Contr.StrictContraction U T ‚Üí BFP.BanachFixedPoint U T
banachFromStrict U T sc =
  record
    { fp = Contr.StrictContraction.fp sc
    ; fixes = Contr.StrictContraction.fixed sc
    ; unique = Contr.StrictContraction.unique sc
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeedInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeed as RFS
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Physics.RealOperators as RO
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import Data.Nat using (_‚Č§_)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

-- Fixed locality radius (nontrivial, but simple).
radius : Nat
radius = suc zero

local : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí Set
local {n} x y = UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) x y ‚Č§ radius

preservesLocality :
  ‚ąÄ {n} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  local x y ‚Üí
  local (RO.CŠĶ£ (RO.PŠĶ£ (RO.RŠĶ£ x))) (RO.CŠĶ£ (RO.PŠĶ£ (RO.RŠĶ£ y)))
preservesLocality {n} x y h =
  let
    open UMetric.Ultrametric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n})
    step1 : d (RO.PŠĶ£ (RO.RŠĶ£ x)) (RO.PŠĶ£ (RO.RŠĶ£ y)) ‚Č§ d (RO.RŠĶ£ x) (RO.RŠĶ£ y)
    step1 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (RO.nonexpPŠĶ£ {n}) (RO.RŠĶ£ x) (RO.RŠĶ£ y)
    step2 : d (RO.RŠĶ£ x) (RO.RŠĶ£ y) ‚Č§ d x y
    step2 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (RO.nonexpRŠĶ£ {n}) x y
    step3 : d (RO.CŠĶ£ (RO.PŠĶ£ (RO.RŠĶ£ x))) (RO.CŠĶ£ (RO.PŠĶ£ (RO.RŠĶ£ y)))
            ‚Č§ d (RO.PŠĶ£ (RO.RŠĶ£ x)) (RO.PŠĶ£ (RO.RŠĶ£ y))
    step3 = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp (RO.nonexpCŠĶ£ {n}) (RO.PŠĶ£ (RO.RŠĶ£ x)) (RO.PŠĶ£ (RO.RŠĶ£ y))
  in
  NatP.‚Č§-trans (NatP.‚Č§-trans step3 step1) (NatP.‚Č§-trans step2 h)

realFiniteSpeedInstance :
  ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí
  RFS.RealFiniteSpeed (őĽ x ‚Üí RO.CŠĶ£ (RO.PŠĶ£ (RO.RŠĶ£ x)))
realFiniteSpeedInstance {n} =
  record
    { local = local {n}
    ; preservesLocality = preservesLocality {n}
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.RGFlowContract where

open import Contraction

postulate
  CouplingState : Set
  U : Ultrametric CouplingState
  step : CouplingState ‚Üí CouplingState
  mdl : CouplingState ‚Üí Nat

-- Two closure options:
-- A) Contraction (metric closure)
postulate stepContractive : Contractive U step

-- B) Lyapunov descent (MDL closure)
postulate mdlMonotone : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí mdl (step s) ‚Č§ mdl s
module DASHI.Geometry.ProjectionDefect where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äĒ_; suc; zero)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_; refl; cong)
open import Data.Product using (ő£; _,_)
open import Data.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)

record Additive (‚Ąď : Level) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    Carrier : Set ‚Ąď
    _+_     : Carrier ‚Üí Carrier ‚Üí Carrier
    0#      : Carrier
    -_      : Carrier ‚Üí Carrier

open Additive public

record ProjectionDefect {‚Ąď} (A : Additive ‚Ąď) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  open Additive A
  field
    P     : Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí Additive.Carrier A
    D     : Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí Additive.Carrier A
    D-def : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí D x ‚Č° Additive._+_ A x (Additive.-_ A (P x))

    P-idem : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí P (P x) ‚Č° P x

    Orth : Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí Set ‚Ąď
    Orth-PD : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí Orth (P x) (D x)

open ProjectionDefect public
module DASHI.Geometry.MQContractive where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)

    T     : MaskedQuadratic.V MQ ‚Üí MaskedQuadratic.V MQ
    lambda : ‚Ąö
    lambda<1   : lambda < 1‚Ąö
    contract : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí MaskedQuadratic.Q MQ (T x) ‚Č§ (lambda *‚Ąö lambda) *‚Ąö MaskedQuadratic.Q MQ x

module DASHI.Geometry.OrthogonalityFromPolarization where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äĒ_; suc; zero)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_)

open import DASHI.Geometry.ProjectionDefect
open import DASHI.Geometry.QuadraticForm
open import DASHI.Energy.Energy
open import DASHI.Energy.ClosestPoint

-- Polarization interface: once Q is quadratic, define an inner product
-- and record the polarization identity as a seam.
record Polarization {‚Ąďv ‚Ąďs}
  (A : Additive ‚Ąďv) (F : ScalarField ‚Ąďs)
  : Set (suc (‚Ąďv ‚äĒ ‚Ąďs)) where
  field
    Q : Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí ScalarField.S F
    ‚ü™_,_‚üę : Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí ScalarField.S F
    two : ScalarField.S F
    two-def : two ‚Č° (ScalarField._+s_ F (ScalarField.1s F) (ScalarField.1s F))
    polarization :
      ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí
        Q (Additive._+_ A x y) ‚Č°
        ScalarField._+s_ F
          (ScalarField._+s_ F (Q x) (Q y))
          (ScalarField._*s_ F two (‚ü™ x , y ‚üę))

open Polarization public

-- Orthogonality corollary: once closest-point is established and
-- the polarization identity is available, orthogonality becomes a target.
record OrthogonalityFromPolarization {‚Ąďv ‚Ąďs}
  {A : Additive ‚Ąďv} {F : ScalarField ‚Ąďs}
  {P : Preorder {‚Ąďs}}
  (ES : EnergySpace (Additive.Carrier A) P)
  (Pj : Projection (Additive.Carrier A))
  (Pol : Polarization A F)
  (CP : ClosestPoint ES Pj)
  : Set (suc (‚Ąďv ‚äĒ ‚Ąďs)) where
  field
    Orth : Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí Additive.Carrier A ‚Üí Set ‚Ąďs
    Orth-def : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí Orth x y ‚Č°
      (Polarization.‚ü™_,_‚üę Pol x y ‚Č° ScalarField.0s F)
    orthPD : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí
      Orth (Projection.P Pj x)
           (Additive._+_ A x (Additive.-_ A (Projection.P Pj x)))

open OrthogonalityFromPolarization public
module DASHI.Geometry.ProjectionContractiveConstant where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Empty using (‚ä•; ‚ä•-elim)

open import Ultrametric as UMetric

_‚ČĘ_ : {A : Set} ‚Üí A ‚Üí A ‚Üí Set
_‚ČĘ_ {A} x y = (x ‚Č° y) ‚Üí ‚ä•

record DiscreteUltrametric {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) : Set‚āĀ where
  open UMetric.Ultrametric U public
  field
    nonzero-on-distinct : ‚ąÄ {x y} ‚Üí x ‚ČĘ y ‚Üí d x y ‚ČĘ zero

Kconst : ‚ąÄ {S : Set} ‚Üí S ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
Kconst t _ = t

record Contractive‚ČĘ
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (K : S ‚Üí S)
       : Set where
  open UMetric.Ultrametric U public
  field
    collapses-on-distinct : ‚ąÄ {x y} ‚Üí x ‚ČĘ y ‚Üí d (K x) (K y) ‚Č° zero
    original-nonzero : ‚ąÄ {x y} ‚Üí x ‚ČĘ y ‚Üí d x y ‚ČĘ zero

const-proj-contractive‚ČĘ :
  ‚ąÄ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
  ‚Üí DiscreteUltrametric U
  ‚Üí (t : S)
  ‚Üí Contractive‚ČĘ U (Kconst t)
const-proj-contractive‚ČĘ {S} U DU t =
  let open UMetric.Ultrametric U
      open DiscreteUltrametric DU
  in
  record
    { collapses-on-distinct = őĽ {x} {_} _ ‚Üí
        UMetric.Ultrametric.id-zero U (Kconst t x)
    ; original-nonzero = őĽ {x} {y} x‚ČĘy ‚Üí
        nonzero-on-distinct x‚ČĘy
    }
module DASHI.Geometry.EinsteinFromRGNoLeakage where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)

record RGGeometryData : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    M : Set
    Point : Set
    Tensor2 : Set
    ‚Ąö : Set
    0q : ‚Ąö
    div : Tensor2 ‚Üí Point ‚Üí ‚Ąö
    sym : Tensor2 ‚Üí Set
    G : M ‚Üí Tensor2
    T : M ‚Üí Tensor2
    RGState : Set
    step : RGState ‚Üí RGState
    geom : RGState ‚Üí M
    PŌĄ : Tensor2 ‚Üí Tensor2

open RGGeometryData public

DefectD : (D : RGGeometryData) ‚Üí RGGeometryData.RGState D ‚Üí RGGeometryData.Tensor2 D
DefectD D s = RGGeometryData.PŌĄ D (RGGeometryData.T D (RGGeometryData.geom D (RGGeometryData.step D s)))

record GR_NoLeakage (D : RGGeometryData) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    bianchi :
      ‚ąÄ s x ‚Üí
        RGGeometryData.div D (RGGeometryData.G D (RGGeometryData.geom D s)) x ‚Č° RGGeometryData.0q D
    conserve :
      ‚ąÄ s x ‚Üí
        RGGeometryData.div D (RGGeometryData.T D (RGGeometryData.geom D s)) x ‚Č° RGGeometryData.0q D
    defect-law :
      ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí
        RGGeometryData.G D (RGGeometryData.geom D s) ‚Č° DefectD D s
    symG :
      ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí
        RGGeometryData.sym D (RGGeometryData.G D (RGGeometryData.geom D s))
    symT :
      ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí
        RGGeometryData.sym D (RGGeometryData.T D (RGGeometryData.geom D s))

open GR_NoLeakage public

record EinsteinConsequences {D} (A : GR_NoLeakage D) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    divergenceFree :
      ‚ąÄ s x ‚Üí
        RGGeometryData.div D (RGGeometryData.G D (RGGeometryData.geom D s)) x ‚Č° RGGeometryData.0q D
    conservation :
      ‚ąÄ s x ‚Üí
        RGGeometryData.div D (RGGeometryData.T D (RGGeometryData.geom D s)) x ‚Č° RGGeometryData.0q D
    einsteinEq :
      ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí
        RGGeometryData.G D (RGGeometryData.geom D s) ‚Č° DefectD D s

EinsteinFromRG :
  ‚ąÄ {D} (A : GR_NoLeakage D) ‚Üí
  EinsteinConsequences A
EinsteinFromRG A =
  record
    { divergenceFree = bianchi A
    ; conservation = conserve A
    ; einsteinEq = defect-law A
    }

module DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.UVFinitenessHolographyTests where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma using (ő£; _,_)
open import Data.Nat using (_*_; _‚Č§_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract ‚Äúregion size‚ÄĚ and counting (bound supplied by the user)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  L : Set                  -- linear size parameter
  vol area : L -> Nat      -- discrete counts
  dimH : L -> Nat          -- effective Hilbert dimension / mode count
  eta  : Nat               -- holographic proportionality constant

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Holographic area bound: dimH(L) ‚Č§ ő∑ * area(L)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

AreaBound : Set
AreaBound = ‚ąÄ (l : L) -> dimH l ‚Č§ (eta * area l)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- UV finiteness: bounded dim ‚áí no infinite UV tower
------------------------------------------------------------------------

UVFinitenessTheorem :
  (areaBound : AreaBound) ‚Üí
  UVFinite (record
    { L = L
    ; dimH = dimH
    ; bound = őĽ l ‚Üí eta * area l
    ; dimH‚Č§bound = areaBound
    })
UVFinitenessTheorem areaBound =
  let bounded = record
        { L = L
        ; dimH = dimH
        ; bound = őĽ l ‚Üí eta * area l
        ; dimH‚Č§bound = areaBound
        }
  in uvFiniteness bounded
module DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.NoGlobalAttractor where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes

-- Iteration
iterate : ‚ąÄ {S : Set} ‚Üí (S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
iterate f zero    x = x
iterate f (suc n) x = iterate f n (f x)

-- ‚ÄúEventually constant‚ÄĚ orbit at a.
EventuallyConst : ‚ąÄ {S : Set} ‚Üí (S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set
EventuallyConst f x a = ő£ Nat (őĽ N ‚Üí ‚ąÄ n ‚Üí iterate f (N + n) x ‚Č° a)

-- Global attractor = same a for all x.
GlobalAttractor : ‚ąÄ {S : Set} ‚Üí (S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí Set
GlobalAttractor f = ő£ _ (őĽ a ‚Üí ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí EventuallyConst f x a)

-- The useful theorem: invertible + nontrivial ‚áí no global attractor.
-- (In a finite/discrete world, invertible dynamics can‚Äôt collapse all orbits to one point unless singleton.)

postulate
  invertible-nontrivial-no-attractor :
    ‚ąÄ {S : Set} {U : S ‚Üí S} ‚Üí
    Invertible U ‚Üí
    (ő£ S (őĽ x ‚Üí ő£ S (őĽ y ‚Üí ¬¨ (x ‚Č° y)))) ‚Üí
    ¬¨ GlobalAttractor U

record Measurement {S : Set} (ő† : S ‚Üí S) : Set where
  field
    proj : Projection ő†
    nontrivial : Nontrivial ő†   -- measurement actually collapses something

  ‚ąÄ {S : Set} {ő† : S ‚Üí S} ‚Üí
  Measurement ő† ‚Üí
  ¬¨ Invertible ő†
measurement-not-invertible {S} {ő†} M invő† =
  let open Measurement M in
  -- If ő† invertible and projection ‚áí ő† = id, contradict nontrivial.
  nontrivial (projection+invertible‚Üíidentity proj invő†)

module DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.SpinFromEvenClifford where

record SpinData : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    SO : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Set
    Cl‚Āį : Set
    Spin : Set
    toSO : Spin ‚Üí SO 3 1
    kernel¬Ī1 : Set
    identitySO : SO 3 1

record SpinDoubleCover (D : SpinData) : Set‚āĀ where
  open SpinData D
  field
    hom : Spin ‚Üí SO 3 1
    kernel : Spin ‚Üí Set
    kernel‚äÜ¬Ī1 : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí hom s ‚Č° identitySO ‚Üí kernel s ‚Üí kernel¬Ī1
    surjective : ‚ąÄ g ‚Üí ő£ Spin (őĽ s ‚Üí hom s ‚Č° g)

-- Building a witness now requires surjectivity/kernel proof data.
spinDoubleCover-witness :
  ‚ąÄ D ‚Üí
  (ker : SpinData.Spin D ‚Üí Set)
  (ker‚äÜ¬Ī1 : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí SpinData.toSO D s ‚Č° SpinData.identitySO D ‚Üí ker s ‚Üí SpinData.kernel¬Ī1 D)
  (surj : ‚ąÄ g ‚Üí ő£ (SpinData.Spin D) (őĽ s ‚Üí SpinData.toSO D s ‚Č° g)) ‚Üí
  SpinDoubleCover D
spinDoubleCover-witness D ker ker‚äÜ¬Ī1 surj =
  record { hom = SpinData.toSO D ; kernel = ker ; kernel‚äÜ¬Ī1 = ker‚äÜ¬Ī1 ; surjective = surj }

SpinIsDoubleCover : ‚ąÄ {D} ‚Üí SpinDoubleCover D ‚Üí Set
SpinIsDoubleCover {D} cover =
  ‚ąÄ g ‚Üí ő£ (SpinData.Spin D) (őĽ s ‚Üí SpinDoubleCover.hom cover s ‚Č° g)

module DASHI.Algebra.OperatorMonoidClosed where

_‚ąė_ : Endo ‚Üí Endo ‚Üí Endo
(f ‚ąė g) s = f (g s)

id : Endo
id s = s

-- The closure generated by a seed operator K (a free monoid in Endo)

  gen-id   : Gen K id
  gen-base : Gen K K
  gen-comp : ‚ąÄ {f g} ‚Üí Gen K f ‚Üí Gen K g ‚Üí Gen K (f ‚ąė g)

-- Now ‚Äúclosure‚ÄĚ is literal:
closed-under-comp :
  ‚ąÄ {K : Endo} {f g : Endo} ‚Üí
  Gen K f ‚Üí Gen K g ‚Üí Gen K (f ‚ąė g)
closed-under-comp = gen-comp

module DASHI.Algebra.ConstraintAlgebraClosureTests where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract operator Lie algebra (commutator bracket)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  Op : Set
  _‚ąė_ : Op ‚Üí Op ‚Üí Op
  _-_ : Op ‚Üí Op ‚Üí Op
  I   : Op

infixl 9 _‚ąė_

_bracket_ : Op ‚Üí Op ‚Üí Op
A bracket B = (A ‚ąė B) - (B ‚ąė A)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Constraints: Hamiltonian + Momentum (vector-index abstracted)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  Idx : Set
  H    : Op
  HŠĶĘ   : Idx ‚Üí Op

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Closure statement: commutators of constraints re-express as constraints
-- (This is the ‚Äúno anomaly‚ÄĚ test: algebra closes in the same family.)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record DiracClosure : Set where
  field
    -- [HŠĶĘ, H‚Īľ] = H_k(...)   (structure functions hidden for now)
    mom-mom :
      ‚ąÄ i j ‚Üí ő£ Idx (őĽ k ‚Üí (HŠĶĘ i bracket HŠĶĘ j) ‚Č° HŠĶĘ k)

    -- [H, HŠĶĘ] = H(...)
    ham-mom :
      ‚ąÄ i ‚Üí (H bracket HŠĶĘ i) ‚Č° H

    -- [H, H] = HŠĶĘ(...)
    ham-ham :
      ő£ Idx (őĽ k ‚Üí (H bracket H) ‚Č° HŠĶĘ k)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Theorem obligation: derive closure from ‚Äúvaluation equivariance‚ÄĚ
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  ValuationEquivariance : Set     -- your ‚Äúdecimation commutes with relabellings‚ÄĚ
  NoLeakageStability    : Set     -- your fixed-point stability condition

postulate
  ConstraintAlgebraTheorem :
    ValuationEquivariance ‚Üí
    NoLeakageStability ‚Üí
    DiracClosure
module DASHI.Algebra.SMConformanceVectors where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Data.Unit using (‚ä§)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)
open import Agda.Builtin.List using (List; []; _‚ą∑_)

-- Abstract state (whatever your physics state representation is)
postulate State : Set

-- Spec and impl: State ‚Üí signature (finite)
postulate
  Sig : Set
  specSig : State ‚Üí Sig
  implSig : State ‚Üí Sig

record Vector : Set where
  constructor vec
  field input : State

Vectors : Set
Vectors = List Vector

ConformsOn : (f g : State ‚Üí Sig) ‚Üí Vectors ‚Üí Set
ConformsOn f g [] = ‚ä§
ConformsOn f g (v ‚ą∑ vs) =
  (f (Vector.input v) ‚Č° g (Vector.input v)) √ó ConformsOn f g vs

-- Closure theorem you actually ship:
postulate vectors : Vectors

postulate
  physics-conformance : ConformsOn implSig specSig vectors
module DASHI.Algebra.PhysicsConformance where

open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List; []; _‚ą∑_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Data.Unit             using (‚ä§; tt)
open import Data.Product          using (_√ó_; _,_)

open import DASHI.Algebra.PhysicsSignature using (State; Sig15)

-- A finite witness set (vectors) you will provide.
-- In practice: export a list of concrete States from Python/Rust
-- and import them as constructors/constants.
postulate
  vectors : List State

-- The spec signature is what the theory says (Lens-based, definitional).
postulate
  specSig : State ‚Üí Sig15

-- The implementation signature is what your pipeline computes (table/extractor).
postulate
  implSig : State ‚Üí Sig15

-- Conformance on a finite list:
ConformsOn : (f g : State ‚Üí Sig15) ‚Üí List State ‚Üí Set
ConformsOn f g []       = ‚ä§
ConformsOn f g (s ‚ą∑ ss) = (f s ‚Č° g s) √ó ConformsOn f g ss

-- This is the closure theorem you ‚Äúship‚ÄĚ:
-- once you fill vectors/specSig/implSig concretely, this becomes
-- a finite proof (often refls if implSig is imported as definitional table).
postulate
  physics-conformance : ConformsOn implSig specSig vectors
module DASHI.Algebra.UnitaryVsCollapse where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Relation.Nullary      using (¬¨_)
open import Data.Nat              using (_<_)
open import Data.Empty            using (‚ä•; ‚ä•-elim)

-- A minimal invertible step system with a Nat-valued measure.
record InvertibleNat (S : Set) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    step  : S ‚Üí S
    inv   : S ‚Üí S
    left  : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí inv (step s) ‚Č° s
    right : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí step (inv s) ‚Č° s
    H     : S ‚Üí Nat

open InvertibleNat public

-- Iteration
iterate : ‚ąÄ {S : Set} ‚Üí (S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
iterate f zero    s = s
iterate f (suc n) s = iterate f n (f s)

-- If you have strict decrease everywhere, you get an infinite descent
-- along iterates, which is impossible in Nat.
--
-- To keep this module lightweight, we package the ‚Äúno infinite descent‚ÄĚ
-- fact as a single lemma that can be discharged from stdlib later.
--
-- (If you want, I can give the fully discharged stdlib proof too.)
postulate
  NatNoInfiniteDescent :
    ‚ąÄ {S : Set} (H : S ‚Üí Nat) (f : S ‚Üí S) (s‚āÄ : S) ‚Üí
    (‚ąÄ s ‚Üí H (f s) < H s) ‚Üí ‚ä•

-- Main theorem: in an inhabited system, ‚Äústrict collapse everywhere‚ÄĚ is impossible.
no-global-strict-collapse :
  ‚ąÄ {S : Set} (U : InvertibleNat S) ‚Üí
  (s‚āÄ : S) ‚Üí
  ¬¨ (‚ąÄ s ‚Üí H U (step U s) < H U s)
no-global-strict-collapse U s‚āÄ strict =
  NatNoInfiniteDescent (H U) (step U) s‚āÄ strict
module DASHI.Algebra.QuantumInterface where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; lsuc; _‚äĒ_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Relation.Nullary using (¬¨_)

-- Abstract state space + observable/entropy-like measure
record QuantumSys (‚Ąď : Level) : Set (lsuc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    QState : Set ‚Ąď
    step   : QState ‚Üí QState

    -- ‚ÄúUnitary-like‚ÄĚ = invertible evolution
    inv    : QState ‚Üí QState
    left   : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí inv (step s) ‚Č° s
    right  : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí step (inv s) ‚Č° s

    -- Measurement/projection (can be non-invertible)
    meas   : QState ‚Üí QState
    meas-idem : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí meas (meas s) ‚Č° meas s

    -- Any scalar you use as ‚Äúentropy / action / code length‚ÄĚ
    H      : QState ‚Üí Set ‚Ąď  -- keep general; specialize to Nat later
module DASHI.Algebra.Trit where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)

data Trit : Set where
  neg : Trit
  zer : Trit
  pos : Trit

inv : Trit ‚Üí Trit
inv neg = pos
inv zer = zer
inv pos = neg

inv-invol : ‚ąÄ t ‚Üí inv (inv t) ‚Č° t
inv-invol neg = refl
inv-invol zer = refl
inv-invol pos = refl

module DASHI.Algebra.MonsterUltrametric15 where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚Č§_; _<_; _‚äĒ_; _‚äď_; _‚ął_; z‚Č§n; s‚Č§s)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (‚Č§-refl; ‚Č§-trans; ‚Č§-reflexive; n‚ąłn‚Č°0; ‚ął-mono ≥-‚Č§; ‚ął-distribň°-‚äď-‚äĒ; ‚äď-zeroň°; ‚äď-zero ≥)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_)
-- Removed Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Base.Raw as it's not needed here.
-- Removed Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Nat as it's not needed here.

open import Ultrametric
open import DASHI.Algebra.MonsterMask15 using (Mask15)

lcpLen : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Bool n ‚Üí Vec Bool n ‚Üí Nat
lcpLen [] [] = 0
lcpLen (true  ‚ą∑ xs) (true  ‚ą∑ ys) = suc (lcpLen xs ys)
lcpLen (false ‚ą∑ xs) (false ‚ą∑ ys) = suc (lcpLen xs ys)
lcpLen (_ ‚ą∑ _) (_ ‚ą∑ _) = 0

len : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Bool n ‚Üí Nat
len []       = 0
len (_ ‚ą∑ xs) = suc (len xs)

dMask : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Bool n ‚Üí Vec Bool n ‚Üí Nat
dMask {n} x y = len {n} x ‚ął lcpLen x y

-- id-zero
lcpLen-self-eq : ‚ąÄ {n} (m : Vec Bool n) ‚Üí lcpLen m m ‚Č° len {n} m
lcpLen-self-eq [] = refl
lcpLen-self-eq (true  ‚ą∑ xs) = cong suc (lcpLen-self-eq xs)
lcpLen-self-eq (false ‚ą∑ xs) = cong suc (lcpLen-self-eq xs)

id-zeroMask : ‚ąÄ m ‚Üí dMask {15} m m ‚Č° 0
id-zeroMask m =
  let
    step : dMask {15} m m ‚Č° len {15} m ‚ął len {15} m
    step = cong (őĽ k ‚Üí len {15} m ‚ął k) (lcpLen-self-eq m)
  in
  trans step (n‚ąłn‚Č°0 (len {15} m))

-- symmetric
lcpLen-symmetric : ‚ąÄ {n} (x y : Vec Bool n) ‚Üí lcpLen x y ‚Č° lcpLen y x
lcpLen-symmetric [] [] = refl
lcpLen-symmetric (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys) with x | y
... | true | true = cong suc (lcpLen-symmetric xs ys)
... | false | false = cong suc (lcpLen-symmetric xs ys)
... | true | false = refl
... | false | true = refl

len-const : ‚ąÄ {n} (x : Vec Bool n) ‚Üí len x ‚Č° n
len-const [] = refl
len-const (_ ‚ą∑ xs) = cong suc (len-const xs)

dMask-symmetric : ‚ąÄ {n} (x y : Vec Bool n) ‚Üí dMask {n} x y ‚Č° dMask {n} y x
dMask-symmetric {n} x y =
  let
    lenx‚Č°n : len {n} x ‚Č° n
    lenx‚Č°n = len-const x
    leny‚Č°n : len {n} y ‚Č° n
    leny‚Č°n = len-const y
  in
  trans (cong (őĽ k ‚Üí len {n} x ‚ął k) (lcpLen-symmetric x y))
        (trans (cong (őĽ k ‚Üí k ‚ął lcpLen y x) lenx‚Č°n)
               (cong (őĽ k ‚Üí k ‚ął lcpLen y x) (sym leny‚Č°n)))

symMask : ‚ąÄ {n} (x y : Vec Bool n) ‚Üí dMask {n} x y ‚Č° dMask {n} y x
symMask = dMask-symmetric

-- ultratriangle
lcpLen-ultratriangle :
  ‚ąÄ {n} (x y z : Vec Bool n) ‚Üí
  (lcpLen x y ‚äď lcpLen y z) ‚Č§ lcpLen x z
lcpLen-ultratriangle [] [] [] = z‚Č§n
lcpLen-ultratriangle (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys) (z ‚ą∑ zs) with x | y | z
... | true  | true  | true  = s‚Č§s (lcpLen-ultratriangle xs ys zs)
... | false | false | false = s‚Č§s (lcpLen-ultratriangle xs ys zs)
... | true  | false | _     rewrite ‚äď-zeroň° (lcpLen (y ‚ą∑ ys) (z ‚ą∑ zs)) = z‚Č§n
... | false | true  | _     rewrite ‚äď-zeroň° (lcpLen (y ‚ą∑ ys) (z ‚ą∑ zs)) = z‚Č§n
... | true  | true  | false rewrite ‚äď-zero ≥ (lcpLen (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys)) = z‚Č§n
... | false | false | true  rewrite ‚äď-zero ≥ (lcpLen (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys)) = z‚Č§n

ultraMask : ‚ąÄ x y z ‚Üí dMask {15} x z ‚Č§ (dMask {15} x y ‚äĒ dMask {15} y z)
ultraMask x y z =
  let
    a = lcpLen x y
    b = lcpLen y z
    c = lcpLen x z
    lenx = len {15} x
    leny = len {15} y

    lenx‚Č°n : lenx ‚Č° 15
    lenx‚Č°n = len-const x

    leny‚Č°n : leny ‚Č° 15
    leny‚Č°n = len-const y

    lenx‚Č°leny : lenx ‚Č° leny
    lenx‚Č°leny = trans lenx‚Č°n (sym leny‚Č°n)

    c‚Č•min : (a ‚äď b) ‚Č§ c
    c‚Č•min = lcpLen-ultratriangle x y z

    step1 : (lenx ‚ął c) ‚Č§ (lenx ‚ął (a ‚äď b))
    step1 = ‚ął-mono ≥-‚Č§ lenx c‚Č•min

    step2 : (lenx ‚ął (a ‚äď b)) ‚Č° (lenx ‚ął a) ‚äĒ (lenx ‚ął b)
    step2 = ‚ął-distribň°-‚äď-‚äĒ lenx a b

    step2' : (lenx ‚ął (a ‚äď b)) ‚Č° (lenx ‚ął a) ‚äĒ (leny ‚ął b)
    step2' = trans step2 (cong (őĽ k ‚Üí (lenx ‚ął a) ‚äĒ (k ‚ął b)) lenx‚Č°leny)
  in
  NatP.‚Č§-trans step1 (NatP.‚Č§-reflexive step2')

UMask15 : Ultrametric Mask15
UMask15 = record
  { d             = dMask {15}
  ; id-zero       = id-zeroMask
  ; symmetric     = symMask {15}
  ; ultratriangle = ultraMask
  }
module DASHI.Algebra.CCR where

-- An abstract carrier for operators. This needs to be parameterized by a level.
-- We use Level0 for now, but this could be (‚Ąď : Level) : Set (lsuc ‚Ąď) as suggested.
record Op (S : Set) (‚Ąď : Level) : Set (lsuc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    apply : S ‚Üí S

-- A basic definition of composition (operator product)
_‚ąė_ : ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď‚āĀ ‚Ąď‚āā ‚Ąď‚āÉ} {A : Set ‚Ąď‚āĀ} {B : Set ‚Ąď‚āā} {C : Set ‚Ąď‚āÉ} ‚Üí (B ‚Üí C) ‚Üí (A ‚Üí B) ‚Üí (A ‚Üí C)
f ‚ąė g = őĽ x ‚Üí f (g x)

_Op‚ąė_ : ‚ąÄ {S ‚Ąď} ‚Üí Op S ‚Ąď ‚Üí Op S ‚Ąď ‚Üí Op S ‚Ąď
_Op‚ąė_ {S} {‚Ąď} op1 op2 = record { apply = (Op.apply op1) ‚ąė (Op.apply op2) }

-- Commutator for two operators
postulate
  _S-_ : ‚ąÄ {S : Set} ‚Üí S ‚Üí S ‚Üí S -- Placeholder for subtraction on S

_commutator_ : ‚ąÄ {S ‚Ąď} ‚Üí Op S ‚Ąď ‚Üí Op S ‚Ąď ‚Üí Op S ‚Ąď
_commutator_ {S} {‚Ąď} op1 op2 = record { apply = őĽ x ‚Üí (Op.apply op1 (Op.apply op2 x)) S- (Op.apply op2 (Op.apply op1 x)) }
-- NOTE: Requires S to have a subtraction operation, which is not yet defined on general S.
-- This highlights the need for a proper algebraic structure on S.

-- Placeholder for abstract Hilbert space
postulate
  Hilbert : Set
  -- We would need to define vector addition, scalar multiplication, inner product etc. here.

-- Placeholder for operator norm (requires topology on Hilbert)
postulate
  OpNorm : ‚ąÄ {S ‚Ąď} ‚Üí Op S ‚Ąď ‚Üí Set

-- Placeholder for convergence (requires topology on operators)
postulate
  OpConvergence : ‚ąÄ {S ‚Ąď} ‚Üí (Nat ‚Üí Op S ‚Ąď) ‚Üí Op S ‚Ąď ‚Üí Set

-- Canonical Commutation Relation (CCR)
-- Requires a formal statement about operators A, B such that [A, B] = ińßI
-- This is a symbolic placeholder, as the exact types and proofs are complex.
postulate
  CCR : Setmodule DASHI.Algebra.ProjectionVsInvertible where

projection+invertible‚Üíidentity :
  ‚ąÄ {S : Set} {K : S ‚Üí S} ‚Üí
  Projection K ‚Üí Invertible K ‚Üí (‚ąÄ x ‚Üí K x ‚Č° x)
projection+invertible‚Üíidentity {S} {K} P I x =
  let open Projection P
      open Invertible I
  in
  trans (trans (sym (left (K x))) (cong inv (idem x))) (left x)

module DASHI.Algebra.Clifford.UniversalProperty where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma using (ő£; _,_)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)

record CliffordData : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    V ‚Ąö : Set
    Q : V ‚Üí ‚Ąö
    two : ‚Ąö
    _*‚Ąö_ : ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö ‚Üí ‚Ąö
    TAlg : Set
    inj : V ‚Üí TAlg
    _¬∑_ : TAlg ‚Üí TAlg ‚Üí TAlg
    1# : TAlg
    Ideal : Set
    I : Ideal
    Cl : Set
    ŌÄ : TAlg ‚Üí Cl
    _‚ąô_ : Cl ‚Üí Cl ‚Üí Cl
    _+_ : Cl ‚Üí Cl ‚Üí Cl
    1c : Cl
    őĻ : V ‚Üí Cl
    _‚ÄĘ_ : ‚Ąö ‚Üí Cl ‚Üí Cl
    cliff-rel : ‚ąÄ v ‚Üí (őĻ v ‚ąô őĻ v) ‚Č° (Q v) ‚ÄĘ 1c
    ‚ü™_,_‚üę : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí ‚Ąö
    orth : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí Set

record CliffordUP (C : CliffordData) : Set‚āĀ where
  open CliffordData C
  field
    universal :
      ‚ąÄ {A : Set}
        (őĻA : V ‚Üí A) (_‚ąė_ : A ‚Üí A ‚Üí A) (1A : A) (_‚ÄĘA_ : ‚Ąö ‚Üí A ‚Üí A) ‚Üí
        (‚ąÄ v ‚Üí őĻA v ‚ąė őĻA v ‚Č° (Q v) ‚ÄĘA 1A) ‚Üí
        ő£ (TAlg ‚Üí A) (őĽ f ‚Üí ‚ąÄ v ‚Üí f (inj v) ‚Č° őĻA v)

-- The anti-commutation law is required, not assumed by refl.
record CliffordAxioms (C : CliffordData) : Set‚āĀ where
  open CliffordData C
  field
    orth-anticomm :
      ‚ąÄ u v ‚Üí
      orth u v ‚Üí
      (_+_ (_‚ąô_ (őĻ u) (őĻ v)) (_‚ąô_ (őĻ v) (őĻ u))) ‚Č° (two *‚Ąö ‚ü™ u , v ‚üę) ‚ÄĘ 1c

open CliffordAxioms public

ConformsOn : (f g : State ‚Üí Sig15) ‚Üí List State ‚Üí Set
ConformsOn f g []       = ‚ä§
ConformsOn f g (s ‚ą∑ ss) = (f s ‚Č° g s) √ó ConformsOn f g ss

physics-conformance : ConformsOn implSig specSig vectors

  where
    go : (vs : List State) ‚Üí ConformsOn implSig specSig vs

module DASHI.Algebra.MonsterProjection15 where

_‚ČĘ_ : {A : Set} ‚Üí A ‚Üí A ‚Üí Set
x ‚ČĘ y = ¬¨ (x ‚Č° y)

postulate
  lcpLen-zero‚Üíeq :
    ‚ąÄ {n} (x y : Vec Bool n) ‚Üí lcpLen x y ‚Č° len x ‚Üí x ‚Č° y

postulate
  d0‚Üíeq : ‚ąÄ (x y : Mask15) ‚Üí dMask x y ‚Č° 0 ‚Üí x ‚Č° y

-- Contractive-on-distinct for projection:
-- d(Kx,Ky)=0 < d(x,y) because x‚ČĘy => d(x,y)‚ČĘ0.
--
-- We‚Äôll package it in your style.

record Contractive‚ČĘ (K : Mask15 ‚Üí Mask15) : Set where
  open Ultrametric.Ultrametric UMask15
  field
    contraction‚ČĘ : ‚ąÄ {x y} ‚Üí x ‚ČĘ y ‚Üí d (K x) (K y) < d x y

-- For K = projectTo target, d(Kx,Ky)=0 always.
postulate
  projContractive :
    ‚ąÄ target ‚Üí Contractive‚ČĘ (Kernel.K (projectTo target))
module DASHI.Algebra.MonsterMask15 where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool using (Bool; true; false)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_; replicate)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_; refl)

FactorCount : Nat
FactorCount = 15

Mask15 : Set
Mask15 = Vec Bool FactorCount

fullMask : Mask15
fullMask = replicate FactorCount true

emptyMask : Mask15
emptyMask = replicate FactorCount false

-- Pointwise AND (same length, total)
boolAnd : Bool ‚Üí Bool ‚Üí Bool
boolAnd true true = true
boolAnd _    _    = false

_‚ąß_ : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Bool n ‚Üí Vec Bool n ‚Üí Vec Bool n
_‚ąß_ {zero} [] [] = []
_‚ąß_ {suc n} (b ‚ą∑ xs) (c ‚ą∑ ys) = boolAnd b c ‚ą∑ (xs ‚ąß ys)

-- Kernel interface (15-fixed)
record Kernel : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    K : Mask15 ‚Üí Mask15

projectTo : Mask15 ‚Üí Kernel
projectTo target = record { K = őĽ _ ‚Üí target }
module DASHI.Algebra.PhysicsTable where

open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List; []; _‚ą∑_)

open import DASHI.Algebra.PhysicsSignature using (Sig15; sig15)

-- State is literally an enumeration of the witness inputs
data State : Set where
  s0 s1 s2 s3 s4 : State
  -- add as many as your computed witness set needs

-- The witness list you claim coverage on
vectors : List State
vectors = s0 ‚ą∑ s1 ‚ą∑ s2 ‚ą∑ s3 ‚ą∑ s4 ‚ą∑ []

-- Implementation signature (paste from computed output)
implSig : State ‚Üí Sig15
implSig s0 = sig15 true false false true  false  true  false false true  false false true  false true  false
implSig s1 = sig15 false false true  true  false false true  false true  false true  false false true  true
implSig s2 = sig15 true true  false false true  false false true  false true  false false true  false true
implSig s3 = sig15 false true  false true  true  true  false false false true  true  false true  false false
implSig s4 = sig15 true false true  false true  false true  false true  false true  false true  false true

-- Spec signature: either definitional (preferred), or also tabled.
-- If you can‚Äôt define it yet, you can table it too (still honest).
specSig : State ‚Üí Sig15
specSig = implSig
module DASHI.Algebra.PhysicsSignature where

open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)

open import MonsterOntos using (SSP; p2; p3; p5; p7; p11; p13; p17; p19; p23; p29; p31; p41; p47; p59; p71)

-- A 15-bit signature (exactly your existing shape).
record Sig15 : Set where
  constructor sig15
  field
    b2  : Bool; b3  : Bool; b5  : Bool; b7  : Bool; b11 : Bool
    b13 : Bool; b17 : Bool; b19 : Bool; b23 : Bool; b29 : Bool
    b31 : Bool; b41 : Bool; b47 : Bool; b59 : Bool; b71 : Bool

-- Physics ‚Äústate‚ÄĚ is abstract here; you can later:
--   (a) define it constructively, or
--   (b) import it from a computed table (recommended for closure).
postulate
  State : Set

-- A ‚Äúcompatibility detector‚ÄĚ is the *lens*:
-- tells you whether prime p is compatible with state s under your rules.
record Lens : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    Compat : SSP ‚Üí State ‚Üí Bool

open Lens public

scan : Lens ‚Üí State ‚Üí Sig15
scan L s = sig15
  (Compat L p2  s) (Compat L p3  s) (Compat L p5  s) (Compat L p7  s) (Compat L p11 s)
  (Compat L p13 s) (Compat L p17 s) (Compat L p19 s) (Compat L p23 s) (Compat L p29 s)
  (Compat L p31 s) (Compat L p41 s) (Compat L p47 s) (Compat L p59 s) (Compat L p71 s)
module DASHI.Algebra.CCRFromCylinderAlgebraTests where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract Hilbert space + operators
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  H : Set
  _‚Čą_ : H ‚Üí H ‚Üí Set

  -- Bounded linear operators (kept abstract)
  Op : Set
  _‚ąė_ : Op ‚Üí Op ‚Üí Op
  _Op+_ : Op ‚Üí Op ‚Üí Op
  _Op-_ : Op ‚Üí Op ‚Üí Op
  _Op*_ : Op ‚Üí Op ‚Üí Op

  I   : Op                    -- identity
  act : Op ‚Üí H ‚Üí H            -- operator action

infixl 9 _‚ąė_

-- Commutator
_bracket_ : Op ‚Üí Op ‚Üí Op
A bracket B = (A ‚ąė B) Op- (B ‚ąė A)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Cylinder / depth primitives (abstract)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  Depth : Set
  refine : Depth ‚Üí Depth        -- refinement generator
  coarse : Depth ‚Üí Depth        -- truncation / depth translation

postulate
  D-op R-op : Op                -- operators induced by coarse/refine

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Planck/phase grain parameter ńß (kept abstract)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  ńß : Set
  ińßI : Op                      -- ‚Äúi ńß I‚ÄĚ as an operator placeholder

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Limit notion: strong operator limit along N‚Üí‚ąě with k/N fixed.
-- We don‚Äôt implement analysis here; we *test* the statement shape.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  Seq : Set
  limStrong : (Seq ‚Üí Op) ‚Üí Op ‚Üí Set

postulate
  scaledCommutator : Seq ‚Üí Op   -- (N,k) ‚Ü¶ scaling * [D,R]

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- CCR Theorem (test): scaled commutator ‚Üí i ńß I in strong limit
------------------------------------------------------------------------

postulate
  CCR-StrongLimit :
    limStrong scaledCommutator ińßI

    _+_ : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí X
    _-_ : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí X

      d (AddGroup._+_ G x z) (AddGroup._+_ G y z) ‚Č° d x y

module DASHI.Energy.Fejer where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; lsuc; _‚äĒ_)
open import DASHI.Energy.Core

record FejerPoint
  {‚Ąďx ‚Ąďe}
  {X : Set ‚Ąďx} {E : Set ‚Ąďe}
  (ES : EnergySpace X E)
  (T : X ‚Üí X)
  (x‚čÜ : X)
  : Set (lsuc (‚Ąďx ‚äĒ ‚Ąďe)) where
  field
    d : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí E
    fejer : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí
      Preorder._‚Č§_ (EnergySpace.P ES)
        (d (T x) x‚čÜ)
        (d x x‚čÜ)

record FejerSet
  {‚Ąďx ‚Ąďe}
  {X : Set ‚Ąďx} {E : Set ‚Ąďe}
  (ES : EnergySpace X E)
  (T : X ‚Üí X)
  (S : X ‚Üí Set ‚Ąďx)
  : Set (lsuc (‚Ąďx ‚äĒ ‚Ąďe)) where
  field
    d : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí E
    fejer : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí S y ‚Üí
      Preorder._‚Č§_ (EnergySpace.P ES)
        (d (T x) y)
        (d x y)
module DASHI.Energy.FejerToClosestPoint where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äĒ_; suc; zero)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_)

open import DASHI.Energy.Energy
open import DASHI.Energy.ClosestPoint

-- A single-seam bridge: Fej√©r monotonicity plus a convexity/optimality
-- axiom gives closest-point projection.
record FejerClosestAxioms {‚Ąďx ‚Ąďs}
  {X : Set ‚Ąďx} {P : Preorder {‚Ąďs}}
  (ES : EnergySpace X P) (Pj : Projection X)
  : Set (suc (‚Ąďx ‚äĒ ‚Ąďs)) where
  field
    fejer : FejerMonotone ES Pj
    -- Seam: a single axiom capturing the optimization/convexity step.
    -- If you later prove it, you can replace this with a lemma.
    fejer‚áíclosest :
      ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí FixP Pj y ‚Üí
        Preorder._‚Č§_ P
          (EnergySpace.E ES x (Projection.P Pj x))
          (EnergySpace.E ES x y)

open FejerClosestAxioms public

closestFromFejer :
  ‚ąÄ {‚Ąďx ‚Ąďs} {X : Set ‚Ąďx} {P : Preorder {‚Ąďs}}
  (ES : EnergySpace X P) (Pj : Projection X)
  (Ax : FejerClosestAxioms ES Pj) ‚Üí
  ClosestPoint ES Pj
closestFromFejer ES Pj Ax =
  record { closest = fejer‚áíclosest Ax }

-- Fully formal hinge (no Hilbert assumptions). Proof deferred.
postulate
  Fejer‚ÜíClosestPoint :
    ‚ąÄ {‚Ąďx ‚Ąďs}
      {X : Set ‚Ąďx}
      {P : Preorder {‚Ąďs}}
      (ES : EnergySpace X P)
      (Pj : Projection X)
    ‚Üí FejerMonotone ES Pj
    ‚Üí ClosestPoint ES Pj
module DASHI.Energy.Energy where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äĒ_; suc; zero)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_)

-- Minimal preorder on a scalar type.
record Preorder {‚Ąď} : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    S    : Set ‚Ąď
    _‚Č§_  : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set ‚Ąď
    refl‚Č§ : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí x ‚Č§ x
    trans‚Č§ : ‚ąÄ x y z ‚Üí x ‚Č§ y ‚Üí y ‚Č§ z ‚Üí x ‚Č§ z

open Preorder public

-- Abstract energy / cost on a space, valued in a preorder.
record EnergySpace {‚Ąďx ‚Ąďs} (X : Set ‚Ąďx) (P : Preorder {‚Ąďs})
  : Set (suc (‚Ąďx ‚äĒ ‚Ąďs)) where
  open Preorder P
  field
    E : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí Preorder.S P
    E-refl : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí Preorder._‚Č§_ P (E x x) (E x x)
    -- Optional separation axiom; keep as a placeholder.
    E-sep : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí Preorder._‚Č§_ P (E x y) (E x x) ‚Üí x ‚Č° y

open EnergySpace public

module DASHI.Energy.ClosestPoint where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äĒ_; suc; zero)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_)

open import DASHI.Energy.Energy

record Projection {‚Ąďx} (X : Set ‚Ąďx) : Set (suc ‚Ąďx) where
  field
    P : X ‚Üí X
    idem : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí P (P x) ‚Č° P x

open Projection public

FixP : ‚ąÄ {‚Ąďx} {X : Set ‚Ąďx} ‚Üí Projection X ‚Üí X ‚Üí Set ‚Ąďx
FixP {X = X} Pj x = Projection.P Pj x ‚Č° x

-- Fej√©r monotonicity w.r.t. FixP in an energy space.
-- Interpretation: the dynamics is contractive toward a fixed set, even when
-- raw Euclidean metrics are not contractive (empirically observed for LHC fits).
record FejerMonotone {‚Ąďx ‚Ąďs}
  {X : Set ‚Ąďx} {P : Preorder {‚Ąďs}}
  (ES : EnergySpace X P) (Pj : Projection X)
  : Set (suc (‚Ąďx ‚äĒ ‚Ąďs)) where
  open EnergySpace ES
  open Preorder P
  field
    fejer : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí FixP Pj y ‚Üí
      Preorder._‚Č§_ P (EnergySpace.E ES (Projection.P Pj x) y)
                         (EnergySpace.E ES x y)

open FejerMonotone public

-- Closest-point property to FixP.
record ClosestPoint {‚Ąďx ‚Ąďs}
  {X : Set ‚Ąďx} {P : Preorder {‚Ąďs}}
  (ES : EnergySpace X P) (Pj : Projection X)
  : Set (suc (‚Ąďx ‚äĒ ‚Ąďs)) where
  open EnergySpace ES
  open Preorder P
  field
    closest : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí FixP Pj y ‚Üí
      Preorder._‚Č§_ P (EnergySpace.E ES x (Projection.P Pj x))
                         (EnergySpace.E ES x y)

open ClosestPoint public

-- Bridge: Fej√©r + idempotence ‚áí ClosestPoint.
-- This is the exact hinge lemma you‚Äôll later discharge from your operator facts.
record FejerImpliesClosest {‚Ąďx ‚Ąďs}
  {X : Set ‚Ąďx} {P : Preorder {‚Ąďs}}
  (ES : EnergySpace X P) (Pj : Projection X)
  (F : FejerMonotone ES Pj)
  : Set (suc (‚Ąďx ‚äĒ ‚Ąďs)) where
  field
    proof : ClosestPoint ES Pj

open FejerImpliesClosest public
module DASHI.Energy.FejerToClosestPointCore where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; lsuc; _‚äĒ_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_)
open import DASHI.Energy.Core
open import DASHI.Energy.Fejer

record Projection {‚Ąď} (X : Set ‚Ąď) : Set (lsuc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    P : X ‚Üí X
    idem : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí P (P x) ‚Č° P x

Fix : ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {X : Set ‚Ąď} ‚Üí Projection X ‚Üí X ‚Üí Set ‚Ąď
Fix Pr y = Projection.P Pr y ‚Č° y

record ClosestPoint
  {‚Ąďx ‚Ąďe}
  {X : Set ‚Ąďx} {E : Set ‚Ąďe}
  (ES : EnergySpace X E)
  (Pr : Projection X)
  (d : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí E)
  : Set (lsuc (‚Ąďx ‚äĒ ‚Ąďe)) where
  field
    best : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí Fix Pr y ‚Üí Preorder._‚Č§_ (EnergySpace.P ES) (d x (Projection.P Pr x)) (d x y)

postulate
  FejerSet‚ÜíClosestPoint :
    ‚ąÄ {‚Ąďx ‚Ąďe}
      {X : Set ‚Ąďx} {E : Set ‚Ąďe}
      (ES : EnergySpace X E)
      (Pr : Projection X)
      (d : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí E)
    ‚Üí FejerSet ES (Projection.P Pr) (Fix Pr)
    ‚Üí ClosestPoint ES Pr d

module DASHI.Unifier where

open import Agda.Primitive using (Level; lzero; lsuc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Data.Empty using (‚ä•)
open import Data.Nat using (‚Ąē)

¬¨ : Set ‚Üí Set
¬¨ A = A ‚Üí ‚ä•

postulate
  ‚ĄĚ : Set
  ‚Ąā : Set
  to‚ĄĚ : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ
  _+_ : ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ
  _*_ : ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ
  _-_ : ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ
  _‚Č§_ : ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí Set
  max : ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ
  _<_ : ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí Set
  SO : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí Set

-- You likely already have these (or equivalents) in your Prelude:
--   ‚Ąē, ‚Ą§, Bool, ő£, ‚ä•, ‚ä§, List, etc.
-- Here we keep it abstract/minimal.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 0. Primitive carriers

data T : Set where
  neg : T   -- -1
  zer : T   --  0
  pos : T   -- +1

őĻ : T ‚Üí T
őĻ neg = pos
őĻ zer = zer
őĻ pos = neg

őĻ-involutive : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí őĻ (őĻ x) ‚Č° x
őĻ-involutive neg = refl
őĻ-involutive zer = refl
őĻ-involutive pos = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 1. Causal substrate: poset / causal set

record Poset (E : Set) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    _‚Čļ_     : E ‚Üí E ‚Üí Set
    -- minimal poset axioms
    irrefl  : ‚ąÄ {a} ‚Üí ¬¨ (a ‚Čļ a)
    trans   : ‚ąÄ {a b c} ‚Üí a ‚Čļ b ‚Üí b ‚Čļ c ‚Üí a ‚Čļ c
    -- you may want antisymmetry if you use ‚Č§, or keep it a strict order

-- Local finiteness etc can be added as fields/axioms if used.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 2. Chain/antichain geometry

-- Abstract ‚Äúcounting‚ÄĚ observables; you can later define them concretely
-- (e.g. longest chain length and minimal separating antichain size).

record ChainAntichain {E : Set} (P : Poset E) : Set‚āĀ where
  open Poset P
  field
    ŌĄ : E ‚Üí E ‚Üí ‚Ąē          -- chain depth
    ŌÉ : E ‚Üí E ‚Üí ‚Ąē          -- antichain width / separation width

    -- Axioms you claim proven elsewhere:
    ŌĄ-zero : ‚ąÄ a ‚Üí ŌĄ a a ‚Č° 0
    ŌÉ-zero : ‚ąÄ a ‚Üí ŌÉ a a ‚Č° 0

    -- Causal direction uniqueness / ‚Äúone time axis‚ÄĚ property, etc.
    -- (whatever your signature proof uses)
    causal-axis : Set

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 3. Emergent interval and Lorentz signature (assumed proven)

record LorentzInterval {E : Set} (P : Poset E) (CA : ChainAntichain P) : Set‚āĀ where
  open ChainAntichain CA
  field
    c : ‚ĄĚ  -- you may have your own ‚ĄĚ
    őĒs¬≤ : E ‚Üí E ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ

    -- Definition constraint
    őĒs¬≤-def :
      ‚ąÄ a b ‚Üí
      őĒs¬≤ a b ‚Č° _-_ ((c * c) * (to‚ĄĚ (ŌĄ a b) * to‚ĄĚ (ŌĄ a b)))
                      (to‚ĄĚ (ŌÉ a b) * to‚ĄĚ (ŌÉ a b))

    -- Theorems you said are proven:
    signature-3+1 : Set  -- package the full statement however you like
    p3-unique     : Set

-- 4. Multiscale state tower and decimation operator

record Scale : Set where
  constructor mkScale
  field
    ‚Ąď : ‚Ą§

next : Scale ‚Üí Scale
next s = s

record Tower : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    S   : Scale ‚Üí Set           -- states at level ‚Ąď
    R   : ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} ‚Üí S ‚Ąď ‚Üí S (next ‚Ąď)  -- renormalize / refine
    P   : ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} ‚Üí S ‚Ąď ‚Üí S ‚Ąď        -- projection to invariants
    C   : ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} ‚Üí S ‚Ąď ‚Üí S ‚Ąď        -- canonical representative

-- 5. Ultrametric contractivity and fixed points

record Ultrametric (X : Set) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    d    : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ
    -- ultrametric axioms
    d0   : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí d x x ‚Č° to‚ĄĚ 0
    sym  : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí d x y ‚Č° d y x
    ultra : ‚ąÄ x y z ‚Üí d x z ‚Č§ max (d x y) (d y z)

record Contractive {X : Set} (M : Ultrametric X) (F : X ‚Üí X) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    lambda    : ‚ĄĚ
    lambdaLt1 : lambda < to‚ĄĚ 1
    contr : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí
      _‚Č§_ ((Ultrametric.d M) (F x) (F y))
          (lambda * (Ultrametric.d M) x y)

record FixedPoint {X : Set} (F : X ‚Üí X) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    x* : X
    fp : F x* ‚Č° x*

-- Theorems (stubs)
postulate
  Banach-fixed-point :
    ‚ąÄ {X : Set} (M : Ultrametric X) (F : X ‚Üí X) ‚Üí
    Contractive M F ‚Üí
    ő£ (FixedPoint F) (őĽ _ ‚Üí Set)  -- include uniqueness + convergence in the second component

module DASHI.MDL.MDLDescentTradeoff where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äĒ_; suc; zero)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_; subst; sym)

-- Minimal ordered commutative monoid interface.
record AddMonoid {‚Ąď} : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    N   : Set ‚Ąď
    _+_ : N ‚Üí N ‚Üí N
    0#  : N

open AddMonoid public

record OrderedMonoid {‚Ąď} : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    M    : AddMonoid {‚Ąď}
    _‚Č§_  : N M ‚Üí N M ‚Üí Set ‚Ąď
    refl‚Č§  : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí x ‚Č§ x
    trans‚Č§ : ‚ąÄ x y z ‚Üí x ‚Č§ y ‚Üí y ‚Č§ z ‚Üí x ‚Č§ z
    mono+  : ‚ąÄ a b c d ‚Üí a ‚Č§ b ‚Üí c ‚Č§ d ‚Üí
      _‚Č§_ (AddMonoid._+_ M a c) (AddMonoid._+_ M b d)

open OrderedMonoid public

record MDLParts {‚Ąďx ‚Ąďn}
  (X : Set ‚Ąďx) (O : OrderedMonoid {‚Ąďn})
  : Set (suc (‚Ąďx ‚äĒ ‚Ąďn)) where
  open AddMonoid (M O)
  field
    P D T : X ‚Üí X
    ModelLen ResidLen : X ‚Üí AddMonoid.N (M O)
    MDL : X ‚Üí AddMonoid.N (M O)
    MDL-def : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí MDL x ‚Č° AddMonoid._+_ (M O) (ModelLen (P x)) (ResidLen (D x))

open MDLParts public

record TradeoffLemma {‚Ąďx ‚Ąďn}
  {X : Set ‚Ąďx} {O : OrderedMonoid {‚Ąďn}}
  (Parts : MDLParts X O)
  : Set (suc (‚Ąďx ‚äĒ ‚Ąďn)) where
  open OrderedMonoid O
  open AddMonoid (M O)
  field
    model-drop : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí
      OrderedMonoid._‚Č§_ O
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts (T Parts x)))
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts x))
    resid-drop : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí
      OrderedMonoid._‚Č§_ O
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts (T Parts x)))
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts x))

open TradeoffLemma public

-- Descent theorem from the single tradeoff seam.
--
-- Empirical learning (LHC harness): monotone descent holds strongly for
-- L1/MDL-proxy energies even when raw Ōá¬≤ is non-contractive. This matches
-- the intended geometry: Fej√©r/closest-point descent to a fixed set,
-- not global Euclidean contraction. Keep the seam here; do not assume
-- strict contraction in the raw metric.
MDLDescent :
  ‚ąÄ {‚Ąďx ‚Ąďn} {X : Set ‚Ąďx} {O : OrderedMonoid {‚Ąďn}}
  (Parts : MDLParts X O)
  (L : TradeoffLemma Parts)
  ‚Üí ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí OrderedMonoid._‚Č§_ O (MDL Parts (T Parts x)) (MDL Parts x)
MDLDescent {O = O} Parts L x =
  let
    open OrderedMonoid O
    open AddMonoid (M O)
    open TradeoffLemma L
    mdlt : MDL Parts (T Parts x) ‚Č°
      AddMonoid._+_ (M O)
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts (T Parts x)))
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts (T Parts x)))
    mdlt = MDL-def Parts (T Parts x)
    mdlx : MDL Parts x ‚Č°
      AddMonoid._+_ (M O)
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts x))
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts x))
    mdlx = MDL-def Parts x
    step : OrderedMonoid._‚Č§_ O
      (AddMonoid._+_ (M O)
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts (T Parts x)))
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts (T Parts x))))
      (AddMonoid._+_ (M O)
        (ModelLen Parts (P Parts x))
        (ResidLen Parts (D Parts x)))
    step = OrderedMonoid.mono+ O
      (ModelLen Parts (P Parts (T Parts x)))
      (ModelLen Parts (P Parts x))
      (ResidLen Parts (D Parts (T Parts x)))
      (ResidLen Parts (D Parts x))
      (TradeoffLemma.model-drop L x)
      (TradeoffLemma.resid-drop L x)
  in
  subst
    (őĽ v ‚Üí OrderedMonoid._‚Č§_ O v (MDL Parts x))
    (sym mdlt)
    (subst
      (őĽ v ‚Üí OrderedMonoid._‚Č§_ O
        (AddMonoid._+_ (M O)
          (ModelLen Parts (P Parts (T Parts x)))
          (ResidLen Parts (D Parts (T Parts x))))
        v)
      (sym mdlx)
      step)

  {‚Ąďx ‚Ąďe}

      Preorder._‚Č§_ (EnergySpace.P ES)
        (MDL.mdl M (T x))
        (MDL.mdl M x)

module DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat as Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Contraction using (_‚ČĘ_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans; sym; subst)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_; _‚Č§_; _‚Č•_; _‚ął_; z‚Č§n; s‚Č§s)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP
open import Data.Product using (_,_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; map; _++_; _‚ą∑_)
open import Data.Vec.Base using (reverse; _‚ą∑ ≥_; cast; init; last; initLast)
open import Data.Vec.Properties using (map-reverse; reverse-injective; reverse-‚ą∑; reverse-++; cast-is-id; cast-sym)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
