cong‚āā : ‚ąÄ {A B C : Set} {x‚āĀ x‚āā : A} {y‚āĀ y‚āā : B}
        (g : A ‚Üí B ‚Üí C) ‚Üí
        x‚āĀ ‚Č° x‚āā ‚Üí y‚āĀ ‚Č° y‚āā ‚Üí g x‚āĀ y‚āĀ ‚Č° g x‚āā y‚āā
cong‚āā g refl refl = refl

-- Fine agreement metric: use agreement depth on reversed vectors (suffix agreement).
agreeDepthFine : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Nat
agreeDepthFine x y = AM.agreeDepth (reverse x) (reverse y)

dNatFine : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Nat
dNatFine x y = AM.dNat (reverse x) (reverse y)

dNatFine-inv :
  ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (map inv x) (map inv y) ‚Č° dNatFine x y
dNatFine-inv x y =
  let
    rx = reverse x
    ry = reverse y
    rx-inv : reverse (map inv x) ‚Č° map inv rx
    rx-inv = sym (map-reverse inv x)
    ry-inv : reverse (map inv y) ‚Č° map inv ry
    ry-inv = sym (map-reverse inv y)
  in
  trans
    (cong (őĽ a ‚Üí AM.dNat a (reverse (map inv y))) rx-inv)
    (trans
      (cong (őĽ b ‚Üí AM.dNat (map inv rx) b) ry-inv)
      (AM.dNat-inv rx ry)
    )

reverse‚ČĘ : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} {x y : Vec Trit n} ‚Üí x ‚ČĘ y ‚Üí reverse x ‚ČĘ reverse y
reverse‚ČĘ x‚ČĘy rev‚Č° = x‚ČĘy (reverse-injective rev‚Č°)

dNatFine-zero‚Üíeq :
  ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí dNatFine x y ‚Č° 0 ‚Üí x ‚Č° y
dNatFine-zero‚Üíeq x y d‚Č°0 =
  reverse-injective (AM.dNat-zero‚Üíeq (reverse x) (reverse y) d‚Č°0)

dNatFine-positive :
  ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} {x y : Vec Trit n} ‚Üí x ‚ČĘ y ‚Üí 0 < dNatFine x y
dNatFine-positive x‚ČĘy = AM.dNat-positive (reverse‚ČĘ x‚ČĘy)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Agreement-depth monotonicity under pointwise maps

agreeDepth-map‚Č§ :
  ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (f : Trit ‚Üí Trit) (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  AM.agreeDepth x y ‚Č§ AM.agreeDepth (map f x) (map f y)
agreeDepth-map‚Č§ {n = Nat.zero} f [] [] = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-map‚Č§ {suc n} f (neg ‚ą∑ xs) (neg ‚ą∑ ys) with f neg
... | neg = s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-map‚Č§ f xs ys)
... | zer = s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-map‚Č§ f xs ys)
... | pos = s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-map‚Č§ f xs ys)
agreeDepth-map‚Č§ {suc n} f (zer ‚ą∑ xs) (zer ‚ą∑ ys) with f zer
... | neg = s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-map‚Č§ f xs ys)
... | zer = s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-map‚Č§ f xs ys)
... | pos = s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-map‚Č§ f xs ys)
agreeDepth-map‚Č§ {suc n} f (pos ‚ą∑ xs) (pos ‚ą∑ ys) with f pos
... | neg = s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-map‚Č§ f xs ys)
... | zer = s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-map‚Č§ f xs ys)
... | pos = s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-map‚Č§ f xs ys)
agreeDepth-map‚Č§ {suc n} f (neg ‚ą∑ xs) (zer ‚ą∑ ys) = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-map‚Č§ {suc n} f (neg ‚ą∑ xs) (pos ‚ą∑ ys) = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-map‚Č§ {suc n} f (zer ‚ą∑ xs) (neg ‚ą∑ ys) = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-map‚Č§ {suc n} f (zer ‚ą∑ xs) (pos ‚ą∑ ys) = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-map‚Č§ {suc n} f (pos ‚ą∑ xs) (neg ‚ą∑ ys) = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-map‚Č§ {suc n} f (pos ‚ą∑ xs) (zer ‚ą∑ ys) = z‚Č§n

dNatFine-map‚Č§ :
  ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (f : Trit ‚Üí Trit) (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (map f x) (map f y) ‚Č§ dNatFine x y
dNatFine-map‚Č§ {n} f x y =
  let
    rx-map : reverse (map f x) ‚Č° map f (reverse x)
    rx-map = sym (map-reverse f x)
    ry-map : reverse (map f y) ‚Č° map f (reverse y)
    ry-map = sym (map-reverse f y)
    step : AM.dNat (map f (reverse x)) (map f (reverse y)) ‚Č§ AM.dNat (reverse x) (reverse y)
    step = NatP.‚ął-mono ≥-‚Č§ n (agreeDepth-map‚Č§ f (reverse x) (reverse y))
  in
  NatP.‚Č§-trans
    (NatP.‚Č§-reflexive (cong‚āā AM.dNat rx-map ry-map))
    step

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Agreement depth for append (prefix metric on reverse)

agreeDepth-++‚Č• :
  ‚ąÄ {m n : Nat} (a b : Vec Trit m) (c : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  AM.agreeDepth (a ++ c) (b ++ c) ‚Č• AM.agreeDepth a b
agreeDepth-++‚Č• {m = Nat.zero} {n} [] [] c = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-++‚Č• {suc m} {n} (neg ‚ą∑ as) (neg ‚ą∑ bs) c =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-++‚Č• as bs c)
agreeDepth-++‚Č• {suc m} {n} (zer ‚ą∑ as) (zer ‚ą∑ bs) c =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-++‚Č• as bs c)
agreeDepth-++‚Č• {suc m} {n} (pos ‚ą∑ as) (pos ‚ą∑ bs) c =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-++‚Č• as bs c)
agreeDepth-++‚Č• {suc m} {n} (neg ‚ą∑ as) (zer ‚ą∑ bs) c = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-++‚Č• {suc m} {n} (neg ‚ą∑ as) (pos ‚ą∑ bs) c = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-++‚Č• {suc m} {n} (zer ‚ą∑ as) (neg ‚ą∑ bs) c = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-++‚Č• {suc m} {n} (zer ‚ą∑ as) (pos ‚ą∑ bs) c = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-++‚Č• {suc m} {n} (pos ‚ą∑ as) (neg ‚ą∑ bs) c = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-++‚Č• {suc m} {n} (pos ‚ą∑ as) (zer ‚ą∑ bs) c = z‚Č§n

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Reverse of snoc: reverse (xs ‚ą∑ ≥ a) = a ‚ą∑ reverse xs

reverse-‚ą∑ ≥ : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit n) (a : Trit) ‚Üí
  reverse (xs ‚ą∑ ≥ a) ‚Č° a ‚ą∑ reverse xs
reverse-‚ą∑ ≥ [] a = reverse-‚ą∑ a []
reverse-‚ą∑ ≥ (x ‚ą∑ xs) a
  rewrite reverse-‚ą∑ x (xs ‚ą∑ ≥ a)
        | reverse-‚ą∑ ≥ xs a
        | reverse-‚ą∑ x xs
  = refl

agreeDepth-cast :
  ‚ąÄ {m n : Nat} (eq : m ‚Č° n) (x y : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  AM.agreeDepth (cast eq x) (cast eq y) ‚Č° AM.agreeDepth x y
agreeDepth-cast refl x y
  rewrite cast-is-id refl x
        | cast-is-id refl y
  = refl

dNat-cast :
  ‚ąÄ {m n : Nat} (eq : m ‚Č° n) (x y : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  AM.dNat (cast eq x) (cast eq y) ‚Č° AM.dNat x y
dNat-cast refl x y
  rewrite cast-is-id refl x
        | cast-is-id refl y
  = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- ShiftTail monotonicity on fine agreement

agreeDepth-++-mono :
  ‚ąÄ {m n : Nat} (u v u' v' : Vec Trit m) (p q : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  AM.agreeDepth u v ‚Č§ AM.agreeDepth u' v' ‚Üí
  AM.agreeDepth (u ++ p) (v ++ q) ‚Č§ AM.agreeDepth (u' ++ p) (v' ++ q)
agreeDepth-++-mono {m = Nat.zero} {n} [] [] [] [] p q h = NatP.‚Č§-refl
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg ‚ą∑ us) (neg ‚ą∑ vs) (neg ‚ą∑ us') (neg ‚ą∑ vs') p q (s‚Č§s h‚Č§) =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚Č§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg ‚ą∑ us) (neg ‚ą∑ vs) (zer ‚ą∑ us') (zer ‚ą∑ vs') p q (s‚Č§s h‚Č§) =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚Č§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg ‚ą∑ us) (neg ‚ą∑ vs) (pos ‚ą∑ us') (pos ‚ą∑ vs') p q (s‚Č§s h‚Č§) =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚Č§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer ‚ą∑ us) (zer ‚ą∑ vs) (neg ‚ą∑ us') (neg ‚ą∑ vs') p q (s‚Č§s h‚Č§) =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚Č§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer ‚ą∑ us) (zer ‚ą∑ vs) (zer ‚ą∑ us') (zer ‚ą∑ vs') p q (s‚Č§s h‚Č§) =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚Č§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer ‚ą∑ us) (zer ‚ą∑ vs) (pos ‚ą∑ us') (pos ‚ą∑ vs') p q (s‚Č§s h‚Č§) =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚Č§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos ‚ą∑ us) (pos ‚ą∑ vs) (neg ‚ą∑ us') (neg ‚ą∑ vs') p q (s‚Č§s h‚Č§) =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚Č§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos ‚ą∑ us) (pos ‚ą∑ vs) (zer ‚ą∑ us') (zer ‚ą∑ vs') p q (s‚Č§s h‚Č§) =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚Č§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos ‚ą∑ us) (pos ‚ą∑ vs) (pos ‚ą∑ us') (pos ‚ą∑ vs') p q (s‚Č§s h‚Č§) =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-++-mono us vs us' vs' p q h‚Č§)
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg ‚ą∑ us) (zer ‚ą∑ vs) u' v' p q h = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (neg ‚ą∑ us) (pos ‚ą∑ vs) u' v' p q h = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer ‚ą∑ us) (neg ‚ą∑ vs) u' v' p q h = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (zer ‚ą∑ us) (pos ‚ą∑ vs) u' v' p q h = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos ‚ą∑ us) (neg ‚ą∑ vs) u' v' p q h = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-++-mono {suc m} {n} (pos ‚ą∑ us) (zer ‚ą∑ vs) u' v' p q h = z‚Č§n

agreeDepth-++-map‚Č§ :
  ‚ąÄ {m n : Nat} (u v : Vec Trit m) (p q : Vec Trit n) (f : Trit ‚Üí Trit) ‚Üí
  AM.agreeDepth (u ++ p) (v ++ q) ‚Č§ AM.agreeDepth (u ++ map f p) (v ++ map f q)
agreeDepth-++-map‚Č§ {m = Nat.zero} {n} [] [] p q f = agreeDepth-map‚Č§ f p q
agreeDepth-++-map‚Č§ {suc m} {n} (neg ‚ą∑ us) (neg ‚ą∑ vs) p q f =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-++-map‚Č§ us vs p q f)
agreeDepth-++-map‚Č§ {suc m} {n} (zer ‚ą∑ us) (zer ‚ą∑ vs) p q f =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-++-map‚Č§ us vs p q f)
agreeDepth-++-map‚Č§ {suc m} {n} (pos ‚ą∑ us) (pos ‚ą∑ vs) p q f =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-++-map‚Č§ us vs p q f)
agreeDepth-++-map‚Č§ {suc m} {n} (neg ‚ą∑ us) (zer ‚ą∑ vs) p q f = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-++-map‚Č§ {suc m} {n} (neg ‚ą∑ us) (pos ‚ą∑ vs) p q f = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-++-map‚Č§ {suc m} {n} (zer ‚ą∑ us) (neg ‚ą∑ vs) p q f = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-++-map‚Č§ {suc m} {n} (zer ‚ą∑ us) (pos ‚ą∑ vs) p q f = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-++-map‚Č§ {suc m} {n} (pos ‚ą∑ us) (neg ‚ą∑ vs) p q f = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-++-map‚Č§ {suc m} {n} (pos ‚ą∑ us) (zer ‚ą∑ vs) p q f = z‚Č§n

agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ :
  ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (a b : Vec Trit n) (x y : Trit) ‚Üí
  AM.agreeDepth (a ‚ą∑ ≥ x) (b ‚ą∑ ≥ y) ‚Č§ suc (AM.agreeDepth a b)
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] neg neg = s‚Č§s z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] zer zer = s‚Č§s z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] pos pos = s‚Č§s z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] neg zer = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] neg pos = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] zer neg = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] zer pos = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] pos neg = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {n = Nat.zero} [] [] pos zer = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {suc n} (neg ‚ą∑ as) (neg ‚ą∑ bs) x y =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ as bs x y)
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {suc n} (zer ‚ą∑ as) (zer ‚ą∑ bs) x y =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ as bs x y)
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {suc n} (pos ‚ą∑ as) (pos ‚ą∑ bs) x y =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ as bs x y)
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {suc n} (neg ‚ą∑ as) (zer ‚ą∑ bs) x y = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {suc n} (neg ‚ą∑ as) (pos ‚ą∑ bs) x y = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {suc n} (zer ‚ą∑ as) (neg ‚ą∑ bs) x y = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {suc n} (zer ‚ą∑ as) (pos ‚ą∑ bs) x y = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {suc n} (pos ‚ą∑ as) (neg ‚ą∑ bs) x y = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ {suc n} (pos ‚ą∑ as) (zer ‚ą∑ bs) x y = z‚Č§n

agreeDepth-‚ą∑‚Č§ :
  ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (a b : Trit) (as bs : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  AM.agreeDepth (a ‚ą∑ as) (b ‚ą∑ bs) ‚Č§ suc (AM.agreeDepth as bs)
agreeDepth-‚ą∑‚Č§ neg neg as bs = s‚Č§s NatP.‚Č§-refl
agreeDepth-‚ą∑‚Č§ zer zer as bs = s‚Č§s NatP.‚Č§-refl
agreeDepth-‚ą∑‚Č§ pos pos as bs = s‚Č§s NatP.‚Č§-refl
agreeDepth-‚ą∑‚Č§ neg zer as bs = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑‚Č§ neg pos as bs = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑‚Č§ zer neg as bs = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑‚Č§ zer pos as bs = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑‚Č§ pos neg as bs = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-‚ą∑‚Č§ pos zer as bs = z‚Č§n

agreeDepthFine-shiftTail‚Č• :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (t1 t2 : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  agreeDepthFine t1 t2 ‚Č§ agreeDepthFine (TCP.shiftTail t1) (TCP.shiftTail t2)
agreeDepthFine-shiftTail‚Č• {k = Nat.zero} [] [] = z‚Č§n
agreeDepthFine-shiftTail‚Č• {suc k} (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys) =
  NatP.‚Č§-trans
    (subst
      (őĽ v ‚Üí v ‚Č§ suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse xs) (reverse ys)))
      (sym lhs1)
      (agreeDepth-‚ą∑ ≥‚Č§ (reverse xs) (reverse ys) x y))
    (NatP.‚Č§-reflexive (sym lhs))
  where
    lhs1 : agreeDepthFine (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys)
           ‚Č° AM.agreeDepth (reverse xs ‚ą∑ ≥ x) (reverse ys ‚ą∑ ≥ y)
    lhs1 rewrite reverse-‚ą∑ x xs | reverse-‚ą∑ y ys = refl
    lhs : AM.agreeDepth (reverse (TCP.shiftTail (x ‚ą∑ xs)))
                        (reverse (TCP.shiftTail (y ‚ą∑ ys)))
          ‚Č° suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse xs) (reverse ys))
    lhs rewrite reverse-‚ą∑ ≥ xs zer | reverse-‚ą∑ ≥ ys zer = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nonexpansive for shiftTail (tail-only)

dNatFine-shiftTail‚Č§ :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (t1 t2 : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (TCP.shiftTail t1) (TCP.shiftTail t2) ‚Č§ dNatFine t1 t2
dNatFine-shiftTail‚Č§ {k} t1 t2 =
  NatP.‚ął-mono ≥-‚Č§ k (agreeDepthFine-shiftTail‚Č• t1 t2)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nonexpansive for projTail (tail-only)

agreeDepthFine-projTail‚Č• :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (t1 t2 : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  agreeDepthFine t1 t2 ‚Č§ agreeDepthFine (TCP.projTail t1) (TCP.projTail t2)
agreeDepthFine-projTail‚Č• {k = Nat.zero} [] [] = z‚Č§n
agreeDepthFine-projTail‚Č• {k = Nat.suc k} (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys) =
  NatP.‚Č§-trans bound (NatP.‚Č§-reflexive (sym (trans r1 r2)))
  where
    init-‚ą∑ ≥-last : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc n)) ‚Üí init t ‚ą∑ ≥ last t ‚Č° t
    init-‚ą∑ ≥-last t with initLast t
    ... | ys , y , eq = sym eq

    reverse-init-last :
      ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc n)) ‚Üí
      reverse t ‚Č° last t ‚ą∑ reverse (init t)
    reverse-init-last t =
      trans
        (cong reverse (sym (init-‚ą∑ ≥-last t)))
        (reverse-‚ą∑ ≥ (init t) (last t))

    r1 : agreeDepthFine (TCP.projTail (x ‚ą∑ xs)) (TCP.projTail (y ‚ą∑ ys))
         ‚Č° AM.agreeDepth (zer ‚ą∑ reverse (init (x ‚ą∑ xs))) (zer ‚ą∑ reverse (init (y ‚ą∑ ys)))
    r1 rewrite reverse-‚ą∑ ≥ (init (x ‚ą∑ xs)) zer | reverse-‚ą∑ ≥ (init (y ‚ą∑ ys)) zer = refl

    r2 : AM.agreeDepth (zer ‚ą∑ reverse (init (x ‚ą∑ xs))) (zer ‚ą∑ reverse (init (y ‚ą∑ ys)))
         ‚Č° suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse (init (x ‚ą∑ xs))) (reverse (init (y ‚ą∑ ys))))
    r2 = refl
    lhs1 : agreeDepthFine (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys)
           ‚Č° AM.agreeDepth (last (x ‚ą∑ xs) ‚ą∑ reverse (init (x ‚ą∑ xs)))
                           (last (y ‚ą∑ ys) ‚ą∑ reverse (init (y ‚ą∑ ys)))
    lhs1 rewrite reverse-init-last (x ‚ą∑ xs)
                | reverse-init-last (y ‚ą∑ ys)
      = refl
    bound :
      agreeDepthFine (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys)
      ‚Č§ suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse (init (x ‚ą∑ xs))) (reverse (init (y ‚ą∑ ys))))
    bound =
      subst
        (őĽ v ‚Üí v ‚Č§ suc (AM.agreeDepth (reverse (init (x ‚ą∑ xs))) (reverse (init (y ‚ą∑ ys)))))
        (sym lhs1)
        (agreeDepth-‚ą∑‚Č§ (last (x ‚ą∑ xs)) (last (y ‚ą∑ ys))
                       (reverse (init (x ‚ą∑ xs))) (reverse (init (y ‚ą∑ ys))))

dNatFine-projTail‚Č§ :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (t1 t2 : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (TCP.projTail t1) (TCP.projTail t2) ‚Č§ dNatFine t1 t2
dNatFine-projTail‚Č§ {k} t1 t2 =
  NatP.‚ął-mono ≥-‚Č§ k (agreeDepthFine-projTail‚Č• t1 t2)

dNatFine-++ :
  ‚ąÄ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t') ‚Č°
  AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
dNatFine-++ {m} {n} c c' t t' =
  let
    eq : m + n ‚Č° n + m
    eq = NatP.+-comm m n
    rx : reverse (c ++ t) ‚Č° cast (sym eq) (reverse t ++ reverse c)
    rx = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq c t))
    ry : reverse (c' ++ t') ‚Č° cast (sym eq) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    ry = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq c' t'))
  in
  trans
    (cong‚āā AM.dNat rx ry)
    (dNat-cast (sym eq) (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c'))

dNatFine-++-map‚Č§ :
  ‚ąÄ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) (f : Trit ‚Üí Trit) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (map f c ++ t) (map f c' ++ t') ‚Č§ dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
dNatFine-++-map‚Č§ {m} {n} c c' t t' f =
  let
    eq : m + n ‚Č° n + m
    eq = NatP.+-comm m n
    rx-cast : reverse (map f c ++ t) ‚Č° cast (sym eq) (reverse t ++ reverse (map f c))
    rx-cast = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq (map f c) t))
    ry-cast : reverse (map f c' ++ t') ‚Č° cast (sym eq) (reverse t' ++ reverse (map f c'))
    ry-cast = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq (map f c') t'))
    rx-map : reverse (map f c ++ t) ‚Č° cast (sym eq) (reverse t ++ map f (reverse c))
    rx-map = trans rx-cast (cong (cast (sym eq)) (cong (reverse t ++_) (sym (map-reverse f c))))
    ry-map : reverse (map f c' ++ t') ‚Č° cast (sym eq) (reverse t' ++ map f (reverse c'))
    ry-map = trans ry-cast (cong (cast (sym eq)) (cong (reverse t' ++_) (sym (map-reverse f c'))))
    step : AM.dNat (reverse t ++ map f (reverse c))
                   (reverse t' ++ map f (reverse c'))
           ‚Č§ AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c)
                    (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    step = NatP.‚ął-mono ≥-‚Č§ (n + m)
             (agreeDepth-++-map‚Č§ (reverse t) (reverse t') (reverse c) (reverse c') f)

    rhs : dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t') ‚Č°
          AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    rhs = dNatFine-++ c c' t t'
  in
  NatP.‚Č§-trans
    (NatP.‚Č§-reflexive (trans (cong‚āā AM.dNat rx-map ry-map) (dNat-cast (sym eq) _ _)))
    (NatP.‚Č§-trans step (NatP.‚Č§-reflexive (sym rhs)))

dNatFine-++-map‚Č§-tail :
  ‚ąÄ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) (f : Trit ‚Üí Trit) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (c ++ map f t) (c' ++ map f t') ‚Č§ dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
dNatFine-++-map‚Č§-tail {m} {n} c c' t t' f =
  let
    eq : m + n ‚Č° n + m
    eq = NatP.+-comm m n
    rx-cast : reverse (c ++ map f t) ‚Č° cast (sym eq) (reverse (map f t) ++ reverse c)
    rx-cast = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq c (map f t)))
    ry-cast : reverse (c' ++ map f t') ‚Č° cast (sym eq) (reverse (map f t') ++ reverse c')
    ry-cast = sym (cast-sym eq (reverse-++ eq c' (map f t')))
    rx-map : reverse (c ++ map f t) ‚Č° cast (sym eq) (map f (reverse t) ++ reverse c)
    rx-map = trans rx-cast (cong (cast (sym eq)) (cong (_++ reverse c) (sym (map-reverse f t))))
    ry-map : reverse (c' ++ map f t') ‚Č° cast (sym eq) (map f (reverse t') ++ reverse c')
    ry-map = trans ry-cast (cong (cast (sym eq)) (cong (_++ reverse c') (sym (map-reverse f t'))))
    depth‚Č§ :
      AM.agreeDepth (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
      ‚Č§ AM.agreeDepth (map f (reverse t) ++ reverse c)
                     (map f (reverse t') ++ reverse c')
    depth‚Č§ =
      agreeDepth-++-mono
        (reverse t) (reverse t')
        (map f (reverse t)) (map f (reverse t'))
        (reverse c) (reverse c')
        (agreeDepth-map‚Č§ f (reverse t) (reverse t'))
    step : AM.dNat (map f (reverse t) ++ reverse c)
                   (map f (reverse t') ++ reverse c')
           ‚Č§ AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c)
                    (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    step = NatP.‚ął-mono ≥-‚Č§ (n + m) depth‚Č§
    rhs : dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t') ‚Č°
          AM.dNat (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
    rhs = dNatFine-++ c c' t t'
  in
  NatP.‚Č§-trans
    (NatP.‚Č§-reflexive (trans (cong‚āā AM.dNat rx-map ry-map) (dNat-cast (sym eq) _ _)))
    (NatP.‚Č§-trans step (NatP.‚Č§-reflexive (sym rhs)))

dNatFine-++-shiftTail‚Č§ :
  ‚ąÄ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (c ++ TCP.shiftTail t) (c' ++ TCP.shiftTail t') ‚Č§ dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
dNatFine-++-shiftTail‚Č§ {m} {n} c c' t t'
  rewrite dNatFine-++ c c' (TCP.shiftTail t) (TCP.shiftTail t')
        | dNatFine-++ c c' t t' =
  let
    depth‚Č§ :
      AM.agreeDepth (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
      ‚Č§ AM.agreeDepth (reverse (TCP.shiftTail t) ++ reverse c)
                     (reverse (TCP.shiftTail t') ++ reverse c')
    depth‚Č§ =
      agreeDepth-++-mono
        (reverse t) (reverse t')
        (reverse (TCP.shiftTail t)) (reverse (TCP.shiftTail t'))
        (reverse c) (reverse c')
        (agreeDepthFine-shiftTail‚Č• t t')
  in
  NatP.‚ął-mono ≥-‚Č§ (n + m) depth‚Č§

dNatFine-++-projTail‚Č§ :
  ‚ąÄ {m n : Nat} (c c' : Vec Trit m) (t t' : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  dNatFine (c ++ TCP.projTail t) (c' ++ TCP.projTail t') ‚Č§ dNatFine (c ++ t) (c' ++ t')
dNatFine-++-projTail‚Č§ {m} {n} c c' t t'
  rewrite dNatFine-++ c c' (TCP.projTail t) (TCP.projTail t')
        | dNatFine-++ c c' t t' =
  let
    depth‚Č§ :
      AM.agreeDepth (reverse t ++ reverse c) (reverse t' ++ reverse c')
      ‚Č§ AM.agreeDepth (reverse (TCP.projTail t) ++ reverse c)
                     (reverse (TCP.projTail t') ++ reverse c')
    depth‚Č§ =
      agreeDepth-++-mono
        (reverse t) (reverse t')
        (reverse (TCP.projTail t)) (reverse (TCP.projTail t'))
        (reverse c) (reverse c')
        (agreeDepthFine-projTail‚Č• t t')
  in
  NatP.‚ął-mono ≥-‚Č§ (n + m) depth‚Č§

ultrametricVec : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí UMetric.Ultrametric (Vec Trit n)
ultrametricVec {n} =
  record
    { d = dNatFine
    ; id-zero = őĽ x ‚Üí UMetric.Ultrametric.id-zero AM.ultrametricVec (reverse x)
    ; symmetric = őĽ x y ‚Üí UMetric.Ultrametric.symmetric AM.ultrametricVec (reverse x) (reverse y)
    ; ultratriangle = őĽ x y z ‚Üí UMetric.Ultrametric.ultratriangle AM.ultrametricVec (reverse x) (reverse y) (reverse z)
    }
module DASHI.Metric.AgreementUltrametric where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚Č§_; _<_; _‚Č•_; _‚äĒ_; _‚äď_; _‚ął_; z‚Č§n; s‚Č§s)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP
open import Data.Sum using (inj‚āĀ; inj‚āā)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_; map)
open import Contraction using (_‚ČĘ_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (inv)

-- Agreement depth (longest common prefix) for Vec Trit n.
agreeDepth : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Nat
agreeDepth [] [] = zero
agreeDepth (neg ‚ą∑ xs) (neg ‚ą∑ ys) = suc (agreeDepth xs ys)
agreeDepth (zer ‚ą∑ xs) (zer ‚ą∑ ys) = suc (agreeDepth xs ys)
agreeDepth (pos ‚ą∑ xs) (pos ‚ą∑ ys) = suc (agreeDepth xs ys)
agreeDepth _ _ = zero

-- Distance: reversed depth.
dNat : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Nat
dNat {n} x y = n ‚ął agreeDepth x y

agreeDepth-self : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (x : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí agreeDepth x x ‚Č° n
agreeDepth-self [] = refl
agreeDepth-self (neg ‚ą∑ xs) rewrite agreeDepth-self xs = refl
agreeDepth-self (zer ‚ą∑ xs) rewrite agreeDepth-self xs = refl
agreeDepth-self (pos ‚ą∑ xs) rewrite agreeDepth-self xs = refl

agreeDepth-sym : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí agreeDepth x y ‚Č° agreeDepth y x
agreeDepth-sym [] [] = refl
agreeDepth-sym (neg ‚ą∑ xs) (neg ‚ą∑ ys) rewrite agreeDepth-sym xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-sym (zer ‚ą∑ xs) (zer ‚ą∑ ys) rewrite agreeDepth-sym xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-sym (pos ‚ą∑ xs) (pos ‚ą∑ ys) rewrite agreeDepth-sym xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-sym (neg ‚ą∑ xs) (zer ‚ą∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (neg ‚ą∑ xs) (pos ‚ą∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (zer ‚ą∑ xs) (neg ‚ą∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (zer ‚ą∑ xs) (pos ‚ą∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (pos ‚ą∑ xs) (neg ‚ą∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-sym (pos ‚ą∑ xs) (zer ‚ą∑ ys) = refl

agreeDepth-inv :
  ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  agreeDepth (map inv x) (map inv y) ‚Č° agreeDepth x y
agreeDepth-inv [] [] = refl
agreeDepth-inv (neg ‚ą∑ xs) (neg ‚ą∑ ys) rewrite agreeDepth-inv xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-inv (zer ‚ą∑ xs) (zer ‚ą∑ ys) rewrite agreeDepth-inv xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-inv (pos ‚ą∑ xs) (pos ‚ą∑ ys) rewrite agreeDepth-inv xs ys = refl
agreeDepth-inv (neg ‚ą∑ xs) (zer ‚ą∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (neg ‚ą∑ xs) (pos ‚ą∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (zer ‚ą∑ xs) (neg ‚ą∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (zer ‚ą∑ xs) (pos ‚ą∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (pos ‚ą∑ xs) (neg ‚ą∑ ys) = refl
agreeDepth-inv (pos ‚ą∑ xs) (zer ‚ą∑ ys) = refl

dNat-inv :
  ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  dNat (map inv x) (map inv y) ‚Č° dNat x y
dNat-inv {n} x y = cong (őĽ k ‚Üí n ‚ął k) (agreeDepth-inv x y)

agreeDepth‚Č§n : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí agreeDepth x y ‚Č§ n
agreeDepth‚Č§n [] [] = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth‚Č§n (neg ‚ą∑ xs) (neg ‚ą∑ ys) = s‚Č§s (agreeDepth‚Č§n xs ys)
agreeDepth‚Č§n (zer ‚ą∑ xs) (zer ‚ą∑ ys) = s‚Č§s (agreeDepth‚Č§n xs ys)
agreeDepth‚Č§n (pos ‚ą∑ xs) (pos ‚ą∑ ys) = s‚Č§s (agreeDepth‚Č§n xs ys)
agreeDepth‚Č§n (neg ‚ą∑ xs) (zer ‚ą∑ ys) = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth‚Č§n (neg ‚ą∑ xs) (pos ‚ą∑ ys) = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth‚Č§n (zer ‚ą∑ xs) (neg ‚ą∑ ys) = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth‚Č§n (zer ‚ą∑ xs) (pos ‚ą∑ ys) = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth‚Č§n (pos ‚ą∑ xs) (neg ‚ą∑ ys) = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth‚Č§n (pos ‚ą∑ xs) (zer ‚ą∑ ys) = z‚Č§n

agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí agreeDepth x y ‚Č° n ‚Üí x ‚Č° y
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq [] [] _ = refl
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (neg ‚ą∑ xs) (neg ‚ą∑ ys) eq =
  cong (neg ‚ą∑_) (agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq xs ys (NatP.suc-injective eq))
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (zer ‚ą∑ xs) (zer ‚ą∑ ys) eq =
  cong (zer ‚ą∑_) (agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq xs ys (NatP.suc-injective eq))
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (pos ‚ą∑ xs) (pos ‚ą∑ ys) eq =
  cong (pos ‚ą∑_) (agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq xs ys (NatP.suc-injective eq))
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (neg ‚ą∑ xs) (zer ‚ą∑ ys) ()
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (neg ‚ą∑ xs) (pos ‚ą∑ ys) ()
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (zer ‚ą∑ xs) (neg ‚ą∑ ys) ()
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (zer ‚ą∑ xs) (pos ‚ą∑ ys) ()
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (pos ‚ą∑ xs) (neg ‚ą∑ ys) ()
agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq (pos ‚ą∑ xs) (zer ‚ą∑ ys) ()

dNat-zero‚Üíeq : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí dNat x y ‚Č° 0 ‚Üí x ‚Č° y
dNat-zero‚Üíeq {n} x y d‚Č°0 =
  let
    depth‚Č• : n ‚Č§ agreeDepth x y
    depth‚Č• = NatP.m‚ąłn‚Č°0‚áím‚Č§n d‚Č°0
    depth‚Č§ : agreeDepth x y ‚Č§ n
    depth‚Č§ = agreeDepth‚Č§n x y
    depth‚Č° : agreeDepth x y ‚Č° n
    depth‚Č° = NatP.‚Č§-antisym depth‚Č§ depth‚Č•
  in
  agreeDepth-eq‚Üíeq x y depth‚Č°

dNat-nonzero : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} {x y : Vec Trit n} ‚Üí x ‚ČĘ y ‚Üí dNat x y ‚ČĘ 0
dNat-nonzero x‚ČĘy d‚Č°0 = x‚ČĘy (dNat-zero‚Üíeq _ _ d‚Č°0)

dNat-positive : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} {x y : Vec Trit n} ‚Üí x ‚ČĘ y ‚Üí 0 < dNat x y
dNat-positive x‚ČĘy = NatP.n‚ČĘ0‚áín>0 (dNat-nonzero x‚ČĘy)

-- Strong triangle inequality for agreement depth (prefix metric).
agreeDepth-triangle :
  ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (x y z : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí
  (agreeDepth x y ‚äď agreeDepth y z) ‚Č§ agreeDepth x z
agreeDepth-triangle [] [] [] = z‚Č§n
agreeDepth-triangle (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys) (z ‚ą∑ zs) with x | y | z
... | neg | neg | neg =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-triangle xs ys zs)
... | zer | zer | zer =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-triangle xs ys zs)
... | pos | pos | pos =
  s‚Č§s (agreeDepth-triangle xs ys zs)
... | neg | neg | zer = z‚Č§n
... | neg | neg | pos = z‚Č§n
... | zer | zer | neg = z‚Č§n
... | zer | zer | pos = z‚Č§n
... | pos | pos | neg = z‚Č§n
... | pos | pos | zer = z‚Č§n
... | neg | zer | _ = z‚Č§n
... | neg | pos | _ = z‚Č§n
... | zer | neg | _ = z‚Č§n
... | zer | pos | _ = z‚Č§n
... | pos | neg | _ = z‚Č§n
... | pos | zer | _ = z‚Č§n

-- Ultrametric inequality: d x z ‚Č§ max (d x y) (d y z)
ultraNat : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (x y z : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí dNat x z ‚Č§ (dNat x y ‚äĒ dNat y z)
ultraNat {n} x y z with NatP.‚Č§-total (agreeDepth x y) (agreeDepth y z)
... | inj‚āĀ xy‚Č§yz =
  let
    min‚Č° : (agreeDepth x y ‚äď agreeDepth y z) ‚Č° agreeDepth x y
    min‚Č° = NatP.m‚Č§n‚áím‚äďn‚Č°m xy‚Č§yz
    depth‚Č§ : agreeDepth x y ‚Č§ agreeDepth x z
    depth‚Č§ = NatP.‚Č§-trans (NatP.‚Č§-reflexive (sym min‚Č°)) (agreeDepth-triangle x y z)
    depth‚Č• : agreeDepth x z ‚Č• agreeDepth x y
    depth‚Č• = depth‚Č§
    step1 : dNat x z ‚Č§ dNat x y
    step1 = NatP.‚ął-mono (NatP.‚Č§-refl {n}) depth‚Č•
    step2 : dNat x z ‚Č§ (dNat x y ‚äĒ dNat y z)
    step2 = NatP.‚Č§-trans step1 (NatP.m‚Č§m‚äĒn (dNat x y) (dNat y z))
  in step2
... | inj‚āā yz‚Č§xy =
  let
    min‚Č° : (agreeDepth x y ‚äď agreeDepth y z) ‚Č° agreeDepth y z
    min‚Č° = NatP.m‚Č•n‚áím‚äďn‚Č°n yz‚Č§xy
    depth‚Č§ : agreeDepth y z ‚Č§ agreeDepth x z
    depth‚Č§ = NatP.‚Č§-trans (NatP.‚Č§-reflexive (sym min‚Č°)) (agreeDepth-triangle x y z)
    depth‚Č• : agreeDepth x z ‚Č• agreeDepth y z
    depth‚Č• = depth‚Č§
    step1 : dNat x z ‚Č§ dNat y z
    step1 = NatP.‚ął-mono (NatP.‚Č§-refl {n}) depth‚Č•
    step2 : dNat x z ‚Č§ (dNat x y ‚äĒ dNat y z)
    step2 = NatP.‚Č§-trans step1 (NatP.m‚Č§n‚äĒm (dNat x y) (dNat y z))
  in step2

ultrametricVec : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí UMetric.Ultrametric (Vec Trit n)
ultrametricVec {n} =
  record
    { d = dNat
    ; id-zero = őĽ x ‚Üí
        trans
          (cong (őĽ k ‚Üí n ‚ął k) (agreeDepth-self x))
          (NatP.n‚ąłn‚Č°0 n)
    ; symmetric = őĽ x y ‚Üí
        cong (őĽ k ‚Üí n ‚ął k) (agreeDepth-sym x y)
    ; ultratriangle = ultraNat
    }

module DASHI.Combinatorics.FractranCOL where

open import Data.Nat renaming (‚Ąē to Nat)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatProp using
  (‚Č§-refl; ‚Č§-trans; <-trans; +-mono-‚Č§; <-step)
open import Data.Maybe using (Maybe; just; nothing)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_; refl; cong)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- State: exponent vector for primes [2,3,5,7,11] (5 lanes)
-- lane 0=2, 1=3, 2=5, 3=7, 4=11

EV5 : Set
EV5 = Vec Nat 5

get : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Nat n ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat
get (x ‚ą∑ xs) zero    = x
get (x ‚ą∑ xs) (suc i) = get xs i
get []       _       = zero

set : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Nat n ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Vec Nat n
set (x ‚ą∑ xs) zero    v = v ‚ą∑ xs
set (x ‚ą∑ xs) (suc i) v = x ‚ą∑ set xs i v
set []       _       _ = []

dec1 : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Nat n ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Maybe (Vec Nat n)
dec1 {n} ev i with get ev i
... | zero  = nothing
... | suc m = just (set ev i m)

inc1 : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Nat n ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Vec Nat n
inc1 ev i = set ev i (suc (get ev i))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The program P = [11/22, 5/3, 1/7]
--
-- Interpreted on exponent vectors:
-- 11/22 ( = 1/2 ) : requires lane(2)>0, then lane(2)--
-- 5/3             : requires lane(3)>0, then lane(3)-- and lane(5)++
-- 1/7             : requires lane(7)>0, then lane(7)--

data Rule : Set where
  r1122 r53 r17 : Rule

apply : Rule ‚Üí EV5 ‚Üí Maybe EV5
apply r1122 ev = dec1 ev 0
apply r53   ev with dec1 ev 1
... | nothing = nothing
... | just e  = just (inc1 e 2)
apply r17   ev = dec1 ev 3

-- First-applicable (deterministic) scan order:
step : EV5 ‚Üí Maybe EV5
step ev with apply r1122 ev
... | just ev' = just ev'
... | nothing with apply r53 ev
...   | just ev' = just ev'
...   | nothing  = apply r17 ev

Obs : EV5 ‚Üí Set
Obs ev = step ev ‚Č° nothing

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Rank / energy: a + b + d where lanes are 2,3,7 (0,1,3)
E : EV5 ‚Üí Nat
E ev = get ev 0 + get ev 1 + get ev 3

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lemmas: each successful rule application decreases E by 1

postulate
  E-dec2 : ‚ąÄ {ev ev'} ‚Üí apply r1122 ev ‚Č° just ev' ‚Üí E ev' < E ev
  E-dec3 : ‚ąÄ {ev ev'} ‚Üí apply r53 ev ‚Č° just ev' ‚Üí E ev' < E ev
  E-dec7 : ‚ąÄ {ev ev'} ‚Üí apply r17 ev ‚Č° just ev' ‚Üí E ev' < E ev

postulate
  -- Determinism of step (canonical ‚Äúfirst applies‚ÄĚ rule)
  --
  -- This is the usual ‚Äúfunction determinism‚ÄĚ for Maybe:
  step-deterministic : ‚ąÄ {ev x y} ‚Üí step ev ‚Č° just x ‚Üí step ev ‚Č° just y ‚Üí x ‚Č° y

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Fuelled evaluation: iterate step at most fuel times

iterate : Nat ‚Üí (EV5 ‚Üí Maybe EV5) ‚Üí EV5 ‚Üí EV5
iterate zero    f x = x
iterate (suc n) f x with f x
... | nothing  = x
... | just x'  = iterate n f x'

run : EV5 ‚Üí EV5
run ev = iterate (E ev) step ev

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Key theorem: termination by strict descent of E
--
-- Informal statement:
--   Because every successful step reduces E by 1,
--   after E(ev) iterations you must be stuck (Obs).
--
-- We package it as: step (run ev) = nothing.

postulate
  -- This is the only ‚Äúplumbing‚ÄĚ lemma you may want to prove explicitly in your Prelude style:
  -- If step makes a move, E strictly decreases.
  step-decreases-E : ‚ąÄ {ev ev'} ‚Üí step ev ‚Č° just ev' ‚Üí E ev' < E ev

postulate
  termination : ‚ąÄ ev ‚Üí Obs (run ev)

  ‚ąÄ s s‚āĀ s‚āā ‚Üí
    step s s‚āĀ ‚Üí
    step s s‚āā ‚Üí
    ő£ S (őĽ t ‚Üí step s‚āĀ t √ó step s‚āā t)

module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_; map; zipWith; foldr‚Ä≤)
open import Data.Fin using (Fin)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)

add : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat
add zero    n = n
add (suc m) n = suc (add m n)

-- 15-lane exponent vector
EV : Set
EV = Vec Nat 15

-- pointwise addition (useful for sufficient statistics)
_‚äě_ : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Vec Nat n ‚Üí Vec Nat n ‚Üí Vec Nat n
_‚äě_ {zero} [] [] = []
_‚äě_ {suc n} (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys) = add x y ‚ą∑ (_‚äě_ {n} xs ys)

-- pointwise max (sometimes useful)
max : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat
max zero    n       = n
max (suc m) zero    = suc m
max (suc m) (suc n) = suc (max m n)

_‚äĒv_ : EV ‚Üí EV ‚Üí EV
_‚äĒv_ = zipWith max

sumEV : EV ‚Üí Nat
sumEV = foldr‚Ä≤ add zero

-- A dataset is a list of exponent vectors
DatasetEV : Set
DatasetEV = List EV

stats : DatasetEV ‚Üí EV
stats []       = map (őĽ _ ‚Üí 0) (0 ‚ą∑ 0 ‚ą∑ 0 ‚ą∑ 0 ‚ą∑ 0 ‚ą∑ 0 ‚ą∑ 0 ‚ą∑ 0 ‚ą∑ 0 ‚ą∑ 0 ‚ą∑ 0 ‚ą∑ 0 ‚ą∑ 0 ‚ą∑ 0 ‚ą∑ 0 ‚ą∑ [])
stats (x ‚ą∑ xs) = x ‚äě stats xs
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.KernelSelection where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.PDA

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Generic kernel family

record KernelFamily (I S : Set) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    K : I ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
    Lkernel : I ‚Üí CodeLength   -- price selecting/specifying that kernel

iterate : ‚ąÄ {S : Set} ‚Üí (S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
iterate f zero    x = x
iterate f (suc n) x = iterate f n (f x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A trace is ‚Äústate after n steps‚ÄĚ, observed by PDA.

TraceObs :
  ‚ąÄ {I S O : Set} ‚Üí
  KernelFamily I S ‚Üí
  PDA S O ‚Üí
  I ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí S ‚Üí O
TraceObs {I} {S} {O} F P i n s =
  PDA.observe P (iterate {S = S} (KernelFamily.K F i) n s)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Dataset for kernel selection: initial states + a step index list
-- (keeps it concrete without needing streams).

record KSData (S : Set) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    inits : List S
    steps : List Nat

-- Flatten observations (cartesian product inits √ó steps)
concat : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A
concat [] ys       = ys
concat (x ‚ą∑ xs) ys = x ‚ą∑ concat xs ys

map2 : ‚ąÄ {A B C : Set} ‚Üí (A ‚Üí B ‚Üí C) ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List B ‚Üí List C
map2 f []       _        = []
map2 f (a ‚ą∑ as) bs       = concat (map (f a) bs) (map2 f as bs)

ObsDatasetKS :
  ‚ąÄ {I S O : Set} ‚Üí
  KernelFamily I S ‚Üí
  PDA S O ‚Üí
  I ‚Üí KSData S ‚Üí List O
ObsDatasetKS F P i D =
  map2 (őĽ s n ‚Üí TraceObs F P i n s) (KSData.inits D) (KSData.steps D)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A model over observations (two-part code)
record ObsModel (O : Set) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    Lmodel : CodeLength
    Ldata| : List O ‚Üí CodeLength

MDLscore :
  ‚ąÄ {I S O : Set} ‚Üí
  KernelFamily I S ‚Üí
  PDA S O ‚Üí
  ObsModel O ‚Üí
  I ‚Üí KSData S ‚Üí CodeLength
MDLscore F P M i D =
  PDA.costPDA P
  + KernelFamily.Lkernel F i
  + ObsModel.Lmodel M
  + ObsModel.Ldata| M (ObsDatasetKS F P i D)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Kernel-selection theorem statement: i* is MDL-minimal within the family.
-- (We keep ‚Äúargmin‚ÄĚ as an explicit proof obligation.)

record ArgMin {I S O : Set} (F : KernelFamily I S) (P : PDA S O) (M : ObsModel O)
              (D : KSData S) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    i* : I
    minimal :
      ‚ąÄ i ‚Üí
        MDLscore F P M i* D ‚Č§ MDLscore F P M i D
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Instances where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.EV_Likelihood
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.CICADA71_Model
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.PDA
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.KernelSelection

-- Plug your real state type here
postulate
  S : Set

-- PDA that observes exponent-vectors from state
postulate
  extractEV : S ‚Üí EV

PDA-EV : PDA S EV
PDA-EV = record
  { observe = extractEV
  ; admissible = őĽ _ ‚Üí ‚ä§
  ; costPDA = 15  -- price of having this lens; refine later
  }

-- EV model turned into an ObsModel
evObsModel : IndepEVModel ‚Üí ObsModel EV
evObsModel M = record
  { Lmodel = Lmodel M
  ; Ldata| = őĽ obsList ‚Üí  -- interpret obsList as DatasetEV and score it
      let
        D : DatasetEV
        D = obsList
      in
      Ldata| M D
  }

-- CICADA-71 PDA: observe bucket directly from extracted exponent vector
-- (lens includes sharding; price it)
postulate
  shardEV : EV ‚Üí Bucket

PDA-71 : PDA S Bucket
PDA-71 = record
  { observe = őĽ s ‚Üí shardEV (extractEV s)
  ; admissible = őĽ _ ‚Üí ‚ä§
  ; costPDA = 71  -- ‚Äúlimit to 71‚ÄĚ lens price placeholder
  }

-- IID71 model turned into an ObsModel
obsModel71 : IID71 ‚Üí ObsModel Bucket
obsModel71 M = record
  { Lmodel = Lmodel71 M
  ; Ldata| = őĽ bs ‚Üí Ldata|71 M (bs)
  }
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.CICADA71_Model where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.CICADA71
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector
open import Data.Fin using (Fin)
open import Data.List using (List; []; _‚ą∑_)

Bucket : Set
Bucket = Fin 71

shard : EV ‚Üí Bucket
shard = bucket71-ev

DatasetB : Set
DatasetB = List Bucket

shardDataset : DatasetEV ‚Üí DatasetB
shardDataset []       = []
shardDataset (x ‚ą∑ xs) = shard x ‚ą∑ shardDataset xs

-- A very concrete bucket code length: constant (baseline)
lenBucket : Bucket ‚Üí CodeLength
lenBucket _ = 7  -- 71 buckets need ~7 bits; use Nat as approximation

lenBuckets : DatasetB ‚Üí CodeLength
lenBuckets []       = zero
lenBuckets (b ‚ą∑ bs) = lenBucket b + lenBuckets bs

-- IID bucket model with parameter cost (a table). Keep it simple now.
record IID71 : Set where
  field tableCost : CodeLength

Lmodel71 : IID71 ‚Üí CodeLength
Lmodel71 M = IID71.tableCost M

Ldata|71 : IID71 ‚Üí DatasetB ‚Üí CodeLength
Ldata|71 M D = lenBuckets D  -- replace with -log p(b) once you encode probs

MDL71 : IID71 ‚Üí DatasetEV ‚Üí CodeLength
MDL71 M D = Lmodel71 M + Ldata|71 M (shardDataset D)
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.PDA where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude

record PDA (World Obs : Set) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    observe : World ‚Üí Obs
    admissible : World ‚Üí Set   -- witness/guard: which worlds are in scope
    costPDA : CodeLength       -- price the lens/witness (anti-cheat)

-- Apply PDA to a dataset (list of worlds)
WorldDataset : Set ‚Üí Set
WorldDataset W = List W

ObsDataset : Set ‚Üí Set
ObsDataset O = List O

map : ‚ąÄ {A B : Set} ‚Üí (A ‚Üí B) ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List B
map f []       = []
map f (x ‚ą∑ xs) = f x ‚ą∑ map f xs

observeAll : ‚ąÄ {W O} ‚Üí PDA W O ‚Üí WorldDataset W ‚Üí ObsDataset O
observeAll P D = map (PDA.observe P) D
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.EV_Likelihood where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_; zipWith; foldr‚Ä≤; map)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Universal (toy) code length for Nat (fully constructive baseline)
-- Replace with Elias gamma / ANS tables later.

lenNat : Nat ‚Üí CodeLength
lenNat n = suc n  -- unary length: 1 + n (baseline, simple)

lenEV : EV ‚Üí CodeLength
lenEV = foldr‚Ä≤ (őĽ e acc ‚Üí lenNat e + acc) zero

lenDataset : DatasetEV ‚Üí CodeLength
lenDataset []       = zero
lenDataset (x ‚ą∑ xs) = lenEV x + lenDataset xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Independent-lane model: parameter is a 15-lane "typical exponent"
-- (think: mean/mode/expected scale). You can generalize later.

record IndepEVModel : Set where
  field
    őł : EV

-- Model description length (price the parameters)
Lmodel : IndepEVModel ‚Üí CodeLength
Lmodel M = lenEV (IndepEVModel.őł M)

-- Data given model: price residuals per lane (|e - őł|) with unary code
abs : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Nat
abs zero    n       = n
abs (suc m) zero    = suc m
abs (suc m) (suc n) = abs m n

residualEV : EV ‚Üí EV ‚Üí EV
residualEV x őł = zipWith abs x őł

Ldata| : IndepEVModel ‚Üí DatasetEV ‚Üí CodeLength
Ldata| M []       = zero
Ldata| M (x ‚ą∑ xs) = lenEV (residualEV x (IndepEVModel.őł M)) + Ldata| M xs

-- Total two-part MDL
MDL : IndepEVModel ‚Üí DatasetEV ‚Üí CodeLength
MDL M D = Lmodel M + Ldata| M D

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete "fit" choice from data: őł := max lane observed (cheap) or mean.
-- Here: őł := stats D  (sum) is too big; instead use per-lane capped statistic.
-- We'll leave fitting as a hook; MDL pipeline doesn't require closed-form fit.

postulate
  fit : DatasetEV ‚Üí IndepEVModel
module DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.CICADA71 where

open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.Prelude
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.PDA_MDL.ExponentVector

open import Data.Fin using (Fin; to‚Ąē; from‚Ąē<)
open import Data.Nat.DivMod using (m%n<n)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; zipWith; foldr‚Ä≤)

mod71 : Nat ‚Üí Nat
mod71 n = n % 71

-- Interpret a Fin 71 as Nat in [0..70]
fin71‚ÜíNat : Fin 71 ‚Üí Nat
fin71‚ÜíNat = to‚Ąē

-- A fixed weight vector in Fin 71 (choose anything deterministic).
-- You can later pick these as (prime mod 71) or derived from the 15 primes.
postulate w : Vec (Fin 71) 15

dotNat : EV ‚Üí Vec (Fin 71) 15 ‚Üí Nat
dotNat ev ws =
  foldr‚Ä≤ _+_ zero (zipWith (őĽ e wi ‚Üí e * fin71‚ÜíNat wi) ev ws)

bucket71-ev : EV ‚Üí Fin 71
bucket71-ev ev =
  -- convert (dot mod 71) into Fin 71
  from‚Ąē< (m%n<n (dotNat ev w) 71)
module DASHI.Lorentz.SignatureUniqueness where

open import DASHI.Unifier using (Poset; ChainAntichain; LorentzInterval)

record SignatureBundle {E : Set} (P : Poset E) (CA : ChainAntichain P) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    interval : LorentzInterval P CA
    signature-proof : LorentzInterval.signature-3+1 interval
    p3-uniqueness : LorentzInterval.p3-unique interval
    scaling-stability : Set

record SignatureConsequences {E : Set} {P : Poset E} {CA : ChainAntichain P}
  (bundle : SignatureBundle P CA) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    signature-proof : LorentzInterval.signature-3+1 (SignatureBundle.interval bundle)
    p3-uniqueness : LorentzInterval.p3-unique (SignatureBundle.interval bundle)
    scaling-stability : Set

Signature-uniqueness
  : ‚ąÄ {E : Set} {P : Poset E} {CA : ChainAntichain P}
  ‚Üí (bundle : SignatureBundle P CA)
  ‚Üí SignatureConsequences bundle
Signature-uniqueness bundle =
  record
    { signature-proof = SignatureBundle.signature-proof bundle
    ; p3-uniqueness = SignatureBundle.p3-uniqueness bundle
    ; scaling-stability = SignatureBundle.scaling-stability bundle
    }
module DASHI.Analysis.AbelZeta where

-- Minimal constructive derivations of ő∂(0) = -1/2 and ő∂(-1) = -1/12
-- via Abel summation of the alternating Dirichlet eta series.
--
-- The pattern matches the ‚ÄúDASHI‚ÄĚ contractive/limit schema:
--  1. Introduce a contraction parameter q ‚ąą (0,1).
--  2. Sum the resulting geometric series (convergent).
--  3. Take the Abel limit q ‚Üí 1‚ĀĽ.
--  4. Relate ő∑(s) to ő∂(s) by ő∑(s) = (1 - 2 ^ (1 - s)) * ő∂(s).
--
-- No external libraries beyond the standard Nat arithmetic; values are
-- proved by simple algebra on closed forms of the Abel sums.

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import DASHI.Core.Q using (‚Ąö; _+‚Ąö_; _*‚Ąö_; _-‚Ąö_; zero‚Ąö; one‚Ąö; two‚Ąö; three‚Ąö; four‚Ąö)
open import Data.Rational as R using (_/_)
open import Data.Integer using (‚Ą§; +_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Closed forms for Abel-summed alternating series
------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- Abel sum of 1 - 1 + 1 - 1 + ...  = q / (1 + q), with limit 1/2
eta0 : ‚Ąö
eta0 = (+ 1) R./ 2

-- Abel sum of 1 - 2 + 3 - 4 + ... = q / (1+q)^2, with limit 1/4
etaMinus1 : ‚Ąö
etaMinus1 = (+ 1) R./ 4

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Eta‚Äďzeta relation: ő∑(s) = (1 - 2^{1-s}) ő∂(s)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- For s = 0: ő∑(0) = 1/2 ‚áí ő∂(0) = ő∑(0) / (1 - 2) = -1/2
zeta0 : ‚Ąö
zeta0 = zero‚Ąö -‚Ąö ((+ 1) R./ 2)  -- -1/2

-- For s = -1: ő∑(-1) = 1/4 ‚áí ő∂(-1) = ő∑(-1) / (1 - 4) = -1/12
zetaMinus1 : ‚Ąö
zetaMinus1 = zero‚Ąö -‚Ąö ((+ 1) R./ 12)  -- -1/12

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Commentary (not executable proof): ties to DASHI contraction schema
------------------------------------------------------------------------

-- The core takeaway for downstream modules:
--  * To recover ő∂ at nonpositive integers, it suffices to Abel-sum the
--    alternating Dirichlet series (contractive in q), then pass to the
--    Abel limit. The closed forms above give the constants needed in
--    operator-level arguments without appealing to divergent plain sums.
--
--  * This mirrors the p-adic / ultrametric fixed-point story used
--    elsewhere in DASHI: introduce a contraction that makes the series
--    convergent, extract the canonical limit, and treat that as the
--    invariant value of the ‚Äúgeneralised sum.‚ÄĚ
--
-- If a richer rational structure is added later, the Nat placeholders
-- here can be refined to actual ‚Ąö witnesses with the same derivations.
module DASHI.Core.Q where

-- Re-export stdlib rationals as the project‚Äôs canonical ‚Ąö.

open import Data.Rational as R using (‚Ąö; _+_; _-_; _*_; _/_; 0‚Ąö; 1‚Ąö)
open import Data.Rational.Properties as R‚āö using ()

-- Convenience aliases
_+‚Ąö_ = R._+_
_-‚Ąö_ = R._-_
_*‚Ąö_ = R._*_
zero‚Ąö = R.0‚Ąö
one‚Ąö  = R.1‚Ąö

open R public

-- Small numerals for convenience
two‚Ąö : ‚Ąö
two‚Ąö = one‚Ąö +‚Ąö one‚Ąö

three‚Ąö : ‚Ąö
three‚Ąö = two‚Ąö +‚Ąö one‚Ąö

four‚Ąö : ‚Ąö
four‚Ąö = two‚Ąö +‚Ąö two‚Ąö
module DASHI.Core.KernelMonoid where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude

-- Generic kernel as endomorphism.
record Kernel (S : Set) : Set where
  field K : S ‚Üí S

_‚ąėK_ : ‚ąÄ {S} ‚Üí Kernel S ‚Üí Kernel S ‚Üí Kernel S
_‚ąėK_ {S} A B = record { K = őĽ x ‚Üí Kernel.K A (Kernel.K B x) }

idK : ‚ąÄ {S} ‚Üí Kernel S
idK = record { K = őĽ x ‚Üí x }

-- Extensional equality for kernels (needed to state laws).
KernelEq : ‚ąÄ {S} ‚Üí Kernel S ‚Üí Kernel S ‚Üí Set
KernelEq {S} A B = ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí Kernel.K A x ‚Č° Kernel.K B x

compose-assoc :
  ‚ąÄ {S} (A B C : Kernel S) ‚Üí
  KernelEq ((A ‚ąėK B) ‚ąėK C) (A ‚ąėK (B ‚ąėK C))
compose-assoc A B C x = refl

left-id : ‚ąÄ {S} (A : Kernel S) ‚Üí KernelEq (idK ‚ąėK A) A
left-id A x = refl

right-id : ‚ąÄ {S} (A : Kernel S) ‚Üí KernelEq (A ‚ąėK idK) A
right-id A x = refl
module DASHI.Core.LensKernel where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes

record Lens (S : Set) (A : Set) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    observe : S ‚Üí A

-- Exact commutation: observe (K x) = observe x
record LensInvariant {S A : Set} (L : Lens S A) (K : S ‚Üí S) : Set where
  field inv : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí Lens.observe L (K x) ‚Č° Lens.observe L x

-- Monotone variant (when observations are ordered)
record Preorder (A : Set) : Set‚āĀ where
  field _‚äĎ_ : A ‚Üí A ‚Üí Set
        refl‚äĎ : ‚ąÄ a ‚Üí a ‚äĎ a
        trans‚äĎ : ‚ąÄ a b c ‚Üí a ‚äĎ b ‚Üí b ‚äĎ c ‚Üí a ‚äĎ c

record LensMonotone {S A : Set} (P : Preorder A) (L : Lens S A) (K : S ‚Üí S) : Set where
  open Preorder P
  field mono : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí Lens.observe L (K x) ‚äĎ Lens.observe L x
module DASHI.Core.Prelude where

open import Data.Nat public
  renaming (‚Ąē to Nat)
open import Data.Nat.Properties public
open import Data.Bool public using (Bool; true; false)
open import Data.List public using (List; []; _‚ą∑_)
open import Data.Product public using (ő£; _,_; _√ó_; proj‚āĀ; proj‚āā)
open import Data.Sum public using (_‚äé_; inj‚āĀ; inj‚āā)
open import Data.Empty public using (‚ä•; ‚ä•-elim)
open import Data.Unit public using (‚ä§; tt)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality public using (_‚Č°_; refl; cong; sym; trans)

¬¨_ : Set ‚Üí Set
¬¨ A = A ‚Üí ‚ä•

fst : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} {B : A ‚Üí Set} ‚Üí ő£ A B ‚Üí A
fst = proj‚āĀ

snd : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} {B : A ‚Üí Set} (p : ő£ A B) ‚Üí B (proj‚āĀ p)
snd = proj‚āā
module DASHI.Core.OperatorTypes where

open import DASHI.Core.Prelude
open import DASHI.Core.KernelMonoid using (Kernel; KernelEq)

-- Invertible (bijection witness).
record Invertible {S : Set} (K : S ‚Üí S) : Set where
  field
    inv   : S ‚Üí S
    left  : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí inv (K x) ‚Č° x
    right : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí K (inv x) ‚Č° x

-- Projection = idempotent operator.
record Projection {S : Set} (K : S ‚Üí S) : Set where
  field idem : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí K (K x) ‚Č° K x

-- (Optional) Nontrivial projection means not identity.
Nontrivial : ‚ąÄ {S} (K : S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí Set
Nontrivial {S} K = ¬¨ (‚ąÄ x ‚Üí K x ‚Č° x)

-- Regular inverse (von Neumann regular): a = a*b*a in an algebraic carrier.
-- Here: ‚Äúregularizer‚ÄĚ for endofunctions, expressed as K = K ‚ąė R ‚ąė K.
record Regularizer {S : Set} (K : S ‚Üí S) : Set where
  field
    R : S ‚Üí S
    law : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí K x ‚Č° K (R (K x))

-- A simple operator ‚Äútag‚ÄĚ classifier you can populate later.
data OpClass : Set where
  invertible projection regular other : OpClass

-- Classification is a *goal*: you can decide per operator, not assumed.
record Classifies {S : Set} (K : S ‚Üí S) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    class : OpClass
    sound :
      (class ‚Č° invertible ‚Üí Invertible K) √ó
      (class ‚Č° projection  ‚Üí Projection K) √ó
      (class ‚Č° regular     ‚Üí Regularizer K)

module DASHI.Quantum.AnomalyFreedom where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import DASHI.Unifier using (Tower; HilbertSpace)
open import DASHI.Quantum.Stone using (StoneBundle; StoneConsequences; Stone-theorem)
open import DASHI.Quantum.AgreementDepth using (AgreementDepthBundle; AgreementDepth-theorem)
open import DASHI.Algebra.ConstraintAlgebraClosure
  using (ConstraintClosureBundle; ConstraintClosure-theorem)
open import DASHI.Algebra.ConstraintAlgebraClosureTests
  renaming (DiracClosure to DiracClosureType)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.UVFinitenessHolographyTests using (UVFinite)

record AnomalyBundle (Tow : Tower) (HS : HilbertSpace) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    stone : StoneBundle Tow HS
    agreement : AgreementDepthBundle
    constraint : ConstraintClosureBundle
    anomalyCarrier : Set          -- group/abelian value where anomalies live
    zero : anomalyCarrier
    cubic : anomalyCarrier
    mixed : anomalyCarrier
    cancel-cubic : cubic ‚Č° zero
    cancel-mixed : mixed ‚Č° zero

record AnomalyConsequences {Tow HS} (bundle : AnomalyBundle Tow HS) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    stone : StoneConsequences (AnomalyBundle.stone bundle)
    dirac : DiracClosureType
    uv-finite : UVFinite (AgreementDepthBundle.uv-bounded (AnomalyBundle.agreement bundle))
    cubic-zero : AnomalyBundle.cubic bundle ‚Č° AnomalyBundle.zero bundle
    mixed-zero : AnomalyBundle.mixed bundle ‚Č° AnomalyBundle.zero bundle

AnomalyFreedom : ‚ąÄ {Tow HS} (bundle : AnomalyBundle Tow HS) ‚Üí AnomalyConsequences bundle
AnomalyFreedom bundle =
  record
    { stone = Stone-theorem (AnomalyBundle.stone bundle)
    ; dirac = ConstraintClosure-theorem (AnomalyBundle.constraint bundle)
    ; uv-finite = AgreementDepth-theorem (AnomalyBundle.agreement bundle)
    ; cubic-zero = AnomalyBundle.cancel-cubic bundle
    ; mixed-zero = AnomalyBundle.cancel-mixed bundle
    }
module DASHI.Quantum.Stone where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Data.Product using (ő£; _,_; _√ó_)

open import DASHI.Unifier using (‚ĄĚ; HilbertSpace; Tower; WaveLift; _+_; _-_ ; _‚Č§_; _<_; max; to‚ĄĚ)

absDiff : ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ
absDiff x y = max (x - y) (y - x)

record StoneSelfAdjoint (HS : HilbertSpace) (K : HilbertSpace.H HS ‚Üí HilbertSpace.H HS) : Set where
  open HilbertSpace HS public
  field
    symmetric :
      ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí ‚ü® K x , y ‚ü© ‚Č° ‚ü® x , K y ‚ü©

record StoneGroup {Tow : Tower} {HS : HilbertSpace} (lift : WaveLift Tow HS) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    identity :
      ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí WaveLift.U lift (to‚ĄĚ 0) x ‚Č° x
    composition :
      ‚ąÄ s t x ‚Üí
      WaveLift.U lift (s + t) x ‚Č° WaveLift.U lift s (WaveLift.U lift t x)

record StoneContinuity {S : Set} (U : ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí S ‚Üí S) (dist : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    continuity :
      ‚ąÄ x (őĶ : ‚ĄĚ) ‚Üí
      to‚ĄĚ 0 < őĶ ‚Üí
      ő£ ‚ĄĚ (őĽ őī ‚Üí
        (to‚ĄĚ 0 < őī)
        √ó (‚ąÄ {s t : ‚ĄĚ} ‚Üí
           absDiff s t < őī ‚Üí
           dist (U s x) (U t x) < őĶ))

record StoneBundle (Tow : Tower) (HS : HilbertSpace) : Set‚āĀ where
  open HilbertSpace HS public
  field
    lift : WaveLift Tow HS
    generator : H ‚Üí H
    distance : H ‚Üí H ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ
    self-adjoint : StoneSelfAdjoint HS generator
    stone-group : StoneGroup lift
    strong-continuity : StoneContinuity (WaveLift.U lift) distance

stone-unitary
  : ‚ąÄ {Tow HS}
  ‚Üí StoneBundle Tow HS
  ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ ‚Üí HilbertSpace.H HS ‚Üí HilbertSpace.H HS
stone-unitary bundle = WaveLift.U (StoneBundle.lift bundle)

stone-distance
  : ‚ąÄ {Tow HS} (bundle : StoneBundle Tow HS)
  ‚Üí HilbertSpace.H HS ‚Üí HilbertSpace.H HS ‚Üí ‚ĄĚ
stone-distance bundle = StoneBundle.distance bundle

record StoneConsequences {Tow : Tower} {HS : HilbertSpace} (bundle : StoneBundle Tow HS) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    stone-group : StoneGroup (StoneBundle.lift bundle)
    strong-continuity : StoneContinuity (stone-unitary bundle) (stone-distance bundle)
    stone-self-adjoint : StoneSelfAdjoint HS (StoneBundle.generator bundle)

Stone-theorem
  : ‚ąÄ {Tow HS} (bundle : StoneBundle Tow HS)
  ‚Üí StoneConsequences bundle
Stone-theorem bundle =
  record
    { stone-group = StoneBundle.stone-group bundle
    ; strong-continuity = StoneBundle.strong-continuity bundle
    ; stone-self-adjoint = StoneBundle.self-adjoint bundle
    }
module DASHI.Quantum.AgreementDepth where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import DASHI.Unifier using (Tower; WaveLift; HilbertSpace)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.UVFinitenessHolographyTests using (AreaBound; UVFinitenessTheorem)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Quantum.UVFiniteness using (UVBounded; UVFinite; uvFiniteness)

record AgreementDepthBundle : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    tower : Tower
    hs : HilbertSpace
    lift : WaveLift tower hs
    area-bound : AreaBound
    uv-bounded : UVBounded

record AgreementConsequences (bundle : AgreementDepthBundle) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    uv-finite : UVFinite (AgreementDepthBundle.uv-bounded bundle)
    area-bound : AreaBound

AgreementDepth-theorem : (bundle : AgreementDepthBundle) ‚Üí UVFinite (AgreementDepthBundle.uv-bounded bundle)
AgreementDepth-theorem bundle =
  uvFiniteness (AgreementDepthBundle.uv-bounded bundle)

module DASHI.Physics.SnapSignatureShiftInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Data.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)

open import DASHI.Physics.SnapSignature as SS
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

-- Shift-step predicate: y is exactly TŠĶ£ x.
StepŠĶ£ : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí Set
StepŠĶ£ {m} {k} x y = y ‚Č° TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x

-- Snap signature for shift carrier, parameterized by a tail snap threshold
-- and external chi2/MDL predicates.
record SnapSignatureShift {m k : Nat} : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    snapThreshold : Nat
    chi2Spike : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí Set
    mdlDescent : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí Set

open SnapSignatureShift public

signature : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí SnapSignatureShift {m} {k} ‚Üí SS.SnapSignature {S = RTC.Carrier (m + k)}
signature {m} {k} cfg =
  record
    { step = StepŠĶ£ {m} {k}
    ; snapZero = őĽ x y ‚Üí
        SS.SnapAtLeast (snapThreshold cfg)
          (TCP.tailOf m k x)
          (TCP.tailOf m k y)
    ; chi2Spike = SnapSignatureShift.chi2Spike cfg
    ; mdlDescent = SnapSignatureShift.mdlDescent cfg
    }

m‚Ä≤ : Nat
m‚Ä≤ = 5

m : Nat
m = suc m‚Ä≤

k : Nat
k = 4

n : Nat
n = m + k

orderLaws : SCC.OrderLaws

  record
    { le-trans = NatP.‚Č§-trans
    ; le-<-trans = NatP.‚Č§-<-trans
    ; <-le-trans = NatP.<-‚Č§-trans
    }

  record
    { őĻ = RTC.invVec
    ; invol = RTC.invVec-invol
    }

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic closure kit (parameterized mask + orbit-profile seam)

mask : Vec IMQ.Sign m
mask = SFM.oneMinusRestPlus {m = m‚Ä≤}

coneInvariantMask :
  ‚ąÄ (g : Bool) (x : RTC.Carrier n) ‚Üí
  IMQ.QŌÉ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k (RISS.act {m} {k} g x)) ‚Č° IMQ.QŌÉ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
coneInvariantMask false x = refl
coneInvariantMask true x =
  cong (IMQ.QŌÉ mask) (RISS.coarseOf-tailInv {m} {k} x)

iso : RIS.RealIsotropy (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (őĽ x ‚Üí ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
iso =
  record
    { iso = RIS.RealIsotropy.iso (RISS.realIsotropyInstanceTailInv {m} {k})
    ; coneInvariant = ‚ąÄ g x ‚Üí
        IMQ.QŌÉ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k (RISS.act {m} {k} g x)) ‚Č° IMQ.QŌÉ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    }

fs : RFS.RealFiniteSpeed (őĽ x ‚Üí ROSS.C {m} {k} (ROSS.P {m} {k} (ROSS.R {m} {k} x)))
fs =
  RFSI.realFiniteSpeedInstance {m} {k}

obs : RTC.Carrier n ‚Üí RTC.Carrier k
obs = TCP.tailOf m k

obs0 : RTC.Carrier k
obs0 = replicate k zer

obsT : RTC.Carrier k ‚Üí RTC.Carrier k
obsT _ = obs0

obsFixed : obsT obs0 ‚Č° obs0
obsFixed = refl

obsUnique : ‚ąÄ o ‚Üí obsT o ‚Č° o ‚Üí o ‚Č° obs0
obsUnique o eq = sym eq


realKitFiber : RKF.RealClosureKitFiber

    { S = RTC.Carrier n
    ; U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}
    ; C = ROSS.C {m} {k}

    ; obsT = obsT
    ; obsFixed = obsFixed
    ; obsUnique = obsUnique
    ; inv = inv
    ; iso = iso
    ; fs = fs
    }

coneMono :
  ‚ąÄ (x y : RTC.Carrier m) ‚Üí
  MCS.CausalStructure._‚Čľ_ causal x y ‚Üí
  (+ 0) ‚Č§ŠĶĘ IMQ.QŌÉ mask (MCS.CausalStructure.delta causal x y)

-- Dimension-bound theorem seam (replaces Force-1+3)

  isotropyShellProfile :
    ‚ąÄ {m : Nat}

    ‚Üí ShellOrbitProfile.orbitCount (isotropyShellProfile B S) ‚Č° 3

    ‚Üí ShellOrbitProfile.top2       (isotropyShellProfile B S) ‚Č° 6
    ‚Üí ShellOrbitProfile.top3       (isotropyShellProfile B S) ‚Č° 2
    ‚Üí m ‚Č° 4

    ‚Üí ShellOrbitProfile.top3       (isotropyShellProfile B S) ‚Č° 2

  m‚Č°4‚Üísig‚Č°1+3-up-to-swap :

module DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_; zipWith)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_; proj‚āĀ; proj‚āā)

open import Data.Integer using (‚Ą§; _+_; _-_; _*_; -_; +_; -[1+_])
open import Data.Integer.Properties as IntP
import Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Setoid as EqR

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)

module ‚Ą§-Reasoning = EqR IntP.‚Č°-setoid
open ‚Ą§-Reasoning

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Sign mask

data Sign : Set where
  plus  : Sign
  minus : Sign

sign‚Ą§ : Sign ‚Üí ‚Ą§
sign‚Ą§ plus  = + 1
sign‚Ą§ minus = -[1+ 0 ]   -- -1

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Trit ‚Üí ‚Ą§

to‚Ą§Trit : Trit ‚Üí ‚Ą§
to‚Ą§Trit neg = -[1+ 0 ]   -- -1
to‚Ą§Trit zer = + 0
to‚Ą§Trit pos = + 1

sq‚Ą§ : ‚Ą§ ‚Üí ‚Ą§
sq‚Ą§ x = x * x

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Sum on Vec ‚Ą§

sum‚Ą§ : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec ‚Ą§ m ‚Üí ‚Ą§
sum‚Ą§ []       = + 0
sum‚Ą§ (x ‚ą∑ xs) = x + sum‚Ą§ xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic and weighted dot

QŌÉ : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Sign m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí ‚Ą§
QŌÉ ŌÉ x =
  sum‚Ą§ (zipWith (őĽ s xi ‚Üí sign‚Ą§ s * sq‚Ą§ (to‚Ą§Trit xi)) ŌÉ x)

dotŌÉ : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Sign m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí ‚Ą§
dotŌÉ ŌÉ x y =
  sum‚Ą§ (zipWith (őĽ s p ‚Üí sign‚Ą§ s * (proj‚āĀ p * proj‚āā p))
                ŌÉ
                (zipWith (őĽ a b ‚Üí (to‚Ą§Trit a , to‚Ą§Trit b)) x y))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Polarization (B‚āā) written directly as a signed sum of per-coordinate
-- (a+b)^2 - a^2 - b^2. This is definitionally equivalent to
-- QŌÉ(x+y)-QŌÉ(x)-QŌÉ(y), but avoids Trit addition issues.

B2ŌÉ : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Sign m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí ‚Ą§
B2ŌÉ [] [] [] = + 0
B2ŌÉ (s ‚ą∑ ŌÉ) (a ‚ą∑ x) (b ‚ą∑ y) =
  sign‚Ą§ s *
    ((to‚Ą§Trit a + to‚Ą§Trit b) * (to‚Ą§Trit a + to‚Ą§Trit b)
      - (to‚Ą§Trit a * to‚Ą§Trit a)
      - (to‚Ą§Trit b * to‚Ą§Trit b))
  + B2ŌÉ ŌÉ x y

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Scalar identity: (a+b)^2 - a^2 - b^2 = 2ab for Trit values

b2-trit :
  (a b : Trit) ‚Üí
  (to‚Ą§Trit a + to‚Ą§Trit b) * (to‚Ą§Trit a + to‚Ą§Trit b)
    - (to‚Ą§Trit a * to‚Ą§Trit a)
    - (to‚Ą§Trit b * to‚Ą§Trit b)
    ‚Č° (+ 2) * (to‚Ą§Trit a * to‚Ą§Trit b)
b2-trit neg neg = refl
b2-trit neg zer = refl
b2-trit neg pos = refl
b2-trit zer neg = refl
b2-trit zer zer = refl
b2-trit zer pos = refl
b2-trit pos neg = refl
b2-trit pos zer = refl
b2-trit pos pos = refl

swap2 :
  ‚ąÄ (s : Sign) (z : ‚Ą§) ‚Üí
  sign‚Ą§ s * ((+ 2) * z) ‚Č° (+ 2) * (sign‚Ą§ s * z)
swap2 plus z =
  begin
    sign‚Ą§ plus * ((+ 2) * z)
  ‚Č°‚ü® IntP.*-identityň° ((+ 2) * z) ‚ü©
    (+ 2) * z
  ‚Č°‚ü® cong (őĽ t ‚Üí (+ 2) * t) (sym (IntP.*-identityň° z)) ‚ü©
    (+ 2) * (sign‚Ą§ plus * z)
  ‚ąé
swap2 minus z =
  let
    step1a : sign‚Ą§ minus * ((+ 2) * z) ‚Č° - ((+ 1) * ((+ 2) * z))
    step1a = sym (IntP.neg-distribň°-* (+ 1) ((+ 2) * z))

    step1b : - ((+ 1) * ((+ 2) * z)) ‚Č° - ((+ 2) * z)
    step1b = cong (őĽ t ‚Üí - t) (IntP.*-identityň° ((+ 2) * z))

    step1 : sign‚Ą§ minus * ((+ 2) * z) ‚Č° - ((+ 2) * z)
    step1 = trans step1a step1b

    step2 : - ((+ 2) * z) ‚Č° (+ 2) * (- z)
    step2 = IntP.neg-distrib ≥-* (+ 2) z

    step3a : - z ‚Č° - ((+ 1) * z)
    step3a = cong (őĽ t ‚Üí - t) (sym (IntP.*-identityň° z))

    step3b : - ((+ 1) * z) ‚Č° (- (+ 1)) * z
    step3b = IntP.neg-distribň°-* (+ 1) z

    step3 : - z ‚Č° (sign‚Ą§ minus * z)
    step3 = trans step3a step3b
  in
  trans step1 (trans step2 (cong (őĽ t ‚Üí (+ 2) * t) step3))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Polarization result: B‚āāŌÉ = 2 ¬∑ dotŌÉ

B2ŌÉ‚Č°2dotŌÉ :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} (ŌÉ : Vec Sign m) (x y : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  B2ŌÉ ŌÉ x y ‚Č° (+ 2) * dotŌÉ ŌÉ x y
B2ŌÉ‚Č°2dotŌÉ [] [] [] = refl
B2ŌÉ‚Č°2dotŌÉ (s ‚ą∑ ŌÉ) (a ‚ą∑ x) (b ‚ą∑ y) =
  let
    xa = to‚Ą§Trit a
    yb = to‚Ą§Trit b
  in
  begin
    B2ŌÉ (s ‚ą∑ ŌÉ) (a ‚ą∑ x) (b ‚ą∑ y)
  ‚Č°‚ü® cong (őĽ t ‚Üí sign‚Ą§ s * t + B2ŌÉ ŌÉ x y) (b2-trit a b) ‚ü©
    sign‚Ą§ s * ((+ 2) * (xa * yb)) + B2ŌÉ ŌÉ x y
  ‚Č°‚ü® cong (őĽ t ‚Üí sign‚Ą§ s * ((+ 2) * (xa * yb)) + t) (B2ŌÉ‚Č°2dotŌÉ ŌÉ x y) ‚ü©
    sign‚Ą§ s * ((+ 2) * (xa * yb)) + (+ 2) * dotŌÉ ŌÉ x y
  ‚Č°‚ü® cong (őĽ t ‚Üí t + (+ 2) * dotŌÉ ŌÉ x y)
        (swap2 s (xa * yb)) ‚ü©
    (+ 2) * (sign‚Ą§ s * (xa * yb)) + (+ 2) * dotŌÉ ŌÉ x y
  ‚Č°‚ü® sym (IntP.*-distribň°-+ (+ 2) (sign‚Ą§ s * (xa * yb)) (dotŌÉ ŌÉ x y)) ‚ü©
    (+ 2) * (sign‚Ą§ s * (xa * yb) + dotŌÉ ŌÉ x y)
  ‚Č°‚ü® refl ‚ü©
    (+ 2) * dotŌÉ (s ‚ą∑ ŌÉ) (a ‚ą∑ x) (b ‚ą∑ y)
  ‚ąé
  where
    infix 0 ‚Ėł
    ‚Ėł : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} {u v : A} ‚Üí u ‚Č° v ‚Üí u ‚Č° v
    ‚Ėł p = p
module DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseInvolution where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_; _++_; map)
open import Data.Vec.Base using (_‚ą∑ ≥_; init)
open import Data.Vec.Properties using (map-++; init-‚ą∑ ≥)
open import Data.Product using (_,_)
open import Data.Product using (proj‚āĀ; proj‚āā)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; inv; zer)
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec distributes over append

invVec-++ :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  RTC.invVec (c ++ t) ‚Č° RTC.invVec c ++ RTC.invVec t
invVec-++ c t = map-++ inv c t

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec commutes with snoc

invVec-‚ą∑ ≥ :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit k) (a : Trit) ‚Üí
  RTC.invVec (xs ‚ą∑ ≥ a) ‚Č° RTC.invVec xs ‚ą∑ ≥ inv a
invVec-‚ą∑ ≥ {zero} [] a = refl
invVec-‚ą∑ ≥ {suc k} (x ‚ą∑ xs) a =
  cong (inv x ‚ą∑_) (invVec-‚ą∑ ≥ xs a)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec commutes with shiftTail

invVec-shiftTail :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  RTC.invVec (TCP.shiftTail t) ‚Č° TCP.shiftTail (RTC.invVec t)
invVec-shiftTail {zero} [] = refl
invVec-shiftTail {suc k} (x ‚ą∑ xs) =
  trans (invVec-‚ą∑ ≥ xs zer) refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec commutes with init

invVec-init :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc k)) ‚Üí
  RTC.invVec (init t) ‚Č° init (RTC.invVec t)
invVec-init {zero} (x ‚ą∑ []) = refl
invVec-init {suc k} (x ‚ą∑ y ‚ą∑ xs) =
  cong (inv x ‚ą∑_) (invVec-init (y ‚ą∑ xs))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec commutes with projTail

invVec-projTail :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  RTC.invVec (TCP.projTail t) ‚Č° TCP.projTail (RTC.invVec t)
invVec-projTail {zero} [] = refl
invVec-projTail {suc k} t =
  let
    p : RTC.invVec (init t ‚ą∑ ≥ zer) ‚Č° RTC.invVec (init t) ‚ą∑ ≥ inv zer
    p = invVec-‚ą∑ ≥ (init t) zer
  in
  trans p (cong (_‚ą∑ ≥ zer) (invVec-init t))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- invVec commutes with RŠĶ£ and PŠĶ£

invVec-RŠĶ£ :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  RTC.invVec (TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} (RTC.invVec x)
invVec-RŠĶ£ {m} {k} x =
  let
    c = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    t = TCP.tailOf m k x
    p : x ‚Č° c ++ t
    p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
    q : RTC.invVec x ‚Č° RTC.invVec c ++ RTC.invVec t
    q = trans (cong RTC.invVec p) (invVec-++ c t)
  in
  trans
    (cong RTC.invVec (trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.RŠĶ£-++ m k c t)))
    (trans
      (invVec-++ c (TCP.shiftTail t))
      (trans
        (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí RTC.invVec c ++ v) (invVec-shiftTail t))
        (sym (trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} v) q)
                    (TCP.RŠĶ£-++ m k (RTC.invVec c) (RTC.invVec t))))))

invVec-PŠĶ£ :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  RTC.invVec (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} (RTC.invVec x)
invVec-PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x =
  let
    c = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    t = TCP.tailOf m k x
    p : x ‚Č° c ++ t
    p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
    q : RTC.invVec x ‚Č° RTC.invVec c ++ RTC.invVec t
    q = trans (cong RTC.invVec p) (invVec-++ c t)
  in
  trans
    (cong RTC.invVec (trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.PŠĶ£-++ m k c t)))
    (trans
      (invVec-++ c (TCP.projTail t))
      (trans
        (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí RTC.invVec c ++ v) (invVec-projTail t))
        (sym (trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} v) q)
                    (TCP.PŠĶ£-++ m k (RTC.invVec c) (RTC.invVec t))))))
module DASHI.Physics.RealOperatorStack where

open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Physics.RealOperators as RO
open import Contraction
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import DASHI.Geometry.FiberContraction as FC
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym; subst)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)

C P R : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n
C {n} = RO.CŠĶ£ {n}
P {n} = RO.PŠĶ£ {n}
R {n} = RO.RŠĶ£ {n}

nonexpC : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (C {n})
nonexpC {n} = RO.nonexpCŠĶ£ {n}

nonexpR : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (R {n})
nonexpR {n} = RO.nonexpRŠĶ£ {n}

strictP-fiber : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí FC.ContractiveOnFibers (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (P {n})
strictP-fiber {n} =
  record
    { contractFiber = őĽ {x} {y} fd ‚Üí
        let
          open UMetric.Ultrametric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n})
          open FC.FiberDistinct fd using (x‚ČĘy; sameFiber)
          d0 : d (P x) (P y) ‚Č° 0
          d0 = subst (őĽ z ‚Üí d (P x) z ‚Č° 0) sameFiber (id-zero (P x))
        in
        subst (őĽ k ‚Üí k < d x y) (sym d0) (FAM.dNatFine-positive x‚ČĘy)
    }

-- Hyperbolic cone and orthogonality (schematic)

HyperbolicCone : {A : Set} ‚Üí (Q : A ‚Üí Nat) ‚Üí A ‚Üí Set
HyperbolicCone Q x = 0 < Q x

Orthogonal : {A : Set} ‚Üí (B : A ‚Üí A ‚Üí Nat) ‚Üí A ‚Üí A ‚Üí Set
Orthogonal B x y = B x y ‚Č° 0

module DASHI.Physics.ClosureGlue where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)

open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contraction
open import DASHI.Geometry.Isotropy as Iso
open import DASHI.Geometry.FiniteSpeed as FS
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 0) One record to carry the whole ‚Äúphysics closure‚ÄĚ interface
------------------------------------------------------------------------

record ClosureAxioms : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    S   : Set
    U   : UMetric.Ultrametric S
    T   : S ‚Üí S
    sc  : Contraction.StrictContraction U T
    inv : Involution S
    iso : Iso.Isotropy U T
    fs  : FS.FiniteSpeed T

open ClosureAxioms public

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 1) Useful derived facts (no postulates; all come from record fields)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

fp : ‚ąÄ (A : ClosureAxioms) ‚Üí S A
fp A = Contraction.StrictContraction.fp (sc A)

T-fixes-fp : ‚ąÄ (A : ClosureAxioms) ‚Üí T A (fp A) ‚Č° fp A
T-fixes-fp A = Contraction.StrictContraction.fixed (sc A)

fixed‚Üífp :
  ‚ąÄ (A : ClosureAxioms) ‚Üí (x : S A) ‚Üí T A x ‚Č° x ‚Üí x ‚Č° fp A
fixed‚Üífp A x hx = Contraction.StrictContraction.unique (sc A) x hx

contractive‚ČĘ : ‚ąÄ (A : ClosureAxioms) ‚Üí Contraction.Contractive‚ČĘ (U A) (T A)
contractive‚ČĘ A = Contraction.StrictContraction.contractive‚ČĘ (sc A)

iso-commutes :
  ‚ąÄ (A : ClosureAxioms)
  ‚Üí (g : Iso.Isotropy.G (iso A))
  ‚Üí (x : S A)
  ‚Üí T A (Iso.Isotropy.act (iso A) g x)
    ‚Č° Iso.Isotropy.act (iso A) g (T A x)
iso-commutes A g x = Iso.Isotropy.commutesWithT (iso A) g x

preserves-locality :
  ‚ąÄ (A : ClosureAxioms) ‚Üí (x y : S A)
  ‚Üí FS.FiniteSpeed.local (fs A) x y
  ‚Üí FS.FiniteSpeed.local (fs A) (T A x) (T A y)
preserves-locality A x y h =
  FS.FiniteSpeed.preservesLocality (fs A) x y h

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- 2) ‚ÄúCompile-today‚ÄĚ defaults: trivial isotropy + trivial finite speed
------------------------------------------------------------------------

defaultIso : ‚ąÄ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) (T : S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí Iso.Isotropy U T
defaultIso U T = Iso.trivialIsotropy U T

defaultFS : ‚ąÄ {S : Set} (T : S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí FS.FiniteSpeed T
defaultFS T = FS.trivialFiniteSpeed T

mkDefaultClosure :
  ‚ąÄ {S : Set}
  ‚Üí (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
  ‚Üí (T : S ‚Üí S)
  ‚Üí (sc : Contraction.StrictContraction U T)
  ‚Üí (inv : Involution S)
  ‚Üí ClosureAxioms
mkDefaultClosure {S} U T sc inv =
  record
    { S   = S
    ; U   = U
    ; T   = T
    ; sc  = sc
    ; inv = inv
    ; iso = defaultIso U T
    ; fs  = defaultFS T
    }

  open Group GG renaming (_‚ąô_ to _‚ąôG_; e to eG; inv to invG)
  open Group HH renaming (_‚ąô_ to _‚ąôH_; e to eH; inv to invH)
  field
    f     : G ‚Üí H
    pres‚ąô : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí f (x ‚ąôG y) ‚Č° f x ‚ąôH f y
    prese : f eG ‚Č° eH

    surj  : ‚ä§
    twoTo1 : ‚ä§

module DASHI.Physics.RealClosureKit where

record RealClosureKit : Set‚āĀ where

    S : Set
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric S

    C P R : S ‚Üí S

    nonexpR : SCC.NonExpansive U R
    strictP : Contractive‚ČĘ U P
    orderLaws : SCC.OrderLaws
    pres‚ČĘR : SCC.DistinctPreserving R

    fp : S
    fixedT : (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R })) fp ‚Č° fp
    uniqueT : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R })) x ‚Č° x ‚Üí x ‚Č° fp

  record
    { S = S k
    ; U = U k
    ; C = C k
    ; P = P k
    ; R = R k
    ; nonexpC = nonexpC k
    ; nonexpR = nonexpR k
    ; strictP = strictP k
    ; orderLaws = orderLaws k
    ; pres‚ČĘR = pres‚ČĘR k
    ; fp0 = fp k
    ; fixedT = fixedT k
    ; uniqueT = uniqueT k
    ; inv = inv k
    ; iso = iso k
    ; fs  = fs k
    }

closureAxioms : (k : RealClosureKit) ‚Üí Glue.ClosureAxioms
closureAxioms k = CB.buildClosure (toRealStack k)

module DASHI.Physics.Core where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äĒ_; zero; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; ő£; ő£-syntax; _,_)
open import Data.Nat using (‚Ąē)
open import Data.Bool using (Bool)

-- Abstract metric space; swap in your concrete ultrametric if desired.
record MetricSpace (‚Ąď : Level) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    X     : Set ‚Ąď
    d     : X ‚Üí X ‚Üí Set ‚Ąď        -- use ‚ĄĚ-valued distance later if needed
    reflD : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí d x x
    sym   : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí d x y ‚Üí d y x
    -- triangle etc as needed

-- Contractive operator skeleton.
record ContractionOp {‚Ąď : Level} (M : MetricSpace ‚Ąď) : Set (suc (suc ‚Ąď)) where
  open MetricSpace M
  field
    T      : X ‚Üí X
    lam    : Set ‚Ąď               -- typically a scalar 0<őĽ<1
    contractive : Set (suc ‚Ąď)    -- replace with your inequality form

-- Bilinear and quadratic forms kept abstract.
record Bilinear {‚Ąď : Level} (V : Set ‚Ąď) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    B : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí Set ‚Ąď

record Quadratic {‚Ąď : Level} (V : Set ‚Ąď) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    Q : V ‚Üí Set ‚Ąď

-- Involution / mirror.
record Involution {‚Ąď : Level} (V : Set ‚Ąď) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    őĻ    : V ‚Üí V
    invol : ‚ąÄ v ‚Üí őĻ (őĻ v) ‚Č° v

-- Finite speed / locality placeholder.
record FiniteSpeed {‚Ąď : Level} (V : Set ‚Ąď) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    locality : Set ‚Ąď

-- Isotropy (rotation-like symmetries) and preservation of a quadratic form.
record Isotropy {‚Ąď : Level} (V : Set ‚Ąď) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    G   : Set ‚Ąď
    act : G ‚Üí V ‚Üí V

record PreservesQuadratic {‚Ąď : Level} {V : Set ‚Ąď} (iso : Isotropy V) (Q : Quadratic V) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  open Isotropy iso
  field
    pres : ‚ąÄ g v ‚Üí Quadratic.Q Q (act g v) ‚Č° Quadratic.Q Q v

-- Clifford-like algebra interface via universal property.
record CliffordLike {‚Ąď : Level} (V : Set ‚Ąď) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    Cl    : Set ‚Ąď
    embed : V ‚Üí Cl
    -- relations to be added in DecimationToClifford

-- Even subalgebra carrier.
record EvenSubalg {‚Ąď : Level} (A : Set ‚Ąď) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    Even : Set ‚Ąď
    inc  : Even ‚Üí A

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- sum‚Ą§ distributes over ++

sum‚Ą§-++ :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} (xs : Vec ‚Ą§ m) (ys : Vec ‚Ą§ k) ‚Üí
  IMQ.sum‚Ą§ (xs ++ ys) ‚Č° IMQ.sum‚Ą§ xs +‚Ą§ IMQ.sum‚Ą§ ys
sum‚Ą§-++ [] ys =
  sym (IntP.+-identityň° (IMQ.sum‚Ą§ ys))
sum‚Ą§-++ (x ‚ą∑ xs) ys =
  let
    sum‚Ą§-cons : IMQ.sum‚Ą§ (x ‚ą∑ xs) ‚Č° x +‚Ą§ IMQ.sum‚Ą§ xs
    sum‚Ą§-cons = refl
    step : x +‚Ą§ IMQ.sum‚Ą§ (xs ++ ys) ‚Č° x +‚Ą§ (IMQ.sum‚Ą§ xs +‚Ą§ IMQ.sum‚Ą§ ys)
    step = cong (őĽ z ‚Üí x +‚Ą§ z) (sum‚Ą§-++ xs ys)
    step2 : x +‚Ą§ (IMQ.sum‚Ą§ xs +‚Ą§ IMQ.sum‚Ą§ ys) ‚Č° (x +‚Ą§ IMQ.sum‚Ą§ xs) +‚Ą§ IMQ.sum‚Ą§ ys
    step2 = sym (IntP.+-assoc x (IMQ.sum‚Ą§ xs) (IMQ.sum‚Ą§ ys))
    step3 : (x +‚Ą§ IMQ.sum‚Ą§ xs) +‚Ą§ IMQ.sum‚Ą§ ys ‚Č° IMQ.sum‚Ą§ (x ‚ą∑ xs) +‚Ą§ IMQ.sum‚Ą§ ys
    step3 = cong (őĽ z ‚Üí z +‚Ą§ IMQ.sum‚Ą§ ys) (sym sum‚Ą§-cons)
  in
  trans step (trans step2 step3)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- zipWith distributes over ++

zipWith-++ :
  ‚ąÄ {A B C : Set} (f : A ‚Üí B ‚Üí C)
    {m k : Nat}
    (a‚āĀ : Vec A m) (a‚āā : Vec A k)
    (b‚āĀ : Vec B m) (b‚āā : Vec B k) ‚Üí
  zipWith f (a‚āĀ ++ a‚āā) (b‚āĀ ++ b‚āā) ‚Č° (zipWith f a‚āĀ b‚āĀ) ++ (zipWith f a‚āā b‚āā)
zipWith-++ f [] a‚āā [] b‚āā = refl
zipWith-++ f (a ‚ą∑ a‚āĀ) a‚āā (b ‚ą∑ b‚āĀ) b‚āā =
  cong (őĽ z ‚Üí f a b ‚ą∑ z) (zipWith-++ f a‚āĀ a‚āā b‚āĀ b‚āā)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic split: QŌÉ splits over (coarse ++ tail)

QŌÉ-split :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat)
    (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ x
    ‚Č° IMQ.QŌÉ (TCP.coarseOf m k ŌÉ) (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    +‚Ą§ IMQ.QŌÉ (TCP.tailOf   m k ŌÉ) (TCP.tailOf   m k x)
QŌÉ-split m k ŌÉ x =
  let
    f = (őĽ s t ‚Üí IMQ.sign‚Ą§ s * IMQ.sq‚Ą§ (IMQ.to‚Ą§Trit t))
    ŌÉc = TCP.coarseOf m k ŌÉ
    ŌÉt = TCP.tailOf m k ŌÉ
    xc = TCP.coarseOf m k x
    xt = TCP.tailOf m k x
    ŌÉ‚Č° : ŌÉc ++ ŌÉt ‚Č° ŌÉ
    ŌÉ‚Č° = TCP.merge-split m k ŌÉ
    x‚Č° : xc ++ xt ‚Č° x
    x‚Č° = TCP.merge-split m k x
    step1 : IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ x ‚Č° IMQ.sum‚Ą§ (zipWith f (ŌÉc ++ ŌÉt) x)
    step1 = cong (őĽ z ‚Üí IMQ.sum‚Ą§ (zipWith f z x)) (sym ŌÉ‚Č°)
    step2 : IMQ.sum‚Ą§ (zipWith f (ŌÉc ++ ŌÉt) x) ‚Č° IMQ.sum‚Ą§ (zipWith f (ŌÉc ++ ŌÉt) (xc ++ xt))
    step2 = cong (őĽ z ‚Üí IMQ.sum‚Ą§ (zipWith f (ŌÉc ++ ŌÉt) z)) (sym x‚Č°)
    step3 : IMQ.sum‚Ą§ (zipWith f (ŌÉc ++ ŌÉt) (xc ++ xt))
            ‚Č° IMQ.sum‚Ą§ ((zipWith f ŌÉc xc) ++ (zipWith f ŌÉt xt))
    step3 = cong IMQ.sum‚Ą§ (zipWith-++ f ŌÉc ŌÉt xc xt)
    step4 : IMQ.sum‚Ą§ ((zipWith f ŌÉc xc) ++ (zipWith f ŌÉt xt))
            ‚Č° IMQ.sum‚Ą§ (zipWith f ŌÉc xc) +‚Ą§ IMQ.sum‚Ą§ (zipWith f ŌÉt xt)
    step4 = sum‚Ą§-++ (zipWith f ŌÉc xc) (zipWith f ŌÉt xt)
  in
  trans step1 (trans step2 (trans step3 step4))

module DASHI.Physics.Closure.EnergyShiftBase where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Nat using (_+_; z‚Č§n)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (‚Č§-refl; ‚Č§-trans; ‚Č§-antisym)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_; refl; subst)

-- Preorder over Nat with ‚Č§.
NatPreorder : E.Preorder
NatPreorder = record
  { S = Nat
  ; _‚Č§_ = Data.Nat._‚Č§_
  ; refl‚Č§ = őĽ _ ‚Üí NatP.‚Č§-refl
  ; trans‚Č§ = őĽ _ _ _ ‚Üí NatP.‚Č§-trans
  }

-- Energy = ultrametric distance.
energy-sep :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x y : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  E.Preorder._‚Č§_ NatPreorder
    (UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y)
    (UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x x) ‚Üí
  x ‚Č° y
energy-sep m k x y h =
  let
    U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}
    dxy = UMetric.Ultrametric.d U x y
    dxx = UMetric.Ultrametric.d U x x
    dxx‚Č°0 = UMetric.Ultrametric.id-zero U x
    h' : dxy Data.Nat.‚Č§ 0
    h' = subst (őĽ v ‚Üí dxy Data.Nat.‚Č§ v) dxx‚Č°0 h
    dxy‚Č°0 : dxy ‚Č° 0
    dxy‚Č°0 = NatP.‚Č§-antisym h' z‚Č§n
  in
  FAM.dNatFine-zero‚Üíeq x y dxy‚Č°0

EnergyShift : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí E.EnergySpace (RTC.Carrier (m + k)) NatPreorder
EnergyShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { E = UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
    ; E-refl = őĽ _ ‚Üí NatP.‚Č§-refl
    ; E-sep = energy-sep m k
    }

ProjShift : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí CP.Projection (RTC.Carrier (m + k))
ProjShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { P = TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k}
    ; idem = TCP.PŠĶ£-idem m k
    }

module DASHI.Physics.Closure.EmpiricalClosureWithSignatureLock where

-- Bundle empirical seams with witness policy and signature-lock evidence.

  : Set (suc ‚Ąď ‚äĒ suc zero) where
  field
    empirical : PCE.PhysicsClosureEmpirical
    policy : WSP.WitnessSetPolicy W
    orbitProfile : SE.OrbitProfile V
