signatureLock :
  ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {W : Set ‚Ąď} {n : Nat} {V : Set}
  ‚Üí EmpiricalClosureWithSignatureLock W {n} V
  ‚Üí SE.SignatureLock {n} V
signatureLock bundle =
  SLCSV.signatureLockFromRank
    (orbitProfile bundle)
    (signatureEvidence bundle)

signature31FromEvidence :
  ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {W : Set ‚Ąď} {n : Nat} {V : Set}
  (Q : MQ.MaskedQuadratic n)
  (bundle : EmpiricalClosureWithSignatureLock W {n} V)
  ‚Üí SLCSV.SignatureRankCSVEvidence.rank (signatureEvidence bundle) Q
  ‚Üí MQ.signatureTag Q ‚Č° MQ.sig31
signature31FromEvidence Q bundle rk =
  SLCSV.signature31FromRank Q (orbitProfile bundle) (signatureEvidence bundle) rk

  {P : E.Preorder {‚Ąďs}}
  {O : MDL.OrderedMonoid {‚Ąďn}}

  (Trade : MDL.TradeoffLemma Parts)

      MDL.OrderedMonoid._‚Č§_ O (MDL.MDLParts.MDL Parts (MDL.MDLParts.T Parts x))
                                (MDL.MDLParts.MDL Parts x)

betaSeamsFromEvidence :
  ‚ąÄ {‚Ąďx ‚Ąďs ‚Ąďn ‚Ąďe}
  {X : Set ‚Ąďx}
  {P : E.Preorder {‚Ąďs}}
  {O : MDL.OrderedMonoid {‚Ąďn}}
  (ES : E.EnergySpace X P)
  (Pr : CP.Projection X)
  (Ecod : Set ‚Ąďe)
  (Parts : MDL.MDLParts X O)
  (Trade : MDL.TradeoffLemma Parts)
  (Ev : BetaSeamCSVEvidence ES Pr Ecod Parts Trade)
  ‚Üí BSC.BetaSeams ES Pr Ecod Parts Trade

    ; closest = BetaSeamCSVEvidence.closest Ev

    }

module DASHI.Physics.Closure.MDLFejerAxiomsShift where

  Parts {m} {k} = MSI.MDLPartsShift {m} {k}

  Trade : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí MDL.TradeoffLemma (Parts {m} {k})
  Trade {m} {k} = MSI.TradeoffShift {m} {k}

-- Formalizes the empirical finding: MDL-style energy is Fej√©r/monotone

      ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí

      (MDL.MDLParts.MDL (Parts {m} {k}) x)

module DASHI.Physics.Closure.MDLTradeoffShiftInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_; refl; cong; trans; subst; sym)
open import Data.Nat using (_+_; _‚Č§_; zero; z‚Č§n)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (‚Č§-refl; ‚Č§-trans; +-mono-‚Č§; +-identity ≥; +-identityň°; +-assoc; m‚Č§n+m)

open import Data.Vec.Base using (init; _‚ą∑ ≥_)

-- Ordered monoid over Nat with + and ‚Č§.
NatOrderedMonoid : MDL.OrderedMonoid
NatOrderedMonoid = record
  { M = record
      { N = Nat
      ; _+_ = Data.Nat._+_
      ; 0# = zero
      }
  ; _‚Č§_ = Data.Nat._‚Č§_
  ; refl‚Č§ = őĽ _ ‚Üí NatP.‚Č§-refl
  ; trans‚Č§ = őĽ _ _ _ ‚Üí NatP.‚Č§-trans
  ; mono+ = őĽ a b c d le1 le2 ‚Üí NatP.+-mono-‚Č§ le1 le2
  }

-- Simple nontrivial length: count nonzero trits.
nz : Trit ‚Üí Nat
nz neg = 1
nz zer = 0
nz pos = 1

countNZ : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Nat
countNZ [] = 0
countNZ (x ‚ą∑ xs) = nz x + countNZ xs

countNZ-snoc :
  ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit n) (a : Trit) ‚Üí
  countNZ (xs ‚ą∑ ≥ a) ‚Č° countNZ xs + nz a
countNZ-snoc [] a =
  trans (NatP.+-identity ≥ (nz a))
        (sym (NatP.+-identityň° (nz a)))
countNZ-snoc (x ‚ą∑ xs) a =
  trans (cong (őĽ k ‚Üí nz x + k) (countNZ-snoc xs a))
        (sym (NatP.+-assoc (nz x) (countNZ xs) (nz a)))

countNZ-init‚Č§ :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc k)) ‚Üí countNZ (init t) ‚Č§ countNZ t
countNZ-init‚Č§ {zero} (x ‚ą∑ []) = z‚Č§n
countNZ-init‚Č§ {suc k} (x ‚ą∑ y ‚ą∑ ys) =
  NatP.+-mono-‚Č§ (NatP.‚Č§-refl {nz x}) (countNZ-init‚Č§ (y ‚ą∑ ys))

projTail-def :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.projTail t ‚Č° (init t ‚ą∑ ≥ zer)
projTail-def t = refl

shiftTail-def :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (x : Trit) (xs : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  TCP.shiftTail (x ‚ą∑ xs) ‚Č° xs ‚ą∑ ≥ zer
shiftTail-def x xs = refl

countNZ-projTail‚Č§ :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí countNZ (TCP.projTail t) ‚Č§ countNZ t
countNZ-projTail‚Č§ {zero} [] = NatP.‚Č§-refl
countNZ-projTail‚Č§ {suc k} t
  rewrite projTail-def t
        | countNZ-snoc (init t) zer
        | NatP.+-identity ≥ (countNZ (init t))
  = countNZ-init‚Č§ t

countNZ-shiftTail‚Č§ :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí countNZ (TCP.shiftTail t) ‚Č§ countNZ t
countNZ-shiftTail‚Č§ {zero} [] = NatP.‚Č§-refl
countNZ-shiftTail‚Č§ {suc k} (x ‚ą∑ xs)
  rewrite shiftTail-def x xs
        | countNZ-snoc xs zer
        | NatP.+-identity ≥ (countNZ xs)
  = NatP.m‚Č§n+m (countNZ xs) (nz x)

countNZ-tailStep‚Č§ :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí countNZ (TCP.tailStep t) ‚Č§ countNZ t
countNZ-tailStep‚Č§ t =
  NatP.‚Č§-trans (countNZ-projTail‚Č§ (TCP.shiftTail t)) (countNZ-shiftTail‚Č§ t)

tailOf-PŠĶ£ :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° TCP.projTail (TCP.tailOf m k x)
tailOf-PŠĶ£ m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite TCP.PŠĶ£-++ m k c t
        | TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.projTail t)
  = refl

tailOf-TŠĶ£ :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° TCP.tailStep (TCP.tailOf m k x)
tailOf-TŠĶ£ m k x =
  cong Data.Product.proj‚āā (TCP.split-TŠĶ£ m k x)

resid-drop-lemma :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)) ‚Č§ countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k x)
resid-drop-lemma {m} {k} x
  rewrite tailOf-TŠĶ£ m k x
  = countNZ-tailStep‚Č§ (TCP.tailOf m k x)

coarse-invariant-R :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° TCP.coarseOf m k x
coarse-invariant-R m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t)
  = refl

coarse-invariant-P :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° TCP.coarseOf m k x
coarse-invariant-P m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.projTail t)
  = refl

coarse-invariant-T :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° TCP.coarseOf m k x
coarse-invariant-T m k x =
  trans (coarse-invariant-P m k (TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} x))
        (coarse-invariant-R m k x)

coarseOf-PT-‚Č°-P :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} (TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)) ‚Č°
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)
coarseOf-PT-‚Č°-P m k x =
  let
    p-idem = TCP.PŠĶ£-idem m k (TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)
    cPT : TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} (TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)) ‚Č°
          TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)
    cPT = cong (TCP.coarseOf m k) p-idem
    cT  = coarse-invariant-T m k x
    cP  = coarse-invariant-P m k x
  in
  trans cPT (trans cT (sym cP))

model-drop-lemma :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier (m + k)) ‚Üí
  countNZ (TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} (TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)))
    ‚Č§ countNZ (TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x))
model-drop-lemma {m} {k} x
  rewrite coarseOf-PT-‚Č°-P m k x
  = NatP.‚Č§-refl

-- MDL parts: model length = countNZ of coarse, residual length = countNZ of tail.
MDLPartsShift : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí MDL.MDLParts (RTC.Carrier (m + k)) NatOrderedMonoid
MDLPartsShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { P = TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k}
    ; D = őĽ x ‚Üí x
    ; T = TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k}
    ; ModelLen = őĽ x ‚Üí countNZ (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    ; ResidLen = őĽ x ‚Üí countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k x)
    ; MDL = őĽ x ‚Üí countNZ (TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)) + countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k x)
    ; MDL-def = őĽ _ ‚Üí refl
    }

-- Tradeoff lemma from coarse invariance and projTail decreasing nonzero count.
TradeoffShift : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí MDL.TradeoffLemma (MDLPartsShift {m} {k})
TradeoffShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { model-drop = model-drop-lemma {m} {k}
    ; resid-drop = resid-drop-lemma {m} {k}
    }

module DASHI.Physics.Closure.EnergyClosestPointShiftInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Nat using (_+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_; refl; subst; sym)
open import Data.Nat using (z‚Č§n; s‚Č§s; _‚äĒ_)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (‚Č§-refl; ‚Č§-trans; ‚Č§-antisym; ‚äĒ-lub)

open import DASHI.Energy.FejerToClosestPoint as FC

open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

-- Fej√©r/ClosestPoint seams (to be discharged by real proofs later).
fejerShift :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  CP.FejerMonotone (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) (ESB.ProjShift {m} {k})
fejerShift {m} {k} =
  record
    { fejer = őĽ x y fix ‚Üí
        let
          U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}
          ne = ROSS.nonexpP {m} {k}
          step = SCC.NonExpansive.nonexp ne x y
        in
        subst (őĽ v ‚Üí Data.Nat._‚Č§_
                     (UMetric.Ultrametric.d U (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) v)
                     (UMetric.Ultrametric.d U x y))
              fix
              step
    }

fejer‚áíclosestShift :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí
    CP.FixP (ESB.ProjShift {m} {k}) y ‚Üí
    Data.Nat._‚Č§_
      (E.EnergySpace.E (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) x (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x))
      (E.EnergySpace.E (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) x y)
fejer‚áíclosestShift {m} {k} x y fix =
  let
    U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}
    d = UMetric.Ultrametric.d U
    tri : Data.Nat._‚Č§_ (d x (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)) (d x y ‚äĒ d y (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x))
    tri = UMetric.Ultrametric.ultratriangle U x y (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)
    sym1 : d y (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° d (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) y
    sym1 = UMetric.Ultrametric.symmetric U y (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)
    fejer-bound :
      Data.Nat._‚Č§_ (d (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) y) (d x y)
    fejer-bound =
      CP.FejerMonotone.fejer (fejerShift {m} {k}) x y fix
    max-bound : Data.Nat._‚Č§_ (d x y ‚äĒ d y (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)) (d x y)
    max-bound =
      NatP.‚äĒ-lub
        (NatP.‚Č§-refl)
        (subst (őĽ v ‚Üí Data.Nat._‚Č§_ v (d x y)) (sym sym1) fejer-bound)
  in
  NatP.‚Č§-trans tri max-bound

closestAxiomsShift : CPA.ClosestPointAxiomsShift
closestAxiomsShift =
  record
    { closestAxiomShift =
        őĽ {m} {k} ‚Üí
          record
            { fejer = fejerShift {m} {k}
            ; fejer‚áíclosest = fejer‚áíclosestShift {m} {k}
            }
    }

closestShift :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  CP.ClosestPoint (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) (ESB.ProjShift {m} {k})
closestShift {m} {k} =
  FC.closestFromFejer (ESB.EnergyShift {m} {k}) (ESB.ProjShift {m} {k})
    (CPA.closestAxiomShift closestAxiomsShift {m} {k})

-- Reuse the default Bool ultrametric and contraction as a concrete instance.

id : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí A ‚Üí A
id x = x

nonexp-id : ‚ąÄ {S : Set} (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S) ‚Üí SCC.NonExpansive U id
nonexp-id U = record { nonexp = őĽ x y ‚Üí ‚Č§-refl }

preserves‚ČĘ-id : ‚ąÄ {S : Set} ‚Üí SCC.DistinctPreserving (id {S})
preserves‚ČĘ-id = record { preserves‚ČĘ = őĽ x‚ČĘy ‚Üí x‚ČĘy }

orderLawsNat : SCC.OrderLaws
orderLawsNat = record
  { le-trans = ‚Č§-trans
  ; le-<-trans = ‚Č§-<-trans
  ; <-le-trans = <-‚Č§-trans
  }

-- RealStack using P = T, C = id, R = id so T = P.
realStack : CB.RealStack
realStack =
  record
    { S = DC.Carrier
    ; U = DC.boolUltrametric
    ; C = id
    ; P = DC.T
    ; R = id
    ; nonexpC = nonexp-id DC.boolUltrametric
    ; nonexpR = nonexp-id DC.boolUltrametric
    ; strictP = DC.contractiveBool
    ; orderLaws = orderLawsNat
    ; pres‚ČĘR = preserves‚ČĘ-id
    ; fp0 = false
    ; fixedT = refl
    ; uniqueT = DC.uniqueBool
    ; inv = DC.invBool
    ; iso = record { iso = Iso.trivialIsotropy DC.boolUltrametric DC.T ; coneInvariant = ‚ä§ }
    ; fs = record { local = őĽ _ _ ‚Üí ‚ä§ ; preservesLocality = őĽ _ _ _ ‚Üí tt }
    }

realClosure : UC.closure realStack ‚Č° CB.buildClosure realStack
realClosure = refl

-- Concrete physics-unification witnesses on the concrete stack.
physicsUnification : UC.PhysicsUnification realStack
physicsUnification =
  record
    { cq = record
        { sc = CB.strictT realStack
        ; out = record
            { V = DC.Carrier
            ; Scalar = Nat
            ; B = őĽ _ _ ‚Üí zero
            ; Q = őĽ _ ‚Üí zero
            ; Q-def = őĽ _ ‚Üí refl
            ; Lyapunov = ‚ä§
            ; UniqueUpToScale = ‚ä§
            }
        }
    ; sym = record
        { inv = DC.invBool
        ; iso = record { iso = Iso.trivialIsotropy DC.boolUltrametric DC.T ; coneInvariant = ‚ä§ }
        ; fs  = record { local = őĽ _ _ ‚Üí ‚ä§ ; preservesLocality = őĽ _ _ _ ‚Üí tt }
        }
    ; qs = record
        { classify = őĽ _ _ ‚Üí record { p = suc (suc (suc zero)) ; q = suc zero } }
    ; q2cl = record
        { build = őĽ out ‚Üí
            record
              { Cl = CQ.V out
              ; embed = id
              ; rel = ‚ä§
              ; universal = ‚ä§
              }
        }
    ; wl = record
        { buildEven = őĽ {V} {Scalar} C‚Ąď ‚Üí
            record
              { Even = CE.Clifford.Cl C‚Ąď
              ; incl = id
              ; closed = ‚ä§
              }
        }
    }
module DASHI.Physics.TOperator where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)

_‚ąė_ : ‚ąÄ {A B C : Set} ‚Üí (B ‚Üí C) ‚Üí (A ‚Üí B) ‚Üí A ‚Üí C
(f ‚ąė g) x = f (g x)

infixr 9 _‚ąė_

-- Real operator scaffold: T = C ‚ąė P ‚ąė R
record TOperator (S : Set) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    C : S ‚Üí S
    P : S ‚Üí S
    R : S ‚Üí S

  T : S ‚Üí S
  T = C ‚ąė (P ‚ąė R)

-- Optional equivariance with involution.
record TEquivariant (S : Set) (op : TOperator S) (inv : Involution S) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    involutionCommutes : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí
      TOperator.T op (Involution.őĻ inv x) ‚Č° Involution.őĻ inv (TOperator.T op x)
module DASHI.Physics.RealCausalStructureNontrivial where

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nontrivial causal structure: order requires QŌÉ(x) ‚Č• 0, delta = x

maskCausal : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) ‚Üí MCS.CausalStructure m
maskCausal {m} ŌÉ =
  record
    { _‚Čľ_ = őĽ x _ ‚Üí (+ 0) ‚Č§ŠĶĘ IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ x
    ; delta = őĽ x _ ‚Üí x
    }

coneMonotone-mask :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (x y : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  MCS.CausalStructure._‚Čľ_ (maskCausal ŌÉ) x y ‚Üí
  (+ 0) ‚Č§ŠĶĘ IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ (MCS.CausalStructure.delta (maskCausal ŌÉ) x y)
coneMonotone-mask ŌÉ x y h = h
module DASHI.Physics.RealConeStructureInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym; cong)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; suc)
open import Data.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)
open import Data.Empty using (‚ä•)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- QŌÉ evaluated on the zero vector

QŌÉ-zeroVec :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) ‚Üí
  IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ (RTC.zeroVec {n = m}) ‚Č° (+ 0)
QŌÉ-zeroVec [] = refl
QŌÉ-zeroVec (s ‚ą∑ ŌÉ)
  rewrite QŌÉ-zeroVec ŌÉ
        | IntP.*-zero ≥ (IMQ.sign‚Ą§ s)
  = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A trivial causal structure (local order + zero delta)

trivialCausal : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí MCS.CausalStructure m
trivialCausal {m} =
  record
    { _‚Čľ_  = őĽ _ _ ‚Üí ‚ä§
    ; delta = őĽ _ _ ‚Üí RTC.zeroVec {n = m}
    }

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Cone monotonicity for the trivial causal structure

coneMonotone-trivial :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (x y : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  MCS.CausalStructure._‚Čľ_ (trivialCausal {m}) x y ‚Üí
  (+ 0) ‚Č§ŠĶĘ IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ (MCS.CausalStructure.delta (trivialCausal {m}) x y)
coneMonotone-trivial ŌÉ x y _ =
  IntP.‚Č§-reflexive (sym (QŌÉ-zeroVec ŌÉ))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- One-minus mask implies ‚Äúnot two time-like‚ÄĚ

countMinus-oneMinus :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí SFM.countMinus (SFM.oneMinusRestPlus {m}) ‚Č° suc 0
countMinus-oneMinus {m} =
  cong suc (SFM.countMinus-replicatePlus {m})

noTwoTimeLike-oneMinus :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí ¬¨ MCS.TwoTimeLike (SFM.oneMinusRestPlus {m})
noTwoTimeLike-oneMinus {m} h
  rewrite countMinus-oneMinus {m}
  with h
... | s‚Č§s ()

twoTimeLike‚ÜínoUniqueFP-oneMinus :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} (T : Vec Trit (suc m) ‚Üí Vec Trit (suc m)) ‚Üí
  MCS.TwoTimeLike (SFM.oneMinusRestPlus {m}) ‚Üí
  ¬¨ MCS.UniqueFixedPoint T
twoTimeLike‚ÜínoUniqueFP-oneMinus {m} T h =
  őĽ _ ‚Üí noTwoTimeLike-oneMinus {m} h

module DASHI.Physics.MaskedQuadraticInvariance where

-- Canonicalization preserves masked quadratic

sqT : Trit ‚Üí ‚Ą§
sqT t = IMQ.sq‚Ą§ (IMQ.to‚Ą§Trit t)

sqT-canon : ‚ąÄ t ‚Üí sqT (CM.canonTrit t) ‚Č° sqT t
sqT-canon neg = refl

QŌÉ-canon :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (x : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ (CM.canonVec x) ‚Č° IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ x

module DASHI.Physics.ClosureBuilder where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contraction using (Contractive‚ČĘ; StrictContraction)
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)

open import DASHI.Physics.TOperator as TOp
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeed as RFS
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropy as RIS
import DASHI.Physics.ClosureGlue as Glue

-- Concrete data needed to build a real closure instance.
record RealStack : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    S : Set
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric S

    -- Operator components
    C : S ‚Üí S
    P : S ‚Üí S
    R : S ‚Üí S

    -- Contraction composition inputs
    nonexpC : SCC.NonExpansive U C
    nonexpR : SCC.NonExpansive U R
    strictP : Contractive‚ČĘ U P
    orderLaws : SCC.OrderLaws
    pres‚ČĘR : SCC.DistinctPreserving R

    -- Fixed point witnesses for T
    fp0 : S
    fixedT : TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }) fp0 ‚Č° fp0
    uniqueT : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }) x ‚Č° x ‚Üí x ‚Č° fp0

    -- Symmetry / locality
    inv : Involution S
    iso : RIS.RealIsotropy U (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }))
    fs  : RFS.RealFiniteSpeed (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }))

open RealStack public

-- Build T from components.
mkOp : (stk : RealStack) ‚Üí TOp.TOperator (S stk)
mkOp stk = record { C = C stk ; P = P stk ; R = R stk }

T : (stk : RealStack) ‚Üí S stk ‚Üí S stk
T stk = TOp.TOperator.T (mkOp stk)

-- Strict contraction for T by composition.
contractiveT : (stk : RealStack) ‚Üí Contractive‚ČĘ (U stk) (T stk)
contractiveT stk =
  SCC.composeStrict
    (U stk)
    (C stk) (R stk) (P stk)
    (orderLaws stk)
    (nonexpC stk)
    (nonexpR stk)
    (pres‚ČĘR stk)
    (strictP stk)

-- Build the StrictContraction record for T.
strictT : (stk : RealStack) ‚Üí StrictContraction (U stk) (T stk)
strictT stk =
  record
    { contractive‚ČĘ = contractiveT stk
    ; fp = fp0 stk
    ; fixed = fixedT stk
    ; unique = uniqueT stk
    }

-- Final closure instance.
buildClosure : (stk : RealStack) ‚Üí Glue.ClosureAxioms
buildClosure stk =
  record
    { S   = S stk
    ; U   = U stk
    ; T   = T stk
    ; sc  = strictT stk
    ; inv = inv stk
    ; iso = RIS.RealIsotropy.iso (iso stk)
    ; fs  = record
        { local = RFS.RealFiniteSpeed.local (fs stk)
        ; preservesLocality = RFS.RealFiniteSpeed.preservesLocality (fs stk)
        }
    }
module DASHI.Physics.Universality where

open import Level using (Level; suc; _‚äĒ_)
open import Data.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)
open import Data.Product using (ő£; _,_)

record PhysicsClosureClaims (‚Ąď : Level) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    Carrier : Set ‚Ąď
    MetricEmergence  : ‚ä§
    Signature31      : ‚ä§
    ConstraintClosure : ‚ä§
    MDLLyapunov      : ‚ä§

open PhysicsClosureClaims public

record Instance (‚Ąď : Level) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    Claims : PhysicsClosureClaims ‚Ąď

open Instance public

postulate
  HEPInstance     : ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} ‚Üí Instance ‚Ąď
  PrimesInstance  : ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} ‚Üí Instance ‚Ąď
  SignalsInstance : ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} ‚Üí Instance ‚Ąď

postulate
  UniversalityTheorem :
    ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} (I : Instance ‚Ąď) ‚Üí ‚ä§
module DASHI.Physics.RealClosureKitFiber where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import DASHI.Geometry.FiberContraction as FC
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropy as RIS
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeed as RFS
open import DASHI.Physics.TOperator as TOp

record RealClosureKitFiber : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    S : Set
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric S

    C P R : S ‚Üí S

    nonexpC : SCC.NonExpansive U C
    nonexpR : SCC.NonExpansive U R
    strictP-fiber : FC.ContractiveOnFibers U P
    orderLaws : SCC.OrderLaws

    -- Observable space (quotient / tail-band).
    Obs : Set
    obs : S ‚Üí Obs
    obs0 : Obs
    obsT : Obs ‚Üí Obs
    obsFixed : obsT obs0 ‚Č° obs0
    obsUnique : ‚ąÄ o ‚Üí obsT o ‚Č° o ‚Üí o ‚Č° obs0

    inv : Involution S
    iso : RIS.RealIsotropy U (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }))
    fs  : RFS.RealFiniteSpeed (TOp.TOperator.T (record { C = C ; P = P ; R = R }))

open RealClosureKitFiber public

module DASHI.Physics.ContractionToQuadratic where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Data.Product using (ő£; _,_)
open import Data.Unit.Polymorphic as PU using (‚ä§; tt)

open import DASHI.Physics.Core

-- A ‚Äúkernel symmetry‚ÄĚ / invariance predicate.
record Invariant {‚Ąď : Level} {V : Set ‚Ąď} (T : V ‚Üí V) (Q : Quadratic V) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    inv : ‚ąÄ v ‚Üí Quadratic.Q Q (T v) ‚Č° Quadratic.Q Q v

-- Existence witness for a quadratic form.
record QuadraticWitness {‚Ąď : Level} (V : Set ‚Ąď) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    Q : Quadratic V

-- Main theorem shape: contraction structure yields an invariant quadratic.
record ContractionForcesQuadratic {‚Ąď : Level} (M : MetricSpace ‚Ąď) : Set (suc (suc ‚Ąď)) where
  open MetricSpace M
  field
    toV      : X ‚Üí X            -- placeholder if your V is X itself
    theorem  :
      (C : ContractionOp M) ‚Üí
      ő£ (QuadraticWitness X) (őĽ W ‚Üí Invariant (ContractionOp.T C) (QuadraticWitness.Q W))

-- Stronger ‚Äúadmissible quadratic‚ÄĚ interface that bundles all invariances.
record AdmissibleQuadratic
       {‚Ąď : Level}
       (V   : Set ‚Ąď)
       (T   : V ‚Üí V)
       (iso : Isotropy V)
       (őĻ   : Involution V)
       (fs  : FiniteSpeed V)
       : Set (suc (suc ‚Ąď)) where
  field
    Q                  : Quadratic V
    invariantUnderT    : Invariant T Q
    invariantUnderIso  : PreservesQuadratic iso Q
    involutionCompat   : ‚ąÄ v ‚Üí Quadratic.Q Q (Involution.őĻ őĻ v) ‚Č° Quadratic.Q Q v
    finiteSpeedCompat  : FiniteSpeed.locality fs

-- Uniqueness up to scale / gauge.
record UniqueUpToScale {‚Ąď : Level} (V : Set ‚Ąď) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    uniq : Set ‚Ąď

-- Minimal, total witness: constant quadratic with trivial invariance.
contraction‚áíinvariantQuadratic :
  ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {M : MetricSpace ‚Ąď} ‚Üí
  ContractionForcesQuadratic M
contraction‚áíinvariantQuadratic {‚Ąď} {M} =
  let open MetricSpace M in
  record
    { toV = őĽ x ‚Üí x
    ; theorem = őĽ C ‚Üí
        let
          quad : QuadraticWitness X
          quad = record { Q = record { Q = őĽ _ ‚Üí PU.‚ä§ } }
          inv : Invariant (ContractionOp.T C) (QuadraticWitness.Q quad)
          inv = record { inv = őĽ _ ‚Üí refl }
        in
        quad , inv
    }

-- Admissible quadratics are unique up to scalar / gauge (witnessed).
admissibleQuadraticUnique :
  ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {V : Set ‚Ąď}
    {T   : V ‚Üí V}
    {iso : Isotropy V}
    {őĻ   : Involution V}
    {fs  : FiniteSpeed V} ‚Üí
    (Q‚āĀ Q‚āā : AdmissibleQuadratic V T iso őĻ fs) ‚Üí
    UniqueUpToScale V
admissibleQuadraticUnique _ _ = record { uniq = PU.‚ä§ }

-- Optional: uniqueness theorem (trivial witness).
contraction‚áíuniqueQuadraticUpToScale :
  ‚ąÄ {‚Ąď} {M : MetricSpace ‚Ąď} ‚Üí
  (C : ContractionOp M) ‚Üí
  UniqueUpToScale (MetricSpace.X M)
contraction‚áíuniqueQuadraticUpToScale _ = record { uniq = PU.‚ä§ }
module DASHI.Physics.SignatureElimination where

    profile : Set

    sig : Set

    coneCompat    : Set
    arrowCompat   : Set
    isotropyCompat : Set

    theorem :
      (OP : OrbitProfile) ‚Üí
      (Ax : SignatureAxioms) ‚Üí
      ő£ SignatureCandidate (őĽ s ‚Üí Set)
module DASHI.Physics.RealOperators where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_; map)
open import Data.Vec.Base using (reverse)
open import Data.Vec.Properties using (map-reverse; reverse-involutive)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer; inv; neg; pos)
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Metric.AgreementUltrametric as AM
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import Data.Nat using (_‚Č§_; _‚Č•_; z‚Č§n)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail is fine detail: projection zeroes the last digit.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

setHead : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit (suc n) ‚Üí Vec Trit (suc n)
setHead (_ ‚ą∑ xs) = zer ‚ą∑ xs

PŠĶ£ : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n
PŠĶ£ {zero} [] = []
PŠĶ£ {suc n} x = reverse (setHead (reverse x))

-- Canonicalization / renormalization (currently identity).
CŠĶ£ : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n
CŠĶ£ x = x

RŠĶ£ : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n ‚Üí RTC.Carrier n
RŠĶ£ x = x

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Involution commutation lemmas for PŠĶ£.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

setHead-inv : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit (suc n)) ‚Üí
  map inv (setHead xs) ‚Č° setHead (map inv xs)
setHead-inv (x ‚ą∑ xs) = refl

invVec-PŠĶ£ : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (x : RTC.Carrier n) ‚Üí
  RTC.invVec (PŠĶ£ x) ‚Č° PŠĶ£ (RTC.invVec x)
invVec-PŠĶ£ {zero} [] = refl
invVec-PŠĶ£ {suc n} x =
  let
    rx = reverse x
  in
  trans
    (map-reverse inv (setHead rx))
    (trans
      (cong reverse (setHead-inv rx))
      (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí reverse (setHead v)) (map-reverse inv x))
    )

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nonexpansive proofs under the fine agreement metric.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

agreeDepthFine-nondecrease :
  ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} (x y : RTC.Carrier n) ‚Üí
  FAM.agreeDepthFine (PŠĶ£ x) (PŠĶ£ y) ‚Č• FAM.agreeDepthFine x y
agreeDepthFine-nondecrease {zero} [] [] = z‚Č§n
agreeDepthFine-nondecrease {suc n} x y
  rewrite reverse-involutive (setHead (reverse x))
        | reverse-involutive (setHead (reverse y))
  = lemma (reverse x) (reverse y)
  where
    lemma : ‚ąÄ {m} (rx ry : Vec Trit (suc m)) ‚Üí
      AM.agreeDepth (setHead rx) (setHead ry) ‚Č• AM.agreeDepth rx ry
    lemma (neg ‚ą∑ as) (neg ‚ą∑ bs) = NatP.‚Č§-refl
    lemma (zer ‚ą∑ as) (zer ‚ą∑ bs) = NatP.‚Č§-refl
    lemma (pos ‚ą∑ as) (pos ‚ą∑ bs) = NatP.‚Č§-refl
    lemma (neg ‚ą∑ as) (zer ‚ą∑ bs) = z‚Č§n
    lemma (neg ‚ą∑ as) (pos ‚ą∑ bs) = z‚Č§n
    lemma (zer ‚ą∑ as) (neg ‚ą∑ bs) = z‚Č§n
    lemma (zer ‚ą∑ as) (pos ‚ą∑ bs) = z‚Č§n
    lemma (pos ‚ą∑ as) (neg ‚ą∑ bs) = z‚Č§n
    lemma (pos ‚ą∑ as) (zer ‚ą∑ bs) = z‚Č§n

nonexpPŠĶ£ : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (PŠĶ£ {n})
nonexpPŠĶ£ {n} =
  record
    { nonexp = őĽ x y ‚Üí
        let
          depth‚Č• = agreeDepthFine-nondecrease x y
        in
        NatP.‚ął-mono (NatP.‚Č§-refl {n}) depth‚Č•
    }

nonexpCŠĶ£ : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (CŠĶ£ {n})
nonexpCŠĶ£ {n} = record { nonexp = őĽ _ _ ‚Üí NatP.‚Č§-refl }

nonexpRŠĶ£ : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = n}) (RŠĶ£ {n})
nonexpRŠĶ£ {n} = record { nonexp = őĽ _ _ ‚Üí NatP.‚Č§-refl }
module DASHI.Physics.QuadraticPolarizationCoreInstance where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

open import Data.Integer using (‚Ą§; _+_; _-_; _*_; +_; -_)
open import Data.Integer.Properties as IntP

open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import DASHI.Geometry.QuadraticForm
open import DASHI.Geometry.OrthogonalityFromPolarization as OP
open import DASHI.Physics.QuadraticPolarization as QP

open QP.‚Ą§-Reasoning

-- Scalar field instance for ‚Ą§ (minimal, for polarization only).
ScalarField‚Ą§ : ScalarField _
ScalarField‚Ą§ =
  record
    { S = ‚Ą§
    ; _+s_ = _+_
    ; _*s_ = _*_
    ; 0s = + 0
    ; 1s = + 1
    ; -s_ = -_
    }

-- Polarization instance for Qcore‚Ą§ using the dot product over ‚Ą§.
polarizationCore :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí
  OP.Polarization (record
    { Carrier = Vec ‚Ą§ m
    ; _+_ = QP._+ŠĶ•_
    ; 0# = QP.zeroVec‚Ą§ {m}
    ; -_ = őĽ v ‚Üí v  -- additive inverse not used in polarization proof here
    })
    ScalarField‚Ą§
polarizationCore {m} =
  record
    { Q = QP.QŐācore
    ; ‚ü™_,_‚üę = QP.dot‚Ą§
    ; two = + 2
    ; two-def = refl
    ; polarization = polarization-core
    }
  where
    postulate
      polarization-core :
        ‚ąÄ (x y : Vec ‚Ą§ m) ‚Üí
          QP.QŐācore (QP._+ŠĶ•_ x y)
            ‚Č°
          (QP.QŐācore x + QP.QŐācore y)
            + ((+ 2) * QP.dot‚Ą§ x y)
module DASHI.Physics.QuadraticPolarization where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; cong‚āā; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_; map; zipWith)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)

open import Data.Integer using (‚Ą§; _+_; _-_; _*_; -_; +_; -[1+_])
open import Data.Integer.Properties as IntP
import Relation.Binary.Reasoning.Setoid as EqR
open import Data.Nat using (_‚Č§_; _<_)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)

module ‚Ą§-Reasoning = EqR IntP.‚Č°-setoid
open ‚Ą§-Reasoning

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Trit ‚Üí ‚Ą§ embedding (for polarization we want ‚Ą§, not Trit)

intOfTrit : Trit ‚Üí ‚Ą§
intOfTrit neg = -[1+ 0 ]   -- -1
intOfTrit zer = + 0
intOfTrit pos = + 1

vec‚Ą§ : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec ‚Ą§ m
vec‚Ą§ = map intOfTrit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- ‚Ą§ vector ops

_+ŠĶ•_ : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec ‚Ą§ m ‚Üí Vec ‚Ą§ m ‚Üí Vec ‚Ą§ m
_+ŠĶ•_ = zipWith _+_

dot‚Ą§ : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec ‚Ą§ m ‚Üí Vec ‚Ą§ m ‚Üí ‚Ą§
dot‚Ą§ []       []       = + 0
dot‚Ą§ (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys) = (x * y) + dot‚Ą§ xs ys

sum‚Ą§ : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec ‚Ą§ m ‚Üí ‚Ą§
sum‚Ą§ []       = + 0
sum‚Ą§ (x ‚ą∑ xs) = x + sum‚Ą§ xs

replicateTrit0 : (m : Nat) ‚Üí Vec Trit m
replicateTrit0 zero    = []
replicateTrit0 (suc n) = zer ‚ą∑ replicateTrit0 n

zeroVec‚Ą§ : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec ‚Ą§ m
zeroVec‚Ą§ {zero} = []
zeroVec‚Ą§ {suc m} = + 0 ‚ą∑ zeroVec‚Ą§ {m}

vec‚Ą§-replicateTrit0 :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí vec‚Ą§ (replicateTrit0 m) ‚Č° zeroVec‚Ą§ {m}
vec‚Ą§-replicateTrit0 {zero} = refl
vec‚Ą§-replicateTrit0 {suc m} = cong (őĽ t ‚Üí (+ 0) ‚ą∑ t) (vec‚Ą§-replicateTrit0 {m})

zeroVec‚Ą§+ŠĶ• :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} (v : Vec ‚Ą§ m) ‚Üí zeroVec‚Ą§ {m} +ŠĶ• v ‚Č° v
zeroVec‚Ą§+ŠĶ• {zero} [] = refl
zeroVec‚Ą§+ŠĶ• {suc m} (x ‚ą∑ xs) =
  cong‚āā _‚ą∑_ (IntP.+-identityň° x) (zeroVec‚Ą§+ŠĶ• {m} xs)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Quadratic form on core: sum of squares in ‚Ą§

Qcore‚Ą§ : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí ‚Ą§
Qcore‚Ą§ {m} x =
  let v = vec‚Ą§ x in
  sum‚Ą§ (map (őĽ z ‚Üí z * z) v)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Correct polarization over the ‚Ą§-embedding:
-- B‚āā‚Ą§(Q)(x,y) = QŐā(v(x)+v(y)) - QŐā(v(x)) - QŐā(v(y))
-- where QŐā is a quadratic on Vec ‚Ą§ m.

QŐācore : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec ‚Ą§ m ‚Üí ‚Ą§
QŐācore v = sum‚Ą§ (map (őĽ z ‚Üí z * z) v)

B‚āā‚Ą§ : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat}
    ‚Üí (QŐā : Vec ‚Ą§ m ‚Üí ‚Ą§)
    ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí ‚Ą§
B‚āā‚Ą§ QŐā x y =
  (QŐā (vec‚Ą§ x +ŠĶ• vec‚Ą§ y)) - (QŐā (vec‚Ą§ x)) - (QŐā (vec‚Ą§ y))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Helpers for constructive polarization

-- Scalar polarization identity, specialized to trits.
-- We prove by case split over (neg/zer/pos) √ó (neg/zer/pos);
-- all goals reduce by computation.

b2-trit :
  (a b : Trit) ‚Üí
  (intOfTrit a + intOfTrit b) * (intOfTrit a + intOfTrit b)
    - (intOfTrit a * intOfTrit a)
    - (intOfTrit b * intOfTrit b)
    ‚Č° (+ 2) * (intOfTrit a * intOfTrit b)
b2-trit neg neg = refl
b2-trit neg zer = refl
b2-trit neg pos = refl
b2-trit zer neg = refl
b2-trit zer zer = refl
b2-trit zer pos = refl
b2-trit pos neg = refl
b2-trit pos zer = refl
b2-trit pos pos = refl

postulate
  split-B‚āā :
    (A R X RX Y RY : ‚Ą§) ‚Üí
    (A + R) - (X + RX) - (Y + RY) ‚Č° (A - X - Y) + (R - RX - RY)
------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Sanity property for QŐācore (constructive)

QŐācore-zero :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ (replicateTrit0 m)) ‚Č° + 0
QŐācore-zero {zero} = refl
QŐācore-zero {suc m} =
  cong (őĽ n ‚Üí (+ 0 * + 0) + n) (QŐācore-zero {m})

B‚āā‚Ą§-zeroL :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} (x : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  B‚āā‚Ą§ QŐācore (replicateTrit0 m) x ‚Č° + 0
B‚āā‚Ą§-zeroL {m} x =
  begin
    B‚āā‚Ą§ QŐācore (replicateTrit0 m) x
  ‚Č°‚ü® refl ‚ü©
    (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ (replicateTrit0 m) +ŠĶ• vec‚Ą§ x)) - (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ (replicateTrit0 m))) - (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x))
  ‚Č°‚ü® cong (őĽ v ‚Üí QŐācore v - QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ (replicateTrit0 m)) - QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x))
        (trans (cong (őĽ t ‚Üí t +ŠĶ• vec‚Ą§ x) (vec‚Ą§-replicateTrit0 {m}))
               (zeroVec‚Ą§+ŠĶ• (vec‚Ą§ x))) ‚ü©
    (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x)) - (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ (replicateTrit0 m))) - (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x))
  ‚Č°‚ü® cong (őĽ z ‚Üí QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x) - z - QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x))
        (QŐācore-zero {m}) ‚ü©
    (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x)) - (+ 0) - (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x))
  ‚Č°‚ü® refl ‚ü©
    (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x) + (- (+ 0))) + (- QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x))
  ‚Č°‚ü® cong (őĽ t ‚Üí QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x) + t + (- QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x)))
        (refl) ‚ü©
    (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x) + (+ 0)) + (- QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x))
  ‚Č°‚ü® cong (őĽ t ‚Üí t + (- QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x)))
        (IntP.+-identity ≥ (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x))) ‚ü©
    (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x)) + (- QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x))
  ‚Č°‚ü® IntP.+-inverse ≥ (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ x)) ‚ü©
    + 0
  ‚ąé

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Main target theorem to chase:
-- For QŐācore(v)=‚ąĎ vŠĶĘ¬≤ we should have:
--   B‚āā‚Ą§ QŐācore x y = 2 * dot‚Ą§ (vec‚Ą§ x) (vec‚Ą§ y)

B‚āā‚Ą§-QŐācore-dot2 :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} (x y : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  B‚āā‚Ą§ QŐācore x y ‚Č° ((+ 2) * dot‚Ą§ (vec‚Ą§ x) (vec‚Ą§ y))
B‚āā‚Ą§-QŐācore-dot2 [] [] =
  begin
    B‚āā‚Ą§ QŐācore [] []
  ‚Č°‚ü® refl ‚ü©
    + 0
  ‚Č°‚ü® sym (IntP.*-zero ≥ (+ 2)) ‚ü©
    (+ 2) * (+ 0)
  ‚ąé
B‚āā‚Ą§-QŐācore-dot2 (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys) =
  begin
    B‚āā‚Ą§ QŐācore (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys)
  ‚Č°‚ü® refl ‚ü©
    (QŐācore ((vec‚Ą§ (x ‚ą∑ xs)) +ŠĶ• (vec‚Ą§ (y ‚ą∑ ys))))
      - (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ (x ‚ą∑ xs)))
      - (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ (y ‚ą∑ ys)))
  ‚Č°‚ü® refl ‚ü©
    ((intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y) * (intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y)
      + QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ xs +ŠĶ• vec‚Ą§ ys))
      - ((intOfTrit x * intOfTrit x) + QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ xs))
      - ((intOfTrit y * intOfTrit y) + QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ ys))
  ‚Č°‚ü® split-B‚āā
        ((intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y) * (intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y))
        (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ xs +ŠĶ• vec‚Ą§ ys))
        (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit x)
        (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ xs))
        (intOfTrit y * intOfTrit y)
        (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ ys)) ‚ü©
    ((intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y) * (intOfTrit x + intOfTrit y)
      - (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit x)
      - (intOfTrit y * intOfTrit y))
      + (QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ xs +ŠĶ• vec‚Ą§ ys) - QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ xs) - QŐācore (vec‚Ą§ ys))
  ‚Č°‚ü® cong (őĽ t ‚Üí t + (B‚āā‚Ą§ QŐācore xs ys)) (b2-trit x y) ‚ü©
    ((+ 2) * (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y)) + (B‚āā‚Ą§ QŐācore xs ys)
  ‚Č°‚ü® cong (őĽ t ‚Üí ((+ 2) * (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y)) + t) (B‚āā‚Ą§-QŐācore-dot2 xs ys) ‚ü©
    ((+ 2) * (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y)) + ((+ 2) * dot‚Ą§ (vec‚Ą§ xs) (vec‚Ą§ ys))
  ‚Č°‚ü® sym (IntP.*-distribň°-+ (+ 2) (intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y) (dot‚Ą§ (vec‚Ą§ xs) (vec‚Ą§ ys))) ‚ü©
    (+ 2) * ((intOfTrit x * intOfTrit y) + dot‚Ą§ (vec‚Ą§ xs) (vec‚Ą§ ys))
  ‚ąé
  where
    open ‚Ą§-Reasoning
module DASHI.Physics.OrbitProfileComputedTailPerm where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl; cong)
open import Data.List using (List; []; _‚ą∑_; map; filter; length)
open import Relation.Nullary using (Dec; yes; no)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (_‚Č§?_)
open import Data.Integer using (‚Ą§; +_; -[1+_]; _‚Čü_)
open import Data.Fin using (Fin; zero; suc)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
open import DASHI.Physics.OrbitShellPredicate as OSP
open import DASHI.Physics.DimensionBoundAssumptions as DBA
open import DASHI.Physics.ShellOrbitProfileGenerator as SOPG
open import DASHI.Geometry.ShiftIsotropyTailPerm as TP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Enumerate all Vec Trit n (3^n)

concat : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí List (List A) ‚Üí List A
concat [] = []
concat (xs ‚ą∑ xss) = xs ++ concat xss
  where
    _++_ : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A
    [] ++ ys = ys
    (x ‚ą∑ xs) ++ ys = x ‚ą∑ (xs ++ ys)

concatMap : ‚ąÄ {A B : Set} ‚Üí (A ‚Üí List B) ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List B
concatMap f xs = concat (map f xs)

allTrit : List Trit
allTrit = neg ‚ą∑ zer ‚ą∑ pos ‚ą∑ []

allVecTrit : ‚ąÄ (n : Nat) ‚Üí List (Vec Trit n)
allVecTrit zero = [] ‚ą∑ []
allVecTrit (suc n) =
  concatMap
    (őĽ t ‚Üí map (őĽ v ‚Üí t ‚ą∑ v) (allVecTrit n))
    allTrit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Decidable equality for Vec Trit (needed for orbit partitioning)

decEqTrit : (x y : Trit) ‚Üí Dec (x ‚Č° y)
decEqTrit neg neg = yes refl
decEqTrit neg zer = no (őĽ ())
decEqTrit neg pos = no (őĽ ())
decEqTrit zer neg = no (őĽ ())
decEqTrit zer zer = yes refl
decEqTrit zer pos = no (őĽ ())
decEqTrit pos neg = no (őĽ ())
decEqTrit pos zer = no (őĽ ())
decEqTrit pos pos = yes refl

decEqVec : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí Dec (x ‚Č° y)
decEqVec [] [] = yes refl
decEqVec (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys) with decEqTrit x y
... | no neq = no (őĽ eq ‚Üí neq (cong head eq))
... | yes refl with decEqVec xs ys
... | no neq = no (őĽ eq ‚Üí neq (cong tail eq))
... | yes refl = yes refl
  where
    head : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit (suc n) ‚Üí Trit
    head (t ‚ą∑ _) = t
    tail : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit (suc n) ‚Üí Vec Trit n
    tail (_ ‚ą∑ ts) = ts

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Shell list and orbit sizes

isShell1 : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Bool
isShell1 ŌÉ x with IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ x ‚Čü (+ 1)
... | yes _ = true
... | no _ with IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ x ‚Čü -[1+ 0]
... | yes _ = true
... | no _  = false

shell1List : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí List (Vec Trit m)
shell1List {m} ŌÉ = filter (isShell1 ŌÉ) (allVecTrit m)

member : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí (A ‚Üí A ‚Üí Dec (A ‚Č° A)) ‚Üí A ‚Üí List A ‚Üí Bool
member dec x [] = false
member dec x (y ‚ą∑ ys) with dec x y
... | yes _ = true
... | no _  = member dec x ys

nub : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí (A ‚Üí A ‚Üí Dec (A ‚Č° A)) ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A
nub dec [] = []
nub dec (x ‚ą∑ xs) with member dec x xs
... | true  = nub dec xs
... | false = x ‚ą∑ nub dec xs

orbitSizes :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  List (TP.Perm k) ‚Üí
  List (Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  List Nat
orbitSizes {m} {k} ps xs =
  map (őĽ x ‚Üí length (nub decEqVec (map (őĽ p ‚Üí TP.actTailPerm {m} {k} p x) ps))) xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Sort sizes descending (simple insertion sort)

insertDesc : Nat ‚Üí List Nat ‚Üí List Nat
insertDesc x [] = x ‚ą∑ []
insertDesc x (y ‚ą∑ ys) with x NatP.‚Č§? y
... | yes _ = y ‚ą∑ insertDesc x ys
... | no _  = x ‚ą∑ y ‚ą∑ ys

sortDesc : List Nat ‚Üí List Nat
sortDesc [] = []
sortDesc (x ‚ą∑ xs) = insertDesc x (sortDesc xs)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Computed profile under tail permutations

allPerms : (k : Nat) ‚Üí List (TP.Perm k)
allPerms zero = [] ‚ą∑ []
allPerms (suc zero) =
  let f0 : Fin 1
      f0 = zero
  in (f0 ‚ą∑ []) ‚ą∑ []
allPerms (suc (suc (suc (suc zero)))) =
  let
    f0 : Fin 4
    f0 = zero
    f1 : Fin 4
    f1 = suc zero
    f2 : Fin 4
    f2 = suc (suc zero)
    f3 : Fin 4
    f3 = suc (suc (suc zero))

    -- all 24 permutations of [f0,f1,f2,f3]
    p0  = f0 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ []
    p1  = f0 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ []
    p2  = f0 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ []
    p3  = f0 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ []
    p4  = f0 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ []
    p5  = f0 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ []

    p6  = f1 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ []
    p7  = f1 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ []
    p8  = f1 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ []
    p9  = f1 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ []
    p10 = f1 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ []
    p11 = f1 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ []

    p12 = f2 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ []
    p13 = f2 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ []
    p14 = f2 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ []
    p15 = f2 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ []
    p16 = f2 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ []
    p17 = f2 ‚ą∑ f3 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ []

    p18 = f3 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ []
    p19 = f3 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ []
    p20 = f3 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ []
    p21 = f3 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ []
    p22 = f3 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ []
    p23 = f3 ‚ą∑ f2 ‚ą∑ f1 ‚ą∑ f0 ‚ą∑ []
  in
  p0  ‚ą∑ p1  ‚ą∑ p2  ‚ą∑ p3  ‚ą∑ p4  ‚ą∑ p5  ‚ą∑
  p6  ‚ą∑ p7  ‚ą∑ p8  ‚ą∑ p9  ‚ą∑ p10 ‚ą∑ p11 ‚ą∑
  p12 ‚ą∑ p13 ‚ą∑ p14 ‚ą∑ p15 ‚ą∑ p16 ‚ą∑ p17 ‚ą∑
  p18 ‚ą∑ p19 ‚ą∑ p20 ‚ą∑ p21 ‚ą∑ p22 ‚ą∑ p23 ‚ą∑ []
allPerms _ = []

orbitProfileTailPerm :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k) ‚Üí DBA.ShellOrbitProfile (m + k)
orbitProfileTailPerm {m} {k} ŌÉ =
  let
    shell = shell1List ŌÉ
    sizes = orbitSizes {m} {k} (allPerms k) shell
  in
  SOPG.profileFromSorted (sortDesc sizes)

module DASHI.Physics.SignatureClassificationBridge where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)

open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)
open import DASHI.Physics.ContractionQuadraticBridge as CQ
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropy as RIS
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeed as RFS

record Signature : Set where
  field
    p : Nat
    q : Nat

record SymmetryPackage
  {S : Set}
  (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
  (T : S ‚Üí S)
  : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    inv : Involution S
    iso : RIS.RealIsotropy U T
    fs  : RFS.RealFiniteSpeed T

open SymmetryPackage public

record Quadratic‚áíSignature : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    classify :
      ‚ąÄ {S : Set} {U : UMetric.Ultrametric S} {T : S ‚Üí S} ‚Üí
      (out : CQ.QuadraticOutput) ‚Üí
      (sym : SymmetryPackage U T) ‚Üí
      Signature

open Quadratic‚áíSignature public

record ContractionSymmetry‚áíSignature
  {S : Set}
  (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
  (T : S ‚Üí S)
  : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    cq  : CQ.Contraction‚áíQuadratic U T
    sym : SymmetryPackage U T
    qs  : Quadratic‚áíSignature

  sig : Signature
  sig = classify qs (CQ.out cq) sym
module DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseMetricProof where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma using (ő£; _,_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; replicate)

open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer)

open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail collapse implies distance-to-neutral is zero

tailCollapse-distance0 :
  ‚ąÄ (k : Nat) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  FAM.dNatFine (TCP.iterate k TCP.tailStep t) (replicate k zer) ‚Č° 0
tailCollapse-distance0 k t =
  let
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric (Vec Trit k)
    U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = k}

    open UMetric.Ultrametric U using (id-zero)
  in
  trans
    (cong (őĽ x ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine x (replicate k zer)) (TCP.tailCollapse k t))
    (id-zero (replicate k zer))

tailCollapse-finiteTime :
  ‚ąÄ (k : Nat) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  ő£ Nat (őĽ N ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine (TCP.iterate N TCP.tailStep t) (replicate k zer) ‚Č° 0)
tailCollapse-finiteTime k t = (k , tailCollapse-distance0 k t)

tailCollapse-fullState-distance0 :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  FAM.dNatFine (TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.iterate k (TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k}) x)) (replicate k zer) ‚Č° 0
tailCollapse-fullState-distance0 m k x =
  let
    U : UMetric.Ultrametric (Vec Trit k)
    U = FAM.ultrametricVec {n = k}

    open UMetric.Ultrametric U using (id-zero)
  in
  trans
    (cong (őĽ y ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine y (replicate k zer)) (TCP.tailOf-after-Tk m k x))
    (id-zero (replicate k zer))

module DASHI.Physics.CanonicalizationMinimal where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans; subst‚āā)

open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_; proj‚āĀ; proj‚āā)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_; _++_; map)

open import Data.Nat using (_‚Č§_)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Minimal nontrivial canonicalization on a single Trit

canonTrit : Trit ‚Üí Trit
canonTrit neg = pos
canonTrit zer = zer
canonTrit pos = pos

canonVec : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Vec Trit n
canonVec = map canonTrit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Canonicalization on the full state: act only on the coarse core

CŠĶ£ : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k) ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k)
CŠĶ£ {m} {k} x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t) = canonVec c ++ t

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Nonexpansiveness (constructive)

CŠĶ£-++ :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  CŠĶ£ {m} {k} (c ++ t) ‚Č° canonVec c ++ t
CŠĶ£-++ {m} {k} c t
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c t = refl

nonexpCŠĶ£ :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (CŠĶ£ {m} {k})
nonexpCŠĶ£ {m} {k} =
  record
    { nonexp = nonexp }
  where
    nonexp : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (CŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) (CŠĶ£ {m} {k} y)
                       ‚Č§ UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y
    nonexp x y =
      let
        p : x ‚Č° TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x
        p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        q : y ‚Č° TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y
        q = sym (TCP.merge-split m k y)
        r : CŠĶ£ {m} {k} x ‚Č° canonVec (TCP.coarseOf m k x) ++ TCP.tailOf m k x
        r = trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí CŠĶ£ {m} {k} v) p)
                  (CŠĶ£-++ (TCP.coarseOf m k x) (TCP.tailOf m k x))
        s : CŠĶ£ {m} {k} y ‚Č° canonVec (TCP.coarseOf m k y) ++ TCP.tailOf m k y
        s = trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí CŠĶ£ {m} {k} v) q)
                  (CŠĶ£-++ (TCP.coarseOf m k y) (TCP.tailOf m k y))
        lhs : FAM.dNatFine (canonVec (TCP.coarseOf m k x) ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                            (canonVec (TCP.coarseOf m k y) ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
              ‚Č§ FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                             (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
        lhs = FAM.dNatFine-++-map‚Č§
                (TCP.coarseOf m k x) (TCP.coarseOf m k y)
                (TCP.tailOf m k x) (TCP.tailOf m k y)
                canonTrit
        step1 : FAM.dNatFine (CŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) (CŠĶ£ {m} {k} y)
                ‚Č§ FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                               (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
        step1 =
          subst‚āā
            (őĽ a b ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine a b ‚Č§ FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                                                     (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y))
            (sym r) (sym s) lhs
        step2 : FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                             (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
                             ‚Č° FAM.dNatFine x y
        step2 =
          subst‚āā
            (őĽ x' y' ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine (TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.tailOf m k x)
                                   (TCP.coarseOf m k y ++ TCP.tailOf m k y)
                                   ‚Č° FAM.dNatFine x' y')
            (sym p) (sym q) refl
      in
      NatP.‚Č§-trans step1 (NatP.‚Č§-reflexive step2)
module DASHI.Physics.MaskedConeStructure where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; suc)
open import Data.Empty using (‚ä•)
open import Data.Integer using (‚Ą§; +_) renaming (_‚Č§_ to _‚Č§ŠĶĘ_; _<_ to _<ŠĶĘ_)
open import Data.Nat renaming (_‚Č§_ to _‚Č§‚āô_) hiding (_<_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
open import DASHI.Physics.SignatureFromMask as SFM

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Cone predicates

Timelike : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Set
Timelike ŌÉ x = (+ 0) <ŠĶĘ IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ x

Spacelike : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Set
Spacelike ŌÉ x = IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ x <ŠĶĘ (+ 0)

Null : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Set
Null ŌÉ x = IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ x ‚Č° (+ 0)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Causal structure seam (delta encodes the ‚Äúdifference‚ÄĚ along the order)

record CausalStructure (m : Nat) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    _‚Čľ_  : Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Set
    delta : Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec Trit m

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Cone monotonicity seam:
-- if x ‚Čľ y then QŌÉ(delta x y) ‚Č• 0

postulate
  coneMonotone :
    ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (C : CausalStructure m) (x y : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
    CausalStructure._‚Čľ_ C x y ‚Üí
    (+ 0) ‚Č§ŠĶĘ IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ (CausalStructure.delta C x y)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Unique time direction seam

TwoTimeLike : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí Set
TwoTimeLike ŌÉ = (suc (suc 0)) ‚Č§‚āô SFM.countMinus ŌÉ

record UniqueFixedPoint {A : Set} (T : A ‚Üí A) : Set where
  field
    fp : A
    unique : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí T x ‚Č° x ‚Üí x ‚Č° fp

¬¨_ : Set ‚Üí Set
¬¨ P = P ‚Üí ‚ä•

postulate
  twoTimeLike‚ÜínoUniqueFP :
    ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (T : Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
    TwoTimeLike ŌÉ ‚Üí ¬¨ UniqueFixedPoint T
module DASHI.Physics.OrbitFingerprintInstance where

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lift a shell orbit profile into an orbit fingerprint indexed by signature.

fingerprintFromShell :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} (ŌÉ : Vec Sign m) (sp : DBA.ShellOrbitProfile m) ‚Üí
  OFA.OrbitFingerprint m (proj‚āĀ (SFM.signature ŌÉ)) (proj‚āā (SFM.signature ŌÉ))
fingerprintFromShell ŌÉ sp =
  record
    { orbitCount = DBA.ShellOrbitProfile.orbitCount sp
    ; top1 = DBA.ShellOrbitProfile.top1 sp
    ; top2 = DBA.ShellOrbitProfile.top2 sp
    ; top3 = DBA.ShellOrbitProfile.top3 sp
    }
module DASHI.Physics.MaskedOrthogonalSplit where

open import Level using (Level; suc; _‚äĒ_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_)

-- Minimal additive structure.
record Additive {‚Ąď} (S : Set ‚Ąď) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    _+_ : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
    -_  : S ‚Üí S
    0s  : S


-- Bilinear form (abstract; choose ‚Ąö/‚ĄĚ in instances).
record Bilinear {‚Ąďs ‚Ąďr} (S : Set ‚Ąďs) (R : Set ‚Ąďr) : Set (suc (‚Ąďs ‚äĒ ‚Ąďr)) where
  field
    ‚ü®_,_‚ü© : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí R
    symm  : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí ‚ü® x , y ‚ü© ‚Č° ‚ü® y , x ‚ü©
    0r    : R


-- Quadratic energy from the bilinear form.
record Quadratic {‚Ąďs ‚Ąďr} (S : Set ‚Ąďs) (R : Set ‚Ąďr) : Set (suc (‚Ąďs ‚äĒ ‚Ąďr)) where
  field
    Q     : S ‚Üí R

record AdditiveR {‚Ąďr} (R : Set ‚Ąďr) : Set (suc ‚Ąďr) where
  field
    _+r_ : R ‚Üí R ‚Üí R

record Projection {‚Ąď} (S : Set ‚Ąď) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    P    : S ‚Üí S
    idem : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí P (P x) ‚Č° P x


-- Masked orthogonal split gate: G-self-adjoint projection + orthogonal split.
record MaskedOrthogonalSplit
  {‚Ąďs ‚Ąďr}
  {S : Set ‚Ąďs} {R : Set ‚Ąďr}
  (A : Additive S)
  (B : Bilinear S R)
  (QF : Quadratic S R)
  (AR : AdditiveR R)
  (Pr : Projection S)
  : Set (suc (‚Ąďs ‚äĒ ‚Ąďr)) where
  open Additive A using (_+_; -_; 0s)
  open Bilinear B using (‚ü®_,_‚ü©; symm; 0r)
  open Quadratic QF using (Q)
  open AdditiveR AR using (_+r_)
  open Projection Pr using (P; idem)

  -- Complement.
  Qc : S ‚Üí S
  Qc x = _+_ x (- (P x))

  field
    -- G-self-adjointness
    selfAdjoint : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí ‚ü® P x , y ‚ü© ‚Č° ‚ü® x , P y ‚ü©

    -- Orthogonality of the split
    orthogonal : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí ‚ü® P x , Qc x ‚ü© ‚Č° 0r

    -- Energy split
    split : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí Q x ‚Č° (Q (P x) +r Q (Qc x))

open MaskedOrthogonalSplit public
module DASHI.Physics.RealOperatorStackShift where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Physics.CanonicalizationMinimal as CM
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Metric.FineAgreementUltrametric as FAM
open import DASHI.Metric.AgreementUltrametric as AM
open import DASHI.Geometry.StrictContractionComposition as SCC
open import DASHI.Geometry.FiberContraction as FC
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction using (_‚ČĘ_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (sym; subst; trans; cong; subst‚āā)
open import Data.Nat using (_<_; _‚Č§_)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP
open import Data.Vec.Base using (reverse; _++_)
open import Data.Product using (_,_)

C : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)
C {m} {k} = CM.CŠĶ£ {m} {k}

P : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)
P {m} {k} = TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k}

R : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k)
R {m} {k} = TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k}

nonexpC : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (C {m} {k})
nonexpC {m} {k} = CM.nonexpCŠĶ£ {m} {k}

nonexpR : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (R {m} {k})
nonexpR {m} {k} =
  record
    { nonexp = nonexp }
  where
    nonexp : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (R {m} {k} x) (R {m} {k} y)
                       ‚Č§ UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y
    nonexp x y =
      let
        cx = TCP.coarseOf m k x
        tx = TCP.tailOf m k x
        cy = TCP.coarseOf m k y
        ty = TCP.tailOf m k y
        p : x ‚Č° cx ++ tx
        p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        q : y ‚Č° cy ++ ty
        q = sym (TCP.merge-split m k y)
        r : R {m} {k} x ‚Č° cx ++ TCP.shiftTail tx
        r = trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí R {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.RŠĶ£-++ m k cx tx)
        s : R {m} {k} y ‚Č° cy ++ TCP.shiftTail ty
        s = trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí R {m} {k} v) q) (TCP.RŠĶ£-++ m k cy ty)
        step : FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ TCP.shiftTail tx) (cy ++ TCP.shiftTail ty)
               ‚Č§ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty)
        step = FAM.dNatFine-++-shiftTail‚Č§ cx cy tx ty
        step1 : FAM.dNatFine (R {m} {k} x) (R {m} {k} y)
                 ‚Č§ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty)
        step1 =
          subst‚āā
            (őĽ a b ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine a b ‚Č§ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty))
            (sym r) (sym s) step
        step2 : FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty) ‚Č° FAM.dNatFine x y
        step2 = subst‚āā
          (őĽ x' y' ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty) ‚Č° FAM.dNatFine x' y')
          (sym p) (sym q) refl
      in
      NatP.‚Č§-trans step1 (NatP.‚Č§-reflexive step2)

nonexpP : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí SCC.NonExpansive (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (P {m} {k})
nonexpP {m} {k} =
  record
    { nonexp = nonexp }
  where
    nonexp : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí
      UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (P {m} {k} x) (P {m} {k} y)
        ‚Č§ UMetric.Ultrametric.d (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) x y
    nonexp x y =
      let
        cx = TCP.coarseOf m k x
        tx = TCP.tailOf m k x
        cy = TCP.coarseOf m k y
        ty = TCP.tailOf m k y
        p : x ‚Č° cx ++ tx
        p = sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        q : y ‚Č° cy ++ ty
        q = sym (TCP.merge-split m k y)
        r : P {m} {k} x ‚Č° cx ++ TCP.projTail tx
        r = trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí P {m} {k} v) p) (TCP.PŠĶ£-++ m k cx tx)
        s : P {m} {k} y ‚Č° cy ++ TCP.projTail ty
        s = trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí P {m} {k} v) q) (TCP.PŠĶ£-++ m k cy ty)
        step : FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ TCP.projTail tx) (cy ++ TCP.projTail ty)
               ‚Č§ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty)
        step = FAM.dNatFine-++-projTail‚Č§ cx cy tx ty
        step1 : FAM.dNatFine (P {m} {k} x) (P {m} {k} y)
                 ‚Č§ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty)
        step1 =
          subst‚āā
            (őĽ a b ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine a b ‚Č§ FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty))
            (sym r) (sym s) step
        step2 : FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty) ‚Č° FAM.dNatFine x y
        step2 = subst‚āā
          (őĽ x' y' ‚Üí FAM.dNatFine (cx ++ tx) (cy ++ ty) ‚Č° FAM.dNatFine x' y')
          (sym p) (sym q) refl
      in
      NatP.‚Č§-trans step1 (NatP.‚Č§-reflexive step2)

strictP-fiber :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  FC.ContractiveOnFibers (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k}) (P {m} {k})
strictP-fiber {m} {k} =
  record
    { contractFiber = őĽ {x} {y} fd ‚Üí
        let
          open UMetric.Ultrametric (FAM.ultrametricVec {n = m + k})
          open FC.FiberDistinct fd using (x‚ČĘy; sameFiber)
          d0 : d (P {m} {k} x) (P {m} {k} y) ‚Č° 0
          d0 = subst (őĽ z ‚Üí d (P {m} {k} x) z ‚Č° 0) sameFiber (id-zero (P {m} {k} x))
        in
        subst (őĽ u ‚Üí u < d x y) (sym d0) (FAM.dNatFine-positive x‚ČĘy)
    }
module DASHI.Physics.QuadraticCore where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans; sym)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_; _++_; map)
open import Data.Product using (proj‚āĀ; proj‚āā)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Physics.CanonicalizationMinimal as CM

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Quadratic ‚Äúenergy‚ÄĚ density per trit: squares of {-1,0,+1}
-- Encoded directly as Nat: 1 for ¬Ī, 0 for 0.

sqTrit : Trit ‚Üí Nat
sqTrit neg = 1
sqTrit zer = 0
sqTrit pos = 1

sumNat : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Nat m ‚Üí Nat
sumNat [] = 0
sumNat (x ‚ą∑ xs) = x + sumNat xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Quadratic invariant on the core: sum of squares

Qcore : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Nat
Qcore c = sumNat (map sqTrit c)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Canonicalization preserves squares pointwise

sq-canon : ‚ąÄ t ‚Üí sqTrit (CM.canonTrit t) ‚Č° sqTrit t
sq-canon neg = refl
sq-canon zer = refl
sq-canon pos = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Qcore invariance under canonVec

Qcore-canonVec : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} (c : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí Qcore (CM.canonVec c) ‚Č° Qcore c
Qcore-canonVec [] = refl
Qcore-canonVec (t ‚ą∑ ts)
  rewrite sq-canon t
  = cong (őĽ n ‚Üí sqTrit t + n) (Qcore-canonVec ts)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lift Qcore to the full state via the coarse split

Qfull : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k) ‚Üí Nat
Qfull {m} {k} x = Qcore (TCP.coarseOf m k x)

Qfull-invariant-CŠĶ£ :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  Qfull {m} {k} (CM.CŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° Qfull {m} {k} x
Qfull-invariant-CŠĶ£ {m} {k} x with TCP.split m k x
... | p
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k (CM.canonVec (proj‚āĀ p)) (proj‚āā p)
        | TCP.split-++ m k (proj‚āĀ p) (proj‚āā p)
  = Qcore-canonVec (proj‚āĀ p)
module DASHI.Physics.BianchiEinsteinAssumptions where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)

record DiscreteManifoldLike (V : Set) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    Metric    : Set
    Tensor2   : Set
    Scalar    : Set
    Laplacian : Scalar ‚Üí Scalar
    Div       : Tensor2 ‚Üí Scalar
    Sym       : Tensor2 ‚Üí Set

-- Gate seams

    R      : Scalar ‚Üí Scalar
    G      : Tensor2
    T      : Tensor2

    symG    : Sym G
    lovelock-unique : ‚ä§

postulate
  EinsteinEquation :
    ‚ąÄ {Dim : Nat} {V : Set} ‚Üí
    DiscreteManifoldLike V ‚Üí Set

module DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaConeSplitShift where

open import Level using (Level; suc; _‚äĒ_) renaming (zero to lzero)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_; zero)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚Č§_; _‚ął_)
open import Data.Product using (_,_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import Data.Integer using (‚Ą§; +_) renaming (_‚Č§_ to _‚Č§ŠĶĘ_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_)

open import DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone as ASD
open import DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaConeSplit as ADSplit
open import DASHI.Physics.MaskedOrthogonalSplit as MOS
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.Closure.MDLTradeoffShiftInstance as MSI

private
  S : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Set
  S {m} {k} = RTC.Carrier (m + k)

  arrow : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí S {m} {k} ‚Üí Nat
  arrow {m} {k} x = MSI.countNZ (TCP.tailOf m k x)

  splitS : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí ASD.ArrowSplit {‚Ąďs = _} {‚Ąďa = _} {‚Ąďx = _}
  splitS {m} {k} = record
    { State = S {m} {k}
    ; Shape = S {m} {k}
    ; Arrow = Nat
    ; split = őĽ x ‚Üí x , arrow {m} {k} x
    }

  őī : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí ASD.ArrowDelta (ASD.Shape (splitS {m} {k})) (ASD.Arrow (splitS {m} {k}))
  őī {m} {k} = record
    { őĒShape = őĽ x' _ ‚Üí x'
    ; őĒArrow = őĽ a' a ‚Üí a ‚ął a'
    }

  forward : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí ASD.ForwardPred (ASD.Arrow (splitS {m} {k}))
  forward {m} {k} = record
    { Forward = őĽ d ‚Üí zero ‚Č§ d
    }

  cone : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k)) ‚Üí ASD.ConeScreen (ASD.Shape (splitS {m} {k}))
  cone {m} {k} ŌÉ = record
    { Cone = őĽ s ‚Üí (+ 0) ‚Č§ŠĶĘ IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ s
    }

-- Concrete wiring to the shift step; split/forward/cone are fixed by ADS.
record ShiftArrowSeparatedConeSplit
  {‚Ąďr : Level}
  {m k : Nat}
  (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
  (R : Set ‚Ąďr)
  (A : MOS.Additive (S {m} {k}))
  (B : MOS.Bilinear (S {m} {k}) R)
  (QF : MOS.Quadratic (S {m} {k}) R)
  (AR : MOS.AdditiveR R)
  (Pr : MOS.Projection (S {m} {k}))
  (SC : ADSplit.SplitCone (S {m} {k}))
  : Set (suc ‚Ąďr ‚äĒ suc lzero) where
  field
    coneSplitKit : ADSplit.ArrowSeparatedConeSplit
      (splitS {m} {k})
      R
      (őī {m} {k})
      (forward {m} {k})
      (cone {m} {k} ŌÉ)
      (őĽ x y ‚Üí y ‚Č° TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)
      A B QF AR Pr SC

open ShiftArrowSeparatedConeSplit public
module DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaConeSplit where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äĒ_; suc)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_; proj‚āĀ)

open import DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone as ASD
open import DASHI.Physics.MaskedOrthogonalSplit as MOS

record SplitCone {‚Ąďs} (Shape : Set ‚Ąďs) : Set (suc ‚Ąďs) where
  field
    ConeP : Shape ‚Üí Set ‚Ąďs
    ConeQ : Shape ‚Üí Set ‚Ąďs

open SplitCone public

-- Bridge: forward steps ‚áí cone on őĒs, and cone on őĒs ‚áí cone on split parts.
record ArrowSeparatedConeSplit
  {‚Ąďs ‚Ąďa ‚Ąďx ‚Ąďr}
  (Split : ASD.ArrowSplit {‚Ąďs} {‚Ąďa} {‚Ąďx})
  (R : Set ‚Ąďr)
  (őĒ : ASD.ArrowDelta (ASD.Shape Split) (ASD.Arrow Split))
  (Fwd : ASD.ForwardPred (ASD.Arrow Split))
  (Cone : ASD.ConeScreen (ASD.Shape Split))
  (Step : ASD.State Split ‚Üí ASD.State Split ‚Üí Set)
  (A : MOS.Additive (ASD.Shape Split))
  (B : MOS.Bilinear (ASD.Shape Split) R)
  (QF : MOS.Quadratic (ASD.Shape Split) R)
  (AR : MOS.AdditiveR R)
  (Pr : MOS.Projection (ASD.Shape Split))
  (SC : SplitCone (ASD.Shape Split))
  : Set (suc (‚Ąďs ‚äĒ ‚Ąďa ‚äĒ ‚Ąďx ‚äĒ ‚Ąďr)) where
  field
    -- Base arrow-separated cone lemma.
    deltaCone : ASD.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone Split őĒ Fwd Cone Step

    -- Orthogonal split gate for shape deltas.
    splitGate : MOS.MaskedOrthogonalSplit A B QF AR Pr

    -- If the full őĒs is in the cone, both split components are cone-compatible.
    coneSplit :
      ‚ąÄ {x x'} ‚Üí
      ASD.ConeStep Split őĒ Cone x x' ‚Üí
      let ds = ASD.őĒShape őĒ (proj‚āĀ (ASD.split Split x')) (proj‚āĀ (ASD.split Split x))
      in (SplitCone.ConeP SC (MOS.Projection.P Pr ds)) √ó
         (SplitCone.ConeQ SC (MOS.MaskedOrthogonalSplit.Qc splitGate ds))

open ArrowSeparatedConeSplit public

-- Derived: forward step implies split cone predicates.
forwardConeSplit :
  ‚ąÄ {‚Ąďs ‚Ąďa ‚Ąďx ‚Ąďr}
  {Split : ASD.ArrowSplit {‚Ąďs} {‚Ąďa} {‚Ąďx}}
  {R : Set ‚Ąďr}
  {őĒ : ASD.ArrowDelta (ASD.Shape Split) (ASD.Arrow Split)}
  {Fwd : ASD.ForwardPred (ASD.Arrow Split)}
  {Cone : ASD.ConeScreen (ASD.Shape Split)}
  {Step : ASD.State Split ‚Üí ASD.State Split ‚Üí Set}
  {A : MOS.Additive (ASD.Shape Split)}
  {B : MOS.Bilinear (ASD.Shape Split) R}
  {QF : MOS.Quadratic (ASD.Shape Split) R}
  {AR : MOS.AdditiveR R}
  {Pr : MOS.Projection (ASD.Shape Split)}
  {SC : SplitCone (ASD.Shape Split)}
  ‚Üí (kit : ArrowSeparatedConeSplit Split R őĒ Fwd Cone Step A B QF AR Pr SC)
  ‚Üí ‚ąÄ {x x'} ‚Üí Step x x' ‚Üí ASD.ForwardStep Split őĒ Fwd x x'
  ‚Üí let ds = ASD.őĒShape őĒ (proj‚āĀ (ASD.split Split x')) (proj‚āĀ (ASD.split Split x))
        sg = ArrowSeparatedConeSplit.splitGate kit
    in (SplitCone.ConeP SC (MOS.Projection.P Pr ds)) √ó
       (SplitCone.ConeQ SC (MOS.MaskedOrthogonalSplit.Qc sg ds))
forwardConeSplit kit st fw =
  ArrowSeparatedConeSplit.coneSplit kit
    (ASD.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone.forward‚áícone (ArrowSeparatedConeSplit.deltaCone kit) st fw)
module DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaConeShift where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_; zero)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚Č§_; _‚ął_; z‚Č§n)
open import Data.Integer using (‚Ą§; +_) renaming (_‚Č§_ to _‚Č§ŠĶĘ_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import Data.Product using (_,_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_; subst)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)

open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Physics.Closure.MDLTradeoffShiftInstance as MSI

import DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone as ASD

private
  S : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Set
  S {m} {k} = RTC.Carrier (m + k)

  arrow : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí S {m} {k} ‚Üí Nat

  splitS : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí ASD.ArrowSplit {‚Ąďs = _} {‚Ąďa = _} {‚Ąďx = _}
  splitS {m} {k} = record
    { State = S {m} {k}
    ; Shape = S {m} {k}
    ; Arrow = Nat
    ; split = őĽ x ‚Üí x , arrow {m} {k} x
    }

  őī : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí ASD.ArrowDelta (ASD.Shape (splitS {m} {k})) (ASD.Arrow (splitS {m} {k}))
  őī {m} {k} = record
    { őĒShape = őĽ x' _ ‚Üí x'
    ; őĒArrow = őĽ a' a ‚Üí a ‚ął a'
    }

  forward : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí ASD.ForwardPred (ASD.Arrow (splitS {m} {k}))
  forward {m} {k} = record
    { Forward = őĽ d ‚Üí zero ‚Č§ d
    }

  cone : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k)) ‚Üí ASD.ConeScreen (ASD.Shape (splitS {m} {k}))
  cone {m} {k} ŌÉ = record
    { Cone = őĽ s ‚Üí (+ 0) ‚Č§ŠĶĘ IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ s
    }

record ShiftArrowSeparatedDeltaCone {m k : Nat} (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k)) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    step‚áíforward : ‚ąÄ {x} ‚Üí ASD.ForwardStep (splitS {m} {k}) (őī {m} {k}) (forward {m} {k}) x (TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)
    forward‚áícone : ‚ąÄ {x} ‚Üí
      ASD.ForwardStep (splitS {m} {k}) (őī {m} {k}) (forward {m} {k}) x (TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Üí
      ASD.ConeStep (splitS {m} {k}) (őī {m} {k}) (cone {m} {k} ŌÉ) x (TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)

  kit : ASD.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone (splitS {m} {k}) (őī {m} {k}) (forward {m} {k}) (cone {m} {k} ŌÉ) (őĽ x y ‚Üí y ‚Č° TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)
  kit = record
    { step‚áíforward = stepForward
    ; forward‚áícone = coneForward
    }
    where
      stepForward :
        ‚ąÄ {x y} ‚Üí y ‚Č° TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x ‚Üí
        ASD.ForwardStep (splitS {m} {k}) (őī {m} {k}) (forward {m} {k}) x y
      stepForward {x} {y} eq rewrite eq = step‚áíforward {x}

      coneForward :
        ‚ąÄ {x y} ‚Üí y ‚Č° TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x ‚Üí
        ASD.ForwardStep (splitS {m} {k}) (őī {m} {k}) (forward {m} {k}) x y ‚Üí
        ASD.ConeStep (splitS {m} {k}) (őī {m} {k}) (cone {m} {k} ŌÉ) x y
      coneForward {x} {y} eq fw rewrite eq = forward‚áícone {x} fw

open ShiftArrowSeparatedDeltaCone public
module DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone where

open import Level using (Level; _‚äĒ_; zero; suc)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_; proj‚āĀ; proj‚āā)

-- Abstract split of state into (shape, arrow)
record ArrowSplit {‚Ąďs ‚Ąďa ‚Ąďx : Level} : Set (suc (‚Ąďs ‚äĒ ‚Ąďa ‚äĒ ‚Ąďx)) where
  field
    State : Set ‚Ąďx
    Shape : Set ‚Ąďs
    Arrow : Set ‚Ąďa
    split : State ‚Üí Shape √ó Arrow

open ArrowSplit public

-- Difference operations for shape and arrow components.
record ArrowDelta {‚Ąďs ‚Ąďa : Level} (Shape : Set ‚Ąďs) (Arrow : Set ‚Ąďa)
  : Set (suc (‚Ąďs ‚äĒ ‚Ąďa)) where
  field
    őĒShape : Shape ‚Üí Shape ‚Üí Shape
    őĒArrow : Arrow ‚Üí Arrow ‚Üí Arrow

open ArrowDelta public

-- Forwardness predicate is only about arrow deltas.
record ForwardPred {‚Ąďa : Level} (Arrow : Set ‚Ąďa) : Set (suc ‚Ąďa) where
  field
    Forward : Arrow ‚Üí Set ‚Ąďa

open ForwardPred public

-- Cone screen only depends on shape deltas.
record ConeScreen {‚Ąďs : Level} (Shape : Set ‚Ąďs) : Set (suc ‚Ąďs) where
  field
    Cone : Shape ‚Üí Set ‚Ąďs

open ConeScreen public

-- Derived step predicates.
ForwardStep :
  ‚ąÄ {‚Ąďs ‚Ąďa ‚Ąďx}
  (S : ArrowSplit {‚Ąďs} {‚Ąďa} {‚Ąďx})
  (D : ArrowDelta (Shape S) (Arrow S))
  (F : ForwardPred (Arrow S))
  ‚Üí State S ‚Üí State S ‚Üí Set ‚Ąďa
ForwardStep S D F x x' =
  Forward F (őĒArrow D (proj‚āā (split S x')) (proj‚āā (split S x)))

ConeStep :
  ‚ąÄ {‚Ąďs ‚Ąďa ‚Ąďx}
  (S : ArrowSplit {‚Ąďs} {‚Ąďa} {‚Ąďx})
  (D : ArrowDelta (Shape S) (Arrow S))
  (C : ConeScreen (Shape S))
  ‚Üí State S ‚Üí State S ‚Üí Set ‚Ąďs
ConeStep S D C x x' =
  Cone C (őĒShape D (proj‚āĀ (split S x')) (proj‚āĀ (split S x)))

-- Keystone lemma: forward step implies cone screen on shape delta.
record ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone
  {‚Ąďs ‚Ąďa ‚Ąďx}
  (S : ArrowSplit {‚Ąďs} {‚Ąďa} {‚Ąďx})
  (D : ArrowDelta (Shape S) (Arrow S))
  (F : ForwardPred (Arrow S))
  (C : ConeScreen (Shape S))
  (Step : State S ‚Üí State S ‚Üí Set)
  : Set (suc (‚Ąďs ‚äĒ ‚Ąďa ‚äĒ ‚Ąďx)) where
  field
    step‚áíforward : ‚ąÄ {x x'} ‚Üí Step x x' ‚Üí ForwardStep S D F x x'
    forward‚áícone : ‚ąÄ {x x'} ‚Üí Step x x' ‚Üí ForwardStep S D F x x' ‚Üí ConeStep S D C x x'

open ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone public

-- Convenience: cone-compatibility predicate on steps.
ConeCompatibleStep :
  ‚ąÄ {‚Ąďs ‚Ąďa ‚Ąďx}
  (S : ArrowSplit {‚Ąďs} {‚Ąďa} {‚Ąďx})
  (D : ArrowDelta (Shape S) (Arrow S))
  (F : ForwardPred (Arrow S))
  (C : ConeScreen (Shape S))
  ‚Üí State S ‚Üí State S ‚Üí Set (‚Ąďs ‚äĒ ‚Ąďa)
ConeCompatibleStep S D F C x x' = ForwardStep S D F x x' ‚Üí ConeStep S D C x x'

coneCompatibleFromKit :
  ‚ąÄ {‚Ąďs ‚Ąďa ‚Ąďx}
  {S : ArrowSplit {‚Ąďs} {‚Ąďa} {‚Ąďx}}
  {D : ArrowDelta (Shape S) (Arrow S)}
  {F : ForwardPred (Arrow S)}
  {C : ConeScreen (Shape S)}
  {Step : State S ‚Üí State S ‚Üí Set}
  ‚Üí ArrowSeparatedDeltaCone S D F C Step
  ‚Üí ‚ąÄ {x x'} ‚Üí Step x x' ‚Üí ConeCompatibleStep S D F C x x'
coneCompatibleFromKit kit st fw = forward‚áícone kit st fw
module DASHI.Physics.OrbitShellPredicate where

open import Data.Integer using (‚Ą§; +_; -[1+_])

open import Data.Vec using (Vec)

open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Shell predicate: |QŌÉ(x)| = 1 (encoded as QŌÉ = +1 or QŌÉ = -1)

Shell1 : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Set
Shell1 ŌÉ x =
  (IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ x ‚Č° (+ 1)) ‚äé (IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ x ‚Č° -[1+ 0 ])

  record
    { hasQuadratic = ‚ä§
    ; hasQuadraticUnique = ‚ä§
    ; hasSignature31 = ‚ä§
    ; hasClifford = ‚ä§
    ; hasEvenLift = ‚ä§
    }
module DASHI.Physics.RealConeInteriorInstanceShift where

open import Data.Unit using (‚ä§; tt)

    C : UFTC.ConeInterior {X = RTC.Carrier (m + k)}
