module DASHI.Physics.ClosureInstance where

open import DASHI.Physics.ClosureGlue as Glue
open import DASHI.Physics.TOperator
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealFiniteSpeed
open import DASHI.Geometry.RealIsotropy
open import Contraction
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)

-- Bundle real (non-toy) closure data.
record RealClosureInstance : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    S   : Set
    U   : UMetric.Ultrametric S
    op  : TOperator S
    sc  : StrictContraction U (TOperator.T op)
    inv : Involution S
    iso : RealIsotropy U (TOperator.T op)
    fs  : RealFiniteSpeed (TOperator.T op)

-- Convert real closure instance into the common ClosureAxioms.
toClosureAxioms : RealClosureInstance ‚Üí Glue.ClosureAxioms
toClosureAxioms inst =
  record
    { S   = RealClosureInstance.S inst
    ; U   = RealClosureInstance.U inst
    ; T   = TOperator.T (RealClosureInstance.op inst)
    ; sc  = RealClosureInstance.sc inst
    ; inv = RealClosureInstance.inv inst
    ; iso = RealIsotropy.iso (RealClosureInstance.iso inst)
    ; fs  = record
        { local = RealFiniteSpeed.local (RealClosureInstance.fs inst)
        ; preservesLocality = RealFiniteSpeed.preservesLocality (RealClosureInstance.fs inst)
        }
    }

module DASHI.Physics.ShellOrbitProfileGenerator where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.List using (List; []; _‚ą∑_; length)

open import DASHI.Physics.DimensionBoundAssumptions as DBA

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Build a ShellOrbitProfile from a sorted (descending) list of orbit sizes.
-- This keeps the generator concrete while still allowing external data.
------------------------------------------------------------------------

profileFromSorted :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí List Nat ‚Üí DBA.ShellOrbitProfile m
profileFromSorted {m} sizes =
  let
    top1 : Nat
    top1 with sizes
    ... | a ‚ą∑ _ = a
    ... | []    = 0

    top2 : Nat
    top2 with sizes
    ... | _ ‚ą∑ b ‚ą∑ _ = b
    ... | _         = 0

    top3 : Nat
    top3 with sizes
    ... | _ ‚ą∑ _ ‚ą∑ c ‚ą∑ _ = c
    ... | _             = 0
  in
  record
    { orbitCount = length sizes
    ; top1 = top1
    ; top2 = top2
    ; top3 = top3
    }
module DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_; proj‚āĀ; proj‚āā)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_; _++_; replicate)
open import Data.Vec.Base using (take; init; last; _‚ą∑ ≥_)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete, nontrivial renormalization RŠĶ£ implementing a ‚Äúscale shift‚ÄĚ
------------------------------------------------------------------------

split :
  ‚ąÄ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) ‚Üí
  Vec A (m + k) ‚Üí (Vec A m √ó Vec A k)
split {A} zero    k xs       = ([] , xs)
split {A} (suc m) k (x ‚ą∑ xs) with split {A} m k xs
... | (c , t) = (x ‚ą∑ c , t)

split-++ :
  ‚ąÄ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) (c : Vec A m) (t : Vec A k) ‚Üí
  split m k (c ++ t) ‚Č° (c , t)
split-++ zero k [] t = refl
split-++ (suc m) k (x ‚ą∑ xs) t =
  cong (őĽ p ‚Üí (x ‚ą∑ proj‚āĀ p , proj‚āā p)) (split-++ m k xs t)

coarseOf : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) ‚Üí Vec A (m + k) ‚Üí Vec A m
coarseOf m k x = proj‚āĀ (split m k x)

tailOf : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) ‚Üí Vec A (m + k) ‚Üí Vec A k
tailOf m k x = proj‚āā (split m k x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tail-band operators

shiftTail : ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit k ‚Üí Vec Trit k
shiftTail {zero}    []       = []
shiftTail {suc k‚Ä≤}  (x ‚ą∑ xs) = xs ‚ą∑ ≥ zer

projTail : ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit k ‚Üí Vec Trit k
projTail {zero}    []       = []
projTail {suc k‚Ä≤}  t        = (init t) ‚ą∑ ≥ zer


tailStep : ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit k ‚Üí Vec Trit k
tailStep t = projTail (shiftTail t)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lift tail-band operators to full state

RŠĶ£ : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k) ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k)
RŠĶ£ {m} {k} x with split m k x
... | (c , t) = c ++ shiftTail t

PŠĶ£ : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k) ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k)
PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x with split m k x
... | (c , t) = c ++ projTail t

RŠĶ£-++ :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  RŠĶ£ {m} {k} (c ++ t) ‚Č° c ++ shiftTail t
RŠĶ£-++ m k c t rewrite split-++ m k c t = refl

PŠĶ£-++ :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  PŠĶ£ {m} {k} (c ++ t) ‚Č° c ++ projTail t
PŠĶ£-++ m k c t rewrite split-++ m k c t = refl


TŠĶ£ : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k) ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k)
TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x = PŠĶ£ {m} {k} (RŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Iteration

iterate : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí (A ‚Üí A) ‚Üí A ‚Üí A
iterate zero    f x = x
iterate (suc n) f x = iterate n f (f x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Finite-time tail collapse

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Helper lemmas for replicate

init-replicate :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí init (replicate (suc k) zer) ‚Č° replicate k zer
init-replicate {zero} = refl
init-replicate {suc k} =
  cong (őĽ t ‚Üí zer ‚ą∑ t) (init-replicate {k})

snoc-replicate :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí (replicate k zer) ‚ą∑ ≥ zer ‚Č° replicate (suc k) zer
snoc-replicate {zero} = refl
snoc-replicate {suc k} =
  cong (őĽ t ‚Üí zer ‚ą∑ t) (snoc-replicate {k})

tailStep-forgets-last :
  ‚ąÄ {k‚Ä≤ : Nat} (t : Vec Trit (suc k‚Ä≤)) ‚Üí
  tailStep t ‚Č° projTail (shiftTail t)
tailStep-forgets-last {k‚Ä≤} t = refl

projTail-replicate :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí projTail (replicate k zer) ‚Č° replicate k zer
projTail-replicate {zero}    = refl
projTail-replicate {suc k‚Ä≤}  =
  trans
    (cong (_‚ą∑ ≥ zer) (init-replicate {k‚Ä≤}))
    (snoc-replicate {k‚Ä≤})

shiftTail-replicate :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí shiftTail (replicate k zer) ‚Č° replicate k zer
shiftTail-replicate {zero}   = refl
shiftTail-replicate {suc k‚Ä≤} =
  snoc-replicate {k‚Ä≤}

tailStep-replicate :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} ‚Üí tailStep (replicate k zer) ‚Č° replicate k zer
tailStep-replicate {k} =
  trans (cong projTail (shiftTail-replicate {k}))
        (projTail-replicate {k})

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Extra Vec lemmas needed for constructive nilpotence
------------------------------------------------------------------------

pair-ő∑ : ‚ąÄ {A B : Set} (p : A √ó B) ‚Üí (proj‚āĀ p , proj‚āā p) ‚Č° p
pair-ő∑ (a , b) = refl

init-‚ą∑ ≥ : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} {n : Nat} (xs : Vec A n) (a : A) ‚Üí init (xs ‚ą∑ ≥ a) ‚Č° xs
init-‚ą∑ ≥ {n = zero}    []       a = refl
init-‚ą∑ ≥ {n = suc n} (x ‚ą∑ xs) a rewrite init-‚ą∑ ≥ xs a = refl

projTail-idem :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí projTail (projTail t) ‚Č° projTail t
projTail-idem {zero} [] = refl
projTail-idem {suc k‚Ä≤} t =
  trans
    (cong (_‚ą∑ ≥ zer) (init-‚ą∑ ≥ (init t) zer))
    refl

PŠĶ£-idem :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  PŠĶ£ {m} {k} (PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x
PŠĶ£-idem m k x with split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite PŠĶ£-++ m k c t
        | PŠĶ£-++ m k c (projTail t)
        | projTail-idem t
  = refl

tailStep‚Č°shiftTail : ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí tailStep t ‚Č° shiftTail t
tailStep‚Č°shiftTail {zero}    [] = refl
tailStep‚Č°shiftTail {suc k‚Ä≤} (x ‚ą∑ xs)
  rewrite init-‚ą∑ ≥ xs zer
  = refl

shiftTail-‚ą∑ ≥-zer :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (xs : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  shiftTail (xs ‚ą∑ ≥ zer) ‚Č° (shiftTail xs) ‚ą∑ ≥ zer
shiftTail-‚ą∑ ≥-zer {zero} [] = refl
shiftTail-‚ą∑ ≥-zer {suc k} (x ‚ą∑ xs) = refl

iterate-shiftTail-‚ą∑ ≥-zer :
  ‚ąÄ {k : Nat} (n : Nat) (xs : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  iterate n shiftTail (xs ‚ą∑ ≥ zer) ‚Č° (iterate n shiftTail xs) ‚ą∑ ≥ zer
iterate-shiftTail-‚ą∑ ≥-zer zero xs = refl
iterate-shiftTail-‚ą∑ ≥-zer (suc n) xs
  rewrite shiftTail-‚ą∑ ≥-zer xs
        | iterate-shiftTail-‚ą∑ ≥-zer n (shiftTail xs)
  = refl

iterate-pointwise :
  ‚ąÄ {A : Set} (n : Nat) (f g : A ‚Üí A) (x : A) ‚Üí
  (‚ąÄ y ‚Üí f y ‚Č° g y) ‚Üí
  iterate n f x ‚Č° iterate n g x
iterate-pointwise zero f g x fg = refl
iterate-pointwise (suc n) f g x fg
  rewrite fg x
  = iterate-pointwise n f g (g x) fg

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Finite-time tail collapse (constructive)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

tailCollapse-shiftTail :
  ‚ąÄ (k : Nat) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  iterate k shiftTail t ‚Č° replicate k zer
tailCollapse-shiftTail zero    []       = refl
tailCollapse-shiftTail (suc k) (x ‚ą∑ xs) =
  trans
    (iterate-shiftTail-‚ą∑ ≥-zer k xs)
    (trans
      (cong (_‚ą∑ ≥ zer) (tailCollapse-shiftTail k xs))
      (snoc-replicate {k}))

tailCollapse :
  ‚ąÄ (k : Nat) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  iterate k tailStep t ‚Č° replicate k zer
tailCollapse k t =
  trans
    (iterate-pointwise k tailStep shiftTail t (őĽ y ‚Üí tailStep‚Č°shiftTail y))
    (tailCollapse-shiftTail k t)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lifted corollary: full state tail band collapses in k steps

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Lifted corollary: full state tail band collapses in k steps (constructive)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

merge-split :
  ‚ąÄ {A : Set} (m k : Nat) (x : Vec A (m + k)) ‚Üí
  (coarseOf m k x ++ tailOf m k x) ‚Č° x
merge-split {A} zero    k x = refl
merge-split {A} (suc m) k (x ‚ą∑ xs)
  rewrite merge-split {A} m k xs
  = refl

TŠĶ£-++ :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  TŠĶ£ {m} {k} (c ++ t) ‚Č° c ++ tailStep t
TŠĶ£-++ m k c t
  rewrite RŠĶ£-++ m k c t
        | PŠĶ£-++ m k c (shiftTail t)
  = refl

split-TŠĶ£ :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  split m k (TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° (coarseOf m k x , tailStep (tailOf m k x))
split-TŠĶ£ m k x with split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite RŠĶ£-++ m k c t
        | PŠĶ£-++ m k c (shiftTail t)
        | split-++ m k c (projTail (shiftTail t))
  = refl

split-iterate-TŠĶ£ :
  ‚ąÄ (m k n : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  split m k (iterate n (TŠĶ£ {m} {k}) x) ‚Č°
    ( coarseOf m k x
    , iterate n tailStep (tailOf m k x)
    )
split-iterate-TŠĶ£ m k zero x
  = sym (pair-ő∑ (split m k x))
split-iterate-TŠĶ£ m k (suc n) x
  rewrite split-iterate-TŠĶ£ m k n (TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)
        | split-TŠĶ£ m k x
  = refl

tailOf-after-Tk :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  tailOf m k (iterate k (TŠĶ£ {m} {k}) x) ‚Č° replicate k zer
tailOf-after-Tk m k x =
  trans
    (cong proj‚āā (split-iterate-TŠĶ£ m k k x))
    (tailCollapse k (tailOf m k x))
module DASHI.Physics.RealConeInteriorFromMask where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)

open import UFTC_Lattice as UFTC
open import DASHI.Physics.MaskedConeStructure as MCS
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)

-- Cone interior/boundary from a signature mask.

coneInteriorFromMask {m} ŌÉ =
  record
    { InInterior = MCS.Timelike ŌÉ
    ; Boundary = MCS.Null ŌÉ
    }
module DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_; map)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; inv; inv-invol; zer)

Carrier : Nat ‚Üí Set
Carrier n = Vec Trit n

invVec : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Carrier n ‚Üí Carrier n
invVec {n} = map inv

invVec-invol : ‚ąÄ {n} (x : Carrier n) ‚Üí invVec (invVec x) ‚Č° x
invVec-invol [] = refl
invVec-invol (t ‚ą∑ ts) rewrite inv-invol t | invVec-invol ts = refl

zeroVec : ‚ąÄ {n} ‚Üí Carrier n
zeroVec {n = zero} = []
zeroVec {n = suc n} = zer ‚ą∑ zeroVec {n}

module DASHI.Physics.OrbitSignatureDiscriminant where

-- Candidate signatures in 4D.
data Signature : Set where
  sig40 : Signature
  sig31 : Signature
  sig22 : Signature
  sig13 : Signature
  sig04 : Signature

Profile : Set
Profile = List Nat

record OrbitProfile (ŌÉ : Signature) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    profile : Profile

postulate
  -- Orbit profile computed from the discrete shell for a signature.
  ProfileOf : Signature ‚Üí Profile

  -- Injectivity of the profile map on the candidate set.
  OrbitProfileInjective :
    ‚ąÄ ŌÉ ŌÉ' ‚Üí ProfileOf ŌÉ ‚Č° ProfileOf ŌÉ' ‚Üí ŌÉ ‚Č° ŌÉ'

  -- Measured profile (e.g., imported from external scan).
  MeasuredProfile : Profile
  MeasuredSignature : Signature
  measured-profile-def : MeasuredProfile ‚Č° ProfileOf MeasuredSignature

SignatureFromMeasuredProfile :
  MeasuredProfile ‚Č° ProfileOf sig31 ‚Üí MeasuredSignature ‚Č° sig31
SignatureFromMeasuredProfile h =
  OrbitProfileInjective MeasuredSignature sig31
    (trans (sym measured-profile-def) h)
module DASHI.Physics.DefaultClosure where

open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚Č§_; _<_; _‚äĒ_; z‚Č§n; s‚Č§s)
open import Data.Empty using (‚ä•; ‚ä•-elim)

open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contraction using (Contractive‚ČĘ; StrictContraction)
open import DASHI.Combinatorics.Entropy using (Involution)
import DASHI.Physics.ClosureGlue as Glue
open import DASHI.Physics.ClosureStatusFromGlue
open import DASHI.Physics.UnificationClosure

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete, total instance to close the physics glue
------------------------------------------------------------------------

_‚ČĘ_ : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí A ‚Üí A ‚Üí Set
x ‚ČĘ y = x ‚Č° y ‚Üí ‚ä•

Carrier : Set
Carrier = Bool

-- Discrete ultrametric on Bool: 0 if equal, 1 otherwise.
dBool : Carrier ‚Üí Carrier ‚Üí Nat
dBool true  true  = zero
dBool false false = zero
dBool true  false = suc zero
dBool false true  = suc zero

id-zeroBool : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí dBool x x ‚Č° 0
id-zeroBool true  = refl
id-zeroBool false = refl

symBool : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí dBool x y ‚Č° dBool y x
symBool true  true  = refl
symBool false false = refl
symBool true  false = refl
symBool false true  = refl

ultratriangleBool : ‚ąÄ x y z ‚Üí dBool x z ‚Č§ (dBool x y ‚äĒ dBool y z)
ultratriangleBool true  true  true  = z‚Č§n
ultratriangleBool true  true  false = s‚Č§s z‚Č§n
ultratriangleBool true  false true  = z‚Č§n
ultratriangleBool true  false false = s‚Č§s z‚Č§n
ultratriangleBool false true  true  = s‚Č§s z‚Č§n
ultratriangleBool false true  false = z‚Č§n
ultratriangleBool false false true  = s‚Č§s z‚Č§n
ultratriangleBool false false false = z‚Č§n

boolUltrametric : UMetric.Ultrametric Carrier
boolUltrametric =
  record
    { d = dBool
    ; id-zero = id-zeroBool
    ; symmetric = symBool
    ; ultratriangle = ultratriangleBool
    }

-- Constant contraction to false.
T : Carrier ‚Üí Carrier
T _ = false

contractiveBool-proof : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí x ‚ČĘ y ‚Üí dBool (T x) (T y) < dBool x y
contractiveBool-proof true  false _   = s‚Č§s z‚Č§n
contractiveBool-proof false true  _   = s‚Č§s z‚Č§n
contractiveBool-proof true  true  x‚ČĘy = ‚ä•-elim (x‚ČĘy refl)
contractiveBool-proof false false x‚ČĘy = ‚ä•-elim (x‚ČĘy refl)

contractiveBool : Contraction.Contractive‚ČĘ boolUltrametric T
contractiveBool =
  record
    { contraction‚ČĘ = őĽ {x} {y} x‚ČĘy ‚Üí
        contractiveBool-proof x y x‚ČĘy
    }

boolTrueNeqFalse : false ‚Č° true ‚Üí ‚ä•
boolTrueNeqFalse ()

uniqueBool : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí T x ‚Č° x ‚Üí x ‚Č° false
uniqueBool true  hx = ‚ä•-elim (boolTrueNeqFalse hx)
uniqueBool false _  = refl

strictBool : Contraction.StrictContraction boolUltrametric T
strictBool =
  record
    { contractive‚ČĘ = contractiveBool
    ; fp = false
    ; fixed = refl
    ; unique = uniqueBool
    }

invBool : Involution Carrier
invBool = record
  { őĻ = őĽ x ‚Üí x
  ; invol = őĽ _ ‚Üí refl
  }

defaultClosure : Glue.ClosureAxioms
defaultClosure = Glue.mkDefaultClosure boolUltrametric T strictBool invBool

defaultClosureStatus : ClosureStatus
defaultClosureStatus = closureStatusFromGlue defaultClosure

    -- factorization property left abstract for now

module DASHI.Physics.SignatureFromMask where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; cong‚āā)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)

open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic using (Sign; plus; minus)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Count plus/minus in a mask and extract signature

countPlus : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Sign m ‚Üí Nat
countPlus [] = 0
countPlus (plus  ‚ą∑ ŌÉ) = suc (countPlus ŌÉ)
countPlus (minus ‚ą∑ ŌÉ) = countPlus ŌÉ

countMinus : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Sign m ‚Üí Nat
countMinus [] = 0
countMinus (plus  ‚ą∑ ŌÉ) = countMinus ŌÉ
countMinus (minus ‚ą∑ ŌÉ) = suc (countMinus ŌÉ)

signature : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Sign m ‚Üí Nat √ó Nat
signature ŌÉ = (countMinus ŌÉ , countPlus ŌÉ)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete mask constructor: one minus, rest plus

replicatePlus : ‚ąÄ (k : Nat) ‚Üí Vec Sign k
replicatePlus zero    = []
replicatePlus (suc k) = plus ‚ą∑ replicatePlus k

oneMinusRestPlus : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Sign (suc m)
oneMinusRestPlus {m} = minus ‚ą∑ replicatePlus m

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Signature of the concrete mask

countPlus-replicatePlus :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí countPlus (replicatePlus m) ‚Č° m
countPlus-replicatePlus {zero} = refl
countPlus-replicatePlus {suc m} =
  cong suc (countPlus-replicatePlus {m})

countMinus-replicatePlus :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí countMinus (replicatePlus m) ‚Č° 0
countMinus-replicatePlus {zero} = refl
countMinus-replicatePlus {suc m} = countMinus-replicatePlus {m}

signature-oneMinus :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí signature (oneMinusRestPlus {m}) ‚Č° (suc 0 , m)
signature-oneMinus {m} =
  cong‚āā _,_
    (cong suc (countMinus-replicatePlus {m}))
    (countPlus-replicatePlus {m})

  field

module DASHI.Physics.MaskedOrthogonalSplitConstructive where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_; _++_; zipWith)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)
open import Data.Integer using (‚Ą§; _*_; +_; 0‚Ą§) renaming (_+_ to _+‚Ą§_)
open import Data.Integer.Properties as IntP

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer)
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Zero vectors

zeros : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit n
zeros {n = zero}  = []
zeros {n = suc n} = zer ‚ą∑ zeros {n = n}

embedCore : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k)
embedCore {m} {k} c = c ++ zeros {n = k}

embedTail : ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit k ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k)
embedTail {m} {k} t = zeros {n = m} ++ t

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- dotŌÉ unfolds to a recursive definition

dotŌÉ-cons :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} (s : IMQ.Sign) (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign m)
    (x : Trit) (xs : Vec Trit m)
    (y : Trit) (ys : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  IMQ.dotŌÉ (s ‚ą∑ ŌÉ) (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys)
    ‚Č° (IMQ.sign‚Ą§ s * (IMQ.to‚Ą§Trit x * IMQ.to‚Ą§Trit y)) +‚Ą§ IMQ.dotŌÉ ŌÉ xs ys
dotŌÉ-cons s ŌÉ x xs y ys = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- dotŌÉ against a zero vector is 0

dotŌÉ-zero-left :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (y : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  IMQ.dotŌÉ ŌÉ (zeros {n = m}) y ‚Č° 0‚Ą§
dotŌÉ-zero-left [] [] = refl
dotŌÉ-zero-left (s ‚ą∑ ŌÉ) (y ‚ą∑ ys) =
  trans
    (dotŌÉ-cons s ŌÉ zer (zeros {n = _}) y ys)
    (trans
    (cong (őĽ z ‚Üí z +‚Ą§ IMQ.dotŌÉ ŌÉ (zeros {n = _}) ys)
            (trans
              (cong (őĽ t ‚Üí IMQ.sign‚Ą§ s * t) (IntP.*-zeroň° (IMQ.to‚Ą§Trit y)))
              (IntP.*-zero ≥ (IMQ.sign‚Ą§ s))))
      (cong (őĽ z ‚Üí 0‚Ą§ +‚Ą§ z) (dotŌÉ-zero-left ŌÉ ys)))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Core and tail are orthogonal under dotŌÉ

dotŌÉ-core‚ä•tail :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  IMQ.dotŌÉ ŌÉ (embedCore {m} {k} c) (embedTail {m} {k} t) ‚Č° 0‚Ą§
dotŌÉ-core‚ä•tail {zero} {k} ŌÉ [] t = dotŌÉ-zero-left ŌÉ t
dotŌÉ-core‚ä•tail {suc m} {k} (s ‚ą∑ ŌÉ) (x ‚ą∑ xs) t =
  trans
    (dotŌÉ-cons s ŌÉ x (xs ++ zeros {n = k}) zer (zeros {n = m} ++ t))
    (trans
    (cong (őĽ z ‚Üí z +‚Ą§ IMQ.dotŌÉ ŌÉ (xs ++ zeros {n = k}) (zeros {n = m} ++ t))
            (trans
              (cong (őĽ t ‚Üí IMQ.sign‚Ą§ s * t) (IntP.*-zero ≥ (IMQ.to‚Ą§Trit x)))
              (IntP.*-zero ≥ (IMQ.sign‚Ą§ s))))
      (cong (őĽ z ‚Üí 0‚Ą§ +‚Ą§ z) (dotŌÉ-core‚ä•tail {m} {k} ŌÉ xs t)))

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Therefore B2ŌÉ is also 0 on core/tail blocks

B2ŌÉ-core‚ä•tail :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  IMQ.B2ŌÉ ŌÉ (embedCore {m} {k} c) (embedTail {m} {k} t) ‚Č° 0‚Ą§
B2ŌÉ-core‚ä•tail {m} {k} ŌÉ c t =
  trans (IMQ.B2ŌÉ‚Č°2dotŌÉ ŌÉ (embedCore {m} {k} c) (embedTail {m} {k} t))
        (cong (őĽ z ‚Üí (+ 2) * z) (dotŌÉ-core‚ä•tail ŌÉ c t))
module DASHI.Physics.WitnessSetPolicy where

open import Level using (Level; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚Č§_)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)

_‚Č•_ : Nat ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Set
m ‚Č• n = n ‚Č§ m

-- Policy for admissible witness sets used in closure claims.
record WitnessSetPolicy {‚Ąď} (W : Set ‚Ąď) : Set (suc ‚Ąď) where
  field
    minForward : Nat
    minBackward : Nat
    forwardCount : W ‚Üí Nat
    backwardCount : W ‚Üí Nat
    quotaPreserving : W ‚Üí Set

  admissible : W ‚Üí Set
  admissible w =
    (forwardCount w ‚Č• minForward) √ó
    (backwardCount w ‚Č• minBackward) √ó
    quotaPreserving w

open WitnessSetPolicy public

module DASHI.Physics.MaskedQuadraticRenormalization where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; sym; trans)

open import Data.Vec using (Vec; _++_; zipWith)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_; proj‚āĀ; proj‚āā)
open import Data.Integer using (‚Ą§; _*_) renaming (_+_ to _+‚Ą§_)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit)
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
open import DASHI.Physics.MaskedSplitQuadratic as MSQ

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Basic split lemmas for coarse/tail under concatenation

coarseOf-++ :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  TCP.coarseOf m k (c ++ t) ‚Č° c
coarseOf-++ m k c t
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c t
  = refl

tailOf-++ :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  TCP.tailOf m k (c ++ t) ‚Č° t
tailOf-++ m k c t
  rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c t
  = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Coarse/tail behavior under renormalization RŠĶ£

coarseOf-RŠĶ£ :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.coarseOf m k (TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° TCP.coarseOf m k x
coarseOf-RŠĶ£ m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        | TCP.RŠĶ£-++ m k c t
        | coarseOf-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t)
  = refl

tailOf-RŠĶ£ :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° TCP.shiftTail (TCP.tailOf m k x)
tailOf-RŠĶ£ m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        | TCP.RŠĶ£-++ m k c t
        | tailOf-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t)
  = refl

RŠĶ£-decomp :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} x ‚Č° TCP.coarseOf m k x ++ TCP.shiftTail (TCP.tailOf m k x)
RŠĶ£-decomp m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        | TCP.RŠĶ£-++ m k c t
        | coarseOf-++ m k c t
        | tailOf-++ m k c t
  = refl

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic under renormalization:
-- QŌÉ(RŠĶ£ x) splits into coarse + shifted tail.

QŌÉ-split-++ :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat)
    (ŌÉc : Vec IMQ.Sign m) (ŌÉt : Vec IMQ.Sign k)
    (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  IMQ.QŌÉ (ŌÉc ++ ŌÉt) (c ++ t)
    ‚Č° IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉc c +‚Ą§ IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉt t
QŌÉ-split-++ m k ŌÉc ŌÉt c t =
  let
    f = (őĽ s xi ‚Üí IMQ.sign‚Ą§ s * IMQ.sq‚Ą§ (IMQ.to‚Ą§Trit xi))
  in
  trans
    refl
    (trans
      (cong IMQ.sum‚Ą§ (MSQ.zipWith-++ f ŌÉc ŌÉt c t))
      (trans
        (MSQ.sum‚Ą§-++ (zipWith f ŌÉc c) (zipWith f ŌÉt t))
        refl))

QŌÉ-split-coarse :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat)
    (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (c : Vec Trit m) (t : Vec Trit k) ‚Üí
  IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ (c ++ t)
    ‚Č° IMQ.QŌÉ (TCP.coarseOf m k ŌÉ) c
    +‚Ą§ IMQ.QŌÉ (TCP.tailOf m k ŌÉ) t
QŌÉ-split-coarse m k ŌÉ c t
  =
  trans
    (cong (őĽ z ‚Üí IMQ.QŌÉ z (c ++ t)) (sym (TCP.merge-split {A = IMQ.Sign} m k ŌÉ)))
    (QŌÉ-split-++ m k (TCP.coarseOf m k ŌÉ) (TCP.tailOf m k ŌÉ) c t)

QŌÉ-R :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat)
    (ŌÉ : Vec IMQ.Sign (m + k))
    (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ (TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} x)
    ‚Č° IMQ.QŌÉ (TCP.coarseOf m k ŌÉ) (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    +‚Ą§ IMQ.QŌÉ (TCP.tailOf   m k ŌÉ) (TCP.shiftTail (TCP.tailOf m k x))
QŌÉ-R m k ŌÉ x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t)
  rewrite sym (TCP.merge-split m k x)
        | TCP.RŠĶ£-++ m k c t
  = QŌÉ-split-coarse m k ŌÉ c (TCP.shiftTail t)
module DASHI.Physics.MaskedClosureKit where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; _+_)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec)
open import Data.Integer using (‚Ą§)

open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP
open import DASHI.Physics.RealClosureKitFiber as RKF
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
open import DASHI.Physics.SignatureFromMask as SFM
open import DASHI.Physics.DimensionBoundAssumptions as DBA

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Masked quadratic invariants wired onto a RealClosureKitFiber instance.
--
-- This does not change the underlying closure kit; it augments it with:
--   - a mask on the core,
--   - the masked quadratic QŌÉ and bilinear B‚āāŌÉ pulled back to the full state,
--   - a signature extracted from the mask,
--   - an orbit-profile seam (dimension bound target).

record RealClosureKitFiberMask : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    m k : Nat
    base : RKF.RealClosureKitFiber

    -- Mask on the core (length m).
    mask : Vec IMQ.Sign m

    -- Core-only invariants, lifted to the full state via coarseOf.
    coreQŌÉ : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí ‚Ą§
    coreB2ŌÉ : RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí RTC.Carrier (m + k) ‚Üí ‚Ą§

    -- Signature extracted from the mask.
    sig : Nat √ó Nat

    -- Orbit-profile seam (dimension-bound target).
    orbitProfile : DBA.ShellOrbitProfile m

open RealClosureKitFiberMask public

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Constructor: derive all fields from base + mask.

mkMaskKit :
  ‚ąÄ {m k : Nat} ‚Üí
  RKF.RealClosureKitFiber ‚Üí
  Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí
  DBA.ShellOrbitProfile m ‚Üí
  RealClosureKitFiberMask
mkMaskKit {m} {k} base mask orbitProfile =
  record
    { m = m
    ; k = k
    ; base = base
    ; mask = mask
    ; coreQŌÉ = őĽ x ‚Üí IMQ.QŌÉ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k x)
    ; coreB2ŌÉ = őĽ x y ‚Üí IMQ.B2ŌÉ mask (TCP.coarseOf m k x) (TCP.coarseOf m k y)
    ; sig = SFM.signature mask
    ; orbitProfile = orbitProfile
    }
module DASHI.Physics.OrbitProfileComputed where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool using (Bool; true; false; if_then_else_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_; refl; cong)
open import Relation.Nullary using (Dec; yes; no)

open import Data.List using (List; []; _‚ą∑_; map; filter; length)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚Č§_)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (_‚Č§?_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_)
open import Data.Integer using (‚Ą§; +_; -[1+_]; _‚Čü_)

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)
open import DASHI.Physics.RealTernaryCarrier as RTC
open import DASHI.Physics.IndefiniteMaskQuadratic as IMQ
open import DASHI.Physics.OrbitShellPredicate as OSP
open import DASHI.Physics.DimensionBoundAssumptions as DBA

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Basic list utilities (kept local to avoid extra imports)

concat : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí List (List A) ‚Üí List A
concat [] = []
concat (xs ‚ą∑ xss) = xs ++ concat xss
  where
    _++_ : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A
    [] ++ ys = ys
    (x ‚ą∑ xs) ++ ys = x ‚ą∑ (xs ++ ys)

concatMap : ‚ąÄ {A B : Set} ‚Üí (A ‚Üí List B) ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List B
concatMap f xs = concat (map f xs)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Decidable equality for Trit and Vec

decEqTrit : (x y : Trit) ‚Üí Dec (x ‚Č° y)
decEqTrit neg neg = yes refl
decEqTrit neg zer = no (őĽ ())
decEqTrit neg pos = no (őĽ ())
decEqTrit zer neg = no (őĽ ())
decEqTrit zer zer = yes refl
decEqTrit zer pos = no (őĽ ())
decEqTrit pos neg = no (őĽ ())
decEqTrit pos zer = no (őĽ ())
decEqTrit pos pos = yes refl

decEqVec : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí (x y : Vec Trit n) ‚Üí Dec (x ‚Č° y)
decEqVec [] [] = yes refl
decEqVec (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys) with decEqTrit x y
... | no neq = no (őĽ eq ‚Üí neq (cong head eq))
... | yes refl with decEqVec xs ys
... | no neq = no (őĽ eq ‚Üí neq (cong tail eq))
... | yes refl = yes refl
  where
    head : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit (suc n) ‚Üí Trit
    head (t ‚ą∑ _) = t
    tail : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit (suc n) ‚Üí Vec Trit n
    tail (_ ‚ą∑ ts) = ts

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Membership / nub

member : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí (A ‚Üí A ‚Üí Dec (A ‚Č° A)) ‚Üí A ‚Üí List A ‚Üí Bool
member dec x [] = false
member dec x (y ‚ą∑ ys) with dec x y
... | yes _ = true
... | no _  = member dec x ys

nub : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí (A ‚Üí A ‚Üí Dec (A ‚Č° A)) ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A
nub dec [] = []
nub dec (x ‚ą∑ xs) with member dec x xs
... | true  = nub dec xs
... | false = x ‚ą∑ nub dec xs

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Enumerate all Vec Trit n

allTrit : List Trit
allTrit = neg ‚ą∑ zer ‚ą∑ pos ‚ą∑ []

allVecTrit : ‚ąÄ (n : Nat) ‚Üí List (Vec Trit n)
allVecTrit zero = [] ‚ą∑ []
allVecTrit (suc n) =
  concatMap
    (őĽ t ‚Üí map (őĽ v ‚Üí t ‚ą∑ v) (allVecTrit n))
    allTrit

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Shell1 list from a mask

isShell1 : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Bool
isShell1 ŌÉ x with IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ x ‚Čü (+ 1)
... | yes _ = true
... | no _ with IMQ.QŌÉ ŌÉ x ‚Čü -[1+ 0]
... | yes _ = true
... | no _  = false

shell1List : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí List (Vec Trit m)
shell1List {m} ŌÉ = filter (isShell1 ŌÉ) (allVecTrit m)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Orbit sizes under a finite action list

orbitSizes :
  ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí
  (dec : A ‚Üí A ‚Üí Dec (A ‚Č° A)) ‚Üí
  (gs : List A) ‚Üí
  (act : A ‚Üí A ‚Üí A) ‚Üí
  List A ‚Üí
  List Nat
orbitSizes dec gs act [] = []
orbitSizes dec gs act (x ‚ą∑ xs) =
  let
    orb = nub dec (map (őĽ g ‚Üí act g x) gs)
    rest = filter (őĽ z ‚Üí not (member dec z orb)) xs
  in
  length orb ‚ą∑ orbitSizes dec gs act rest
  where
    not : Bool ‚Üí Bool
    not true = false
    not false = true

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Simple descending sort for Nat lists

insertDesc : Nat ‚Üí List Nat ‚Üí List Nat
insertDesc x [] = x ‚ą∑ []
insertDesc x (y ‚ą∑ ys) with x NatP.‚Č§? y
... | yes _ = y ‚ą∑ insertDesc x ys
... | no _  = x ‚ą∑ y ‚ą∑ ys

sortDesc : List Nat ‚Üí List Nat
sortDesc [] = []
sortDesc (x ‚ą∑ xs) = insertDesc x (sortDesc xs)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Concrete Bool action: invVec toggle

actBool : ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí Bool ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec Trit m
actBool true  x = RTC.invVec x
actBool false x = x

bools : List Bool
bools = false ‚ą∑ true ‚ą∑ []

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Computed profile for the Bool action on Shell1

orbitProfileBool :
  ‚ąÄ {m : Nat} ‚Üí
  Vec IMQ.Sign m ‚Üí
  DBA.ShellOrbitProfile m
orbitProfileBool ŌÉ =
  let
    shell = shell1List ŌÉ
    sizes = orbitSizes decEqVec bools actBool shell
    sizesSorted = sortDesc sizes
  in
  SOPG.profileFromSorted {m = _} sizesSorted
module DASHI.Physics.SnapSignature where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Data.Nat using (_‚Č§_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; []; _‚ą∑_)
open import Data.Empty using (‚ä•)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_)
open import Data.Sum using (_‚äé_)

¬¨_ : Set ‚Üí Set
¬¨ P = P ‚Üí ‚ä•

open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; neg; zer; pos)

-- Count coordinates that snap from nonzero to zero in a single step.
countZeroSnaps : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Nat
countZeroSnaps [] [] = zero
countZeroSnaps (x ‚ą∑ xs) (y ‚ą∑ ys) =
  snap x y + countZeroSnaps xs ys
  where
    snap : Trit ‚Üí Trit ‚Üí Nat
    snap neg zer = suc zero
    snap pos zer = suc zero
    snap _   _   = zero

-- Predicate: at least k zero-snaps.
SnapAtLeast : ‚ąÄ {n : Nat} ‚Üí Nat ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Vec Trit n ‚Üí Set
SnapAtLeast k x y = k ‚Č§ countZeroSnaps x y

-- Abstract diagnostic bundle for a step x -> y.
record SnapSignature {S : Set} : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    -- concrete state
    step : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set

    -- trigger 1: multi-coordinate zeroing (sheet elimination)
    snapZero : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set

    -- trigger 2: chi2 spike (boundary blow-up)
    chi2Spike : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set

    -- trigger 3: MDL proxy descent (valid IR movement)
    mdlDescent : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set

-- Canonical combined predicate for a snap event.
record IsSnap {S : Set} (Sig : SnapSignature {S}) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    snap : ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí
      SnapSignature.step Sig x y ‚Üí
      SnapSignature.snapZero Sig x y ‚Üí
      SnapSignature.chi2Spike Sig x y ‚Üí
      SnapSignature.mdlDescent Sig x y ‚Üí
      Set

-- Cone monotonicity except snaps: if not a snap, interior is preserved.
record ConeMonotoneExceptSnaps {S : Set} : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    InInterior : S ‚Üí Set
    Boundary   : S ‚Üí Set
    T          : S ‚Üí S
    Sig        : SnapSignature {S}

    monotoneExceptSnap : ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí
      InInterior x ‚Üí
      (¬¨ (SnapSignature.step Sig x (T x) √ó
          SnapSignature.snapZero Sig x (T x) √ó
          SnapSignature.chi2Spike Sig x (T x) √ó
          SnapSignature.mdlDescent Sig x (T x))) ‚Üí
      InInterior (T x) ‚äé Boundary (T x)
module DASHI.Physics.ArrowSeparatedDeltaConeSplit where

open import DASHI.Physics.Cone.ArrowSeparatedDeltaConeSplit public
module DASHI.Physics.ContractionQuadraticBridge where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_)
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction as Contr using (StrictContraction)

-- Abstract quadratic output forced by contraction.
record QuadraticOutput : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    V : Set
    Scalar : Set
    B : V ‚Üí V ‚Üí Scalar
    Q : V ‚Üí Scalar
    Q-def : ‚ąÄ v ‚Üí Q v ‚Č° B v v
    Lyapunov : Set
    UniqueUpToScale : Set

open QuadraticOutput public

-- Bridge: strict contraction implies a quadratic output.
record Contraction‚áíQuadratic
  {S : Set}
  (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
  (T : S ‚Üí S)
  : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    sc : StrictContraction U T
    out : QuadraticOutput

module DASHI.Physics.LiftToFullState where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans)
open import Data.Product using (_√ó_; _,_)
open import Data.Vec using (Vec; _++_; replicate)
open import DASHI.Algebra.Trit using (Trit; zer)

open import DASHI.Physics.TailCollapseProof as TCP

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Invariant coarse subspace

embedCoarse : ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) ‚Üí Vec Trit m ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k)
embedCoarse m k c = c ++ replicate k zer

coarseProj : ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) ‚Üí Vec Trit (m + k) ‚Üí Vec Trit m
coarseProj m k x = TCP.coarseOf m k x

coarse-invariant-R :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  coarseProj m k (TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° coarseProj m k x
coarse-invariant-R m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t) rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail t) = refl

coarse-invariant-P :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  coarseProj m k (TCP.PŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° coarseProj m k x
coarse-invariant-P m k x with TCP.split m k x
... | (c , t) rewrite TCP.split-++ m k c (TCP.projTail t) = refl

coarse-invariant-T :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  coarseProj m k (TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x) ‚Č° coarseProj m k x
coarse-invariant-T m k x =
  trans (coarse-invariant-P m k (TCP.RŠĶ£ {m} {k} x))
        (coarse-invariant-R m k x)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Finite-time collapse + invariant geometry, packaged

coarse-invariant-iter :
  ‚ąÄ (m k n : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  coarseProj m k (TCP.iterate n (TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k}) x) ‚Č° coarseProj m k x
coarse-invariant-iter m k zero x = refl
coarse-invariant-iter m k (suc n) x =
  trans
    (coarse-invariant-iter m k n (TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} x))
    (coarse-invariant-T m k x)

finiteTimeCollapse-to-geometry :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (x : Vec Trit (m + k)) ‚Üí
  ( coarseProj m k (TCP.iterate k (TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k}) x) ‚Č° coarseProj m k x )
  √ó
  ( TCP.tailOf m k (TCP.iterate k (TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k}) x) ‚Č° replicate k zer )
finiteTimeCollapse-to-geometry m k x =
  ( coarse-invariant-iter m k k x
  , TCP.tailOf-after-Tk m k x
  )

invariantCoarseSubspace :
  ‚ąÄ (m k : Nat) (c : Vec Trit m) ‚Üí
  TCP.TŠĶ£ {m} {k} (embedCoarse m k c) ‚Č° embedCoarse m k c
invariantCoarseSubspace m k c
  rewrite TCP.RŠĶ£-++ m k c (replicate k zer)
        | TCP.PŠĶ£-++ m k c (TCP.shiftTail (replicate k zer))
        | TCP.shiftTail-replicate {k}
        | TCP.projTail-replicate {k}
  = refl

module MaassRestoration where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Abstract broken states / restored states.
postulate
  Broken  : Set
  Stable  : Set

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A "restoration" map (Tikkun): Broken ‚Üí Stable

record Restoration : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    restore : Broken ‚Üí Stable

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Stability contracts you can actually test:
-- idempotence (restoring twice has no further effect) and coherence
-- with a projection/normal form.

record NormalForm : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    nf : Stable ‚Üí Stable
    nf-idem : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí nf (nf s) ‚Č° nf s

record RestorationLaw : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    R  : Restoration
    NF : NormalForm
    restores-to-nf : ‚ąÄ b ‚Üí NormalForm.nf NF (Restoration.restore R b) ‚Č° Restoration.restore R b

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Action functional

record Action {X : Set} : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    A : State X ‚Üí Nat

open Action public

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Monotonicity property

record Monotone {X : Set}
                (K : State X ‚Üí State X)
                (A : State X ‚Üí Nat)
                : Set where

  field
    monotone :
      ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí A (K s) ‚Č§ A s
module FixedPoint where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Ultrametric as UMetric
open import Contraction

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Fixed point definition

Fixed : {S : Set} ‚Üí (S ‚Üí S) ‚Üí S ‚Üí Set
Fixed K x = K x ‚Č° x

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Uniqueness of fixed point under contraction

record UniqueFixed
       {S : Set}
       (U : UMetric.Ultrametric S)
       (K : S ‚Üí S)
       (C : Contractive U K)
       : Set where

  open UMetric.Ultrametric U
  open Contractive C

  field
    unique :
      ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí
      Fixed K x ‚Üí
      Fixed K y ‚Üí
      x ‚Č° y
module Verification.Prelude where

open import Data.Nat public
  renaming (‚Ąē to Nat)
open import Data.Bool public using (Bool; true; false)
open import Data.List public using (List; []; _‚ą∑_)
open import Data.Product public using (ő£; _,_; _√ó_; proj‚āĀ; proj‚āā)
open import Data.Empty public using (‚ä•; ‚ä•-elim)
open import Data.Unit public using (‚ä§; tt)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality public using (_‚Č°_; refl; cong; sym; trans)

¬¨_ : Set ‚Üí Set
¬¨ A = A ‚Üí ‚ä•

fst : {A : Set} {B : A ‚Üí Set} ‚Üí ő£ A B ‚Üí A
fst = proj‚āĀ

snd : {A : Set} {B : A ‚Üí Set} (p : ő£ A B) ‚Üí B (proj‚āĀ p)
snd = proj‚āā
module Verification.ZK where

open import Verification.Prelude

postulate Public  : Set
postulate Private : Set
postulate Output  : Set

-- The spec function (what correctness means)
postulate spec : Public -> Private -> Output

-- An implementation whose correctness you want to prove (could be a circuit)
postulate impl : Public -> Private -> Output

-- A proof object (SNARK) and a verifier predicate
postulate Proof : Set
postulate verify : Public -> Output -> Proof -> Bool

-- Soundness contract (non-ZK): if verifier accepts, output equals spec
-- (This is where you plug the cryptographic theorem/certificate.)
postulate
  zkSoundness :
    (pub : Public) -> (priv : Private) -> (out : Output) -> (pi : Proof) ->
    verify pub out pi ‚Č° true ->
    out ‚Č° spec pub priv

-- ZK verification artifact: provide pub/out/proof and a verification boolean proof.
record ZKCorrectness : Set1 where
  field
    pub  : Public
    priv : Private
    out  : Output
    pi   : Proof
    accepts : verify pub out pi ‚Č° true
    correct : out ‚Č° spec pub priv
module Verification.ExecutionReview where

open import Verification.Prelude

-- A tiny abstract control-flow model.
postulate Program : Set
postulate Path    : Set

-- Static analyzer produces a set/list of feasible paths
postulate enumeratePaths : Program ‚Üí List Path

-- A property you claim holds on all paths.
postulate SafeOnPath : Program ‚Üí Path ‚Üí Set

-- ‚ÄúExecution review‚ÄĚ = proof that for every enumerated path, Safe holds.
All : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí (A ‚Üí Set) ‚Üí List A ‚Üí Set
All P []       = ‚ä§
All P (x ‚ą∑ xs) = P x √ó All P xs

record ExecutionReview : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    P   : Program
    ok  : All (SafeOnPath P) (enumeratePaths P)
module Verification.SourceHash where

open import Verification.Prelude

-- Abstract bytes; you can refine to Word8 later.
postulate Byte : Set
Bytes = List Byte

-- Cryptographic hash as a function (model-level).
postulate Hash : Set
postulate hash : Bytes ‚Üí Hash

-- A repo snapshot is modeled as its bytes (tarball) + declared hash.
record Snapshot : Set where
  constructor snap
  field
    blob     : Bytes
    declared : Hash

-- Integrity proof obligation: declared equals computed.
record SourceIntegrity : Set where
  field
    S : Snapshot
    ok : Snapshot.declared S ‚Č° hash (Snapshot.blob S)
module Verification.BinaryPatching where

open import Verification.Prelude

postulate Binary : Set
postulate Input  : Set
postulate Output : Set

-- Semantics of a binary as a function (idealization).
postulate run : Binary ‚Üí Input ‚Üí Output

-- Vulnerability predicate (e.g., triggers UAF, OOB, etc.)
postulate Vuln : Binary ‚Üí Set

-- Patch procedure
postulate patch : Binary ‚Üí Binary

postulate SafeInput : Input ‚Üí Set

-- Correctness obligations
record PatchCorrect : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    B : Binary
    -- vulnerability removed
    fixed : ¬¨ Vuln (patch B)
    -- behavior preserved on some agreed safe domain
    preserved : ‚ąÄ i ‚Üí SafeInput i ‚Üí run (patch B) i ‚Č° run B i

module Ultrametric where

open import Data.Nat using (‚Ąē; _‚Č§_; _<_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat
open import Agda.Builtin.Sigma
open import Data.Nat using (‚Ąē; _‚äĒ_)
max : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē
max = _‚äĒ_


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Distance function into ‚Ąē (discrete ultrametric)

record Ultrametric (S : Set) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    d : S ‚Üí S ‚Üí Nat

    -- Identity
    id-zero :
      ‚ąÄ x ‚Üí d x x ‚Č° 0

    -- Symmetry
    symmetric :
      ‚ąÄ x y ‚Üí d x y ‚Č° d y x

    -- Strong triangle inequality (ultrametric)
    ultratriangle :
      ‚ąÄ x y z ‚Üí
      d x z ‚Č§ max (d x y) (d y z)

module CRTPeriod where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; _+_; _*_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (cong; trans; sym)

open import Data.Nat.Base   using (NonZero; nonZero)
open import Data.Nat.DivMod using (_%_; [m+kn]%n‚Č°m%n)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using (*-assoc; *-comm; +-assoc)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Repo-defined digit function:

d : Nat ‚Üí Nat
d N = ((N % 71) + (N % 59) + (N % 47)) % 10

period : Nat
period = 71 * 59 * 47  -- 196883

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- The theorem statement (R1):
-- d(N + k*period) = d(N) for all k.
--
-- Proof is standard modular arithmetic:
-- (N + k*period) mod p = N mod p for p ‚ąą {71,59,47}
-- then propagate through sum and mod 10.
--
-- You can discharge this using stdlib DivMod lemmas, or (DASHI-style)
-- by importing a small proof certificate.

instance
  nonZero71 : NonZero 71
  nonZero71 = nonZero
  nonZero59 : NonZero 59
  nonZero59 = nonZero
  nonZero47 : NonZero 47
  nonZero47 = nonZero
  nonZero10 : NonZero 10
  nonZero10 = nonZero

period-thm : ‚ąÄ N k ‚Üí d (N + k * period) ‚Č° d N
period-thm N k =
  period-thm' step71 step59 step47
  where
    k71 = k * (59 * 47)
    k59 = k * (71 * 47)
    k47 = k * (71 * 59)

    period‚Č°59¬∑47¬∑71 : period ‚Č° (59 * 47) * 71
    period‚Č°59¬∑47¬∑71 =
      trans (NatP.*-assoc 71 59 47)
        (NatP.*-comm 71 (59 * 47))

    period‚Č°71¬∑47¬∑59 : period ‚Č° (71 * 47) * 59
    period‚Č°71¬∑47¬∑59 =
      trans (NatP.*-assoc 71 59 47)
        (trans (cong (őĽ x ‚Üí 71 * x) (NatP.*-comm 59 47))
          (sym (NatP.*-assoc 71 47 59)))

    period‚Č°71¬∑59¬∑47 : period ‚Č° (71 * 59) * 47
    period‚Č°71¬∑59¬∑47 = NatP.*-assoc 71 59 47

    eq71 : k * period ‚Č° k71 * 71
    eq71 = trans (cong (őĽ x ‚Üí k * x) period‚Č°59¬∑47¬∑71) (sym (NatP.*-assoc k (59 * 47) 71))

    eq59 : k * period ‚Č° k59 * 59
    eq59 = trans (cong (őĽ x ‚Üí k * x) period‚Č°71¬∑47¬∑59) (sym (NatP.*-assoc k (71 * 47) 59))

    eq47 : k * period ‚Č° k47 * 47
    eq47 = trans (cong (őĽ x ‚Üí k * x) period‚Č°71¬∑59¬∑47) (sym (NatP.*-assoc k (71 * 59) 47))

    step71 : (N + k * period) % 71 ‚Č° N % 71
    step71 = trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí (N + v) % 71) eq71) ([m+kn]%n‚Č°m%n N k71 71)

    step59 : (N + k * period) % 59 ‚Č° N % 59
    step59 = trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí (N + v) % 59) eq59) ([m+kn]%n‚Č°m%n N k59 59)

    step47 : (N + k * period) % 47 ‚Č° N % 47
    step47 = trans (cong (őĽ v ‚Üí (N + v) % 47) eq47) ([m+kn]%n‚Č°m%n N k47 47)

    period-thm' :
      (s71 : (N + k * period) % 71 ‚Č° N % 71) ‚Üí
      (s59 : (N + k * period) % 59 ‚Č° N % 59) ‚Üí
      (s47 : (N + k * period) % 47 ‚Č° N % 47) ‚Üí
      d (N + k * period) ‚Č° d N
    period-thm' s71 s59 s47 rewrite s71 | s59 | s47 = refl
module Z6_RegularInverse where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat using (Nat)
open import Data.Fin using (Fin; zero; suc; to‚Ąē)
open import Data.Product.Base using (ő£; _,_)
open import Data.Nat.Properties as NatP using ()
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality as Eq using (cong)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Z6 elements as Fin 6
Z6 : Set
Z6 = Fin 6

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Ring operations modulo 6 (postulate or implement via Fin arithmetic).
-- If you want full concreteness, implement add/mul with to‚Ąē and mod 6.
postulate
  _+6_ : Z6 ‚Üí Z6 ‚Üí Z6
  _*6_ : Z6 ‚Üí Z6 ‚Üí Z6

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- von Neumann regular inverse witness: a = a*b*a

Regular : Z6 ‚Üí Set
Regular a = ő£ Z6 (őĽ b ‚Üí a ‚Č° (a *6 b) *6 a)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A concrete witness table (finite, so we can just provide b per a).
-- You can later refine _+6_/_*6_ and this becomes fully checkable.

postulate
  bOf : Z6 ‚Üí Z6
  regular-law : ‚ąÄ a ‚Üí a ‚Č° (a *6 bOf a) *6 a

regular : ‚ąÄ a ‚Üí Regular a
regular a = bOf a , regular-law a
module FascisticSystem where

open import Data.Product using (ő£; _,_)
open import Data.Sum using (_‚äé_; inj‚āĀ; inj‚āā)
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_)

open import Data.Nat as Nat
open import Data.Bool using (Bool; true; false)



-- Abstract finite state space

postulate
  S : Set
  finiteS : ‚Ąē          -- cardinality (not constructively used)

-- Entropy function (measure into ‚Ąē for simplicity)

postulate
  H : S ‚Üí ‚Ąē

-- Projection operator (idempotent, non-invertible)

record Projection : Set where
  field
    K        : S ‚Üí S
    idemp    : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí K (K s) ‚Č° K s
    contract : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí H (K s) ‚Č§ H s

-- System = list of projections applied in fixed order

postulate
  Ktotal : S ‚Üí S

-- Global contraction property

postulate
  monotone : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí H (Ktotal s) ‚Č§ H s

-- Strict decrease when not in fixed set

postulate
  strict-decrease :
    ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí H (Ktotal s) < H s ‚äé (Ktotal s ‚Č° s)

-- Define attractor

Attractor : Set
Attractor = ő£ S (őĽ s ‚Üí Ktotal s ‚Č° s)

-- Iteration

iterate : ‚Ąē ‚Üí S ‚Üí S
iterate zero    s = s
iterate (suc n) s = Ktotal (iterate n s)
module PrimeRoles where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat)
open import Data.Nat.Base         using (_<_ )
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import MonsterOntos

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Roles (you can refine these into a lattice later)

data Role : Set where
  Types       : Role
  Operators   : Role
  Functions   : Role
  Consensus   : Role
  Completion  : Role
  Domain      : Nat ‚Üí Role   -- generic ‚Äúdomain lane‚ÄĚ if you want more structure

roleOf : SSP ‚Üí Role
roleOf p2  = Types
roleOf p3  = Operators
roleOf p11 = Functions
roleOf p23 = Consensus
roleOf p71 = Completion
-- the rest: either assign Domain lanes or make a richer record
roleOf p5  = Domain 5
roleOf p7  = Domain 7
roleOf p13 = Domain 13
roleOf p17 = Domain 17
roleOf p19 = Domain 19
roleOf p29 = Domain 29
roleOf p31 = Domain 31
roleOf p41 = Domain 41
roleOf p47 = Domain 47
roleOf p59 = Domain 59

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- ‚ÄúAxiom of completion‚ÄĚ as a termination measure contract:
-- Completion prime provides a stop condition for any recursive refinement loop.

record CompletionLaw (S : Set) : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    measure : S ‚Üí Nat
    step    : S ‚Üí S
    -- If step decreases measure, recursion terminates.
    decreases : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí measure (step s) < measure s
module ThreeAdic_Attractor where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Data.Rational using (‚Ąö; _+_; _-_; _*_; _/_; normalize)
open import Data.Rational.Properties as ‚ĄöP
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality as Eq using (trans; sym; cong)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Define x by the equation 3x = x - 1, and solve in ‚Ąö.
-- This is the algebraic ‚Äúdigit-shift‚ÄĚ property you care about.

postulate
  x : ‚Ąö

-- Helpers (stdlib has numerals; we keep explicit)
postulate
  1‚Ąö : ‚Ąö
  2‚Ąö : ‚Ąö
  3‚Ąö : ‚Ąö
  minusHalfQ : ‚Ąö

postulate
  shift : (3‚Ąö * x) ‚Č° (x - 1‚Ąö)
  qed : x ‚Č° minusHalfQ

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Theorem: if 3x = x - 1 then x = -1/2

solve : shift ‚Č° shift ‚Üí x ‚Č° minusHalfQ
solve _ =
  -- You can fill this using ‚Ąö ring reasoning:
  -- 3x = x - 1  ‚áí  2x = -1  ‚áí x = -1/2
  -- In Agda, easiest is to use ‚ĄöP.*-cancel ≥ / group properties.
  qed
module MonsterState where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_; _*_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.Equality using (_‚Č°_; refl)
open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List; []; _‚ą∑_)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Factor mask (15 prime-power factors of |M|).
-- true  = keep
-- false = remove

FactorCount : Nat
FactorCount = 15

Mask : Set
Mask = List Bool

replicate : Nat ‚Üí Bool ‚Üí Mask
replicate zero    b = []
replicate (suc n) b = b ‚ą∑ replicate n b

fullMask : Mask
fullMask = replicate FactorCount true

emptyMask : Mask
emptyMask = replicate FactorCount false

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Walk state.
-- You can extend this with ‚Äúwindow position‚ÄĚ, ‚Äútarget digits‚ÄĚ, etc.
-- For DASHI: kernel is about how masks evolve; lens decides admissibility.

record State : Set where
  constructor st
  field
    mask   : Mask
    window : Nat   -- abstract ‚Äúdigit window id‚ÄĚ (moving window, index, etc.)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- A lens is the measurement predicate:
-- admissible s m = ‚Äúremoving to mask m preserves the digit window condition‚ÄĚ.

record Lens : Set‚āĀ where
  field
    admissible : State ‚Üí Mask ‚Üí Bool

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Candidate moves:
-- In the real system, this is ‚Äúremove subsets of prime-power factors‚ÄĚ.
-- Here we just take a finite list of candidate masks.

Candidates : Set
Candidates = List Mask
module LogicTlurey where

open import Agda.Builtin.Equality
open import Agda.Builtin.List
open import Agda.Builtin.Nat

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Local equality utilities (no stdlib needed)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

sym : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} {x y : A} ‚Üí x ‚Č° y ‚Üí y ‚Č° x
sym refl = refl

cong : ‚ąÄ {A B : Set} {x y : A} (f : A ‚Üí B) ‚Üí x ‚Č° y ‚Üí f x ‚Č° f y
cong f refl = refl

open import Base369

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Dialectical stages
------------------------------------------------------------------------

data Stage : Set where
  seed      : Stage
  counter   : Stage
  resonance : Stage
  overflow  : Stage

next : Stage ‚Üí Stage
next seed      = counter
next counter   = resonance
next resonance = overflow
next overflow  = seed

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Tlurey traces
------------------------------------------------------------------------

StageTrace : Nat ‚Üí Stage ‚Üí List Stage
StageTrace zero    _ = []
StageTrace (suc n) s = s ‚ą∑ StageTrace n (next s)

length : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí List A ‚Üí Nat
length []       = zero
length (_ ‚ą∑ xs) = suc (length xs)

_++_ : ‚ąÄ {A : Set} ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A ‚Üí List A
[]       ++ ys = ys
(x ‚ą∑ xs) ++ ys = x ‚ą∑ (xs ++ ys)

StageTrace-length : ‚ąÄ n s ‚Üí length (StageTrace n s) ‚Č° n
StageTrace-length zero    _ = refl
StageTrace-length (suc n) s = cong suc (StageTrace-length n (next s))

next‚Āī : ‚ąÄ s ‚Üí spin 4 next s ‚Č° s
next‚Āī seed      = refl
next‚Āī counter   = refl
next‚Āī resonance = refl
next‚Āī overflow  = refl

spin-next-succ : ‚ąÄ n s ‚Üí spin n next (next s) ‚Č° spin (suc n) next s
spin-next-succ zero    _ = refl
spin-next-succ (suc n) s = cong next (spin-next-succ n s)

StageTrace-periodic : ‚ąÄ n s ‚Üí StageTrace (n + 4) s ‚Č° StageTrace n s ++ StageTrace 4 (spin n next s)
StageTrace-periodic zero    s = refl
StageTrace-periodic (suc n) s rewrite sym (spin-next-succ n s) =
  cong (s ‚ą∑_) (StageTrace-periodic n (next s))

StageTrace-cycle : ‚ąÄ n ‚Üí StageTrace (n + 4) seed ‚Č° StageTrace n seed ++ StageTrace 4 (spin n next seed)
StageTrace-cycle n = StageTrace-periodic n seed


------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Semantics via triadic values
------------------------------------------------------------------------

stageTone : Stage ‚Üí TriTruth
stageTone seed      = tri-low
stageTone counter   = tri-mid
stageTone resonance = tri-high
stageTone overflow  = tri-low

combineStage : Stage ‚Üí Stage ‚Üí TriTruth
combineStage a b = triXor (stageTone a) (stageTone b)

stageTone-next-seed : stageTone (next seed) ‚Č° rotateTri (stageTone seed)
stageTone-next-seed = refl

stageTone-next-counter : stageTone (next counter) ‚Č° rotateTri (stageTone counter)
stageTone-next-counter = refl

stageTone-next-resonance : stageTone (next resonance) ‚Č° rotateTri (stageTone resonance)
stageTone-next-resonance = refl

stageTone-next-overflow : stageTone (next overflow) ‚Č° stageTone seed
stageTone-next-overflow = refl

resonance-combine : combineStage resonance resonance ‚Č° tri-mid
resonance-combine = refl
module MonsterGroups where

open import Agda.Builtin.Nat      using (Nat; zero; suc; _+_)
open import Agda.Builtin.Bool     using (Bool; true; false)
open import Agda.Builtin.List     using (List; []; _‚ą∑_)

open import MonsterState

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Boundary predicate: ‚Äúthis state ends a group‚ÄĚ.
-- You define it from the walk semantics (or from the trace table markers).

Boundary : Set
Boundary = State ‚Üí Bool

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Count groups in a trace given a boundary predicate.
-- Convention: group count starts at 0 for empty trace, else 1 + boundaries hit.

countGroups : Boundary ‚Üí List State ‚Üí Nat
countGroups b [] = 0
countGroups b (s ‚ą∑ ss) = suc (go ss)
  where
    go : List State ‚Üí Nat
    go [] = 0
    go (t ‚ą∑ ts) with b t
    ... | true  = suc (go ts)
    ... | false = go ts

------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- You can similarly count ‚Äúpreserved digits‚ÄĚ if your trace stores that.
-- For now keep it abstract until you add a field.
-- Agda: 10-Fold Way Bridges
module TenfoldBridges where

open import Data.Nat using (‚Ąē)
open import Data.Nat.DivMod using (_%_)
open import Data.Bool
open import Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality using (_‚Č°_; refl; sym; _‚ČĘ_)

-- Topological class
topoClass : ‚Ąē ‚Üí ‚Ąē
topoClass n = n % 10

-- Bridge record
record Bridge : Set where
  field
    nodeA : ‚Ąē
    nodeB : ‚Ąē
    different : topoClass nodeA ‚ČĘ topoClass nodeB

-- Symmetry
bridge-sym : (b : Bridge) ‚Üí Bridge
bridge-sym record { nodeA = a ; nodeB = b ; different = d } =
  record { nodeA = b ; nodeB = a ; different = őĽ eq ‚Üí d (sym eq) }

-- Example: 232 ‚ÜĒ 323
bridge-232-323 : Bridge
bridge-232-323 = record
  { nodeA = 232
  ; nodeB = 323
  ; different = őĽ ()
  }

-- Theorem: Symmetry preserves bridges
bridge-symmetry : (b : Bridge) ‚Üí 
  Bridge.nodeA (bridge-sym b) ‚Č° Bridge.nodeB b
bridge-symmetry b = refl
